The event that defines this entire chronological window is Kamala Khan's death in *Amazing Spider-Man* #26 (June 2022) — an editorial set-piece that took place *outside* the *Ms. Marvel* book's own diegetic infrastructure, in a Spider-Man storyline, and that the subject therefore experienced as second-hand information about the person whose body he had spent eight years building gear to protect.

This is critical and must be stated plainly: the subject was not present. He did not see it. He learned of Kamala's death the way her parents did — through notification, through other people's faces, through the unbearable interval between a phone ringing and someone speaking the sentence.

His on-panel response was suppressed past the point of legibility. In *Fallen Friend: The Death of Ms. Marvel* (2023, the wake/memorial one-shot), the subject is present but is given strikingly little dialogue for a character of his structural importance to the deceased. He is drawn at the back of rooms. He helps. He carries chairs. He is shown once, mid-shot, with his good hand pressed flat against a wall and his head down — not weeping, not collapsed, just *stopped* — and then the panel moves on. This is the diagnostic image of the entire window. A person whose affect-containment training had been calibrated to the wartime tolerances of an adolescence spent absorbing his family's chaos discovered, in his early twenties, that the calibration held even against the unmetabolizable.

He did not break. He should have. The file note here is that *the absence of breakdown is not health.* The suppression machinery built across two decades performed exactly as engineered, and the cost — which he has not yet paid and may not pay for years — is being deferred into the somatic and relational future.

**Behavioral micro-pattern in the immediate post-death weeks (inferred from longitudinal extrapolation of his stress-response signature):** lab hours up, sleep down further, Vick contacted more frequently (the parentified instinct routing toward the only family-coded attachment still available), Mike not contacted (the prior displacement object would be unbearable here), Kareem contacted but kept at conversational arm's length. He would not have allowed anyone to provide care in a structured way. He would have shown up at the Khan household to fix things — literal household objects, a broken latch, a wiring issue — because that is the only mode in which his grief is permitted to express itself.

---

## 3. The resurrection and the mutant reveal (*Fallen Friend* coda → *Ms. Marvel: The New Mutant*, 2023)

Kamala's restoration via Krakoan resurrection protocols — and the accompanying reveal that she carried a latent mutant gene that her Inhuman activation had masked — restructured every relationship in her field, the subject's included, and did so along an axis he was uniquely poorly equipped to process.

The reveal hit him on three vectors at once:

**First**, the *epistemic* vector. The subject is the character whose stability rests on accurate models of the people he loves. He has spent eight years building bespoke gear for an Inhuman physiology, modeling polymorph stress tolerances, calibrating fail-safes against a specific power-set's failure modes. The discovery that the substrate was not what he had modeled — that the most thoroughly engineered relationship of his life had rested on a category error he could not have detected — is, for a person whose self-concept is load-bearing on technical competence, a quiet detonation. He will not say this is what it was. It is what it was.

**Second**, the *temporal* vector. He had already done the grieving. He had crossed the threshold of *learning to live without her*, the threshold an entire personality structure had been re-zoning toward for the better part of a year. The reversal of that grief is, in psychological terms, not a clean restoration. It is a *second* destabilization layered on top of the first, with the additional burden that one is not socially permitted to mourn a death that has been undone. He cannot be sad in public about a friend who is alive. The grief is now load-bearing in private only.

**Third**, the *relational* vector. Kamala returns embedded in a new social field — the X-Men, the Krakoan/post-Krakoan mutant infrastructure, a peer group of literal demigods and centuries-old telepaths — into which the subject does not project. He is again, as he was in the Wakanda interval, the human in the room of the more-than-human. But where Wakanda was *his* technical milieu and he was the visitor with credentials, the X-side is not his theater. He has no entry point. He is not a mutant. He is not Inhuman. He is, in the new configuration, *Kamala's friend from before* — a category that comes with a built-in past tense.

His response, observable across the *New Mutant* and adjacent material: he stays. He does not retreat the way he retreated in 2017. This is the single most important behavioral datum of the current window. He has *learned the cost of geographic flight* and is refusing it as a solution this time. He keeps showing up. He keeps being in the room. He has accepted a peripheral position in the new configuration rather than removing himself from it. Whether this represents genuine growth or a more sophisticated containment strategy is, frankly, undecidable from the present record — both readings are consistent with the evidence. The functional outcome is the same: he is present, he is steady, and he is no longer the first person she calls.

---

## 4. The Kareem question, current status

The relationship with Kareem (Red Dagger) — established in the late-Wilson Wakanda interval as the subject's first real adult-coded romantic attachment outside the Kamala-displacement field — has, across the recent window, settled into a structure that is best described as *durable and geographically distended*. They have not been depicted as broken up. They have also not been depicted in the kind of sustained shared-life proximity that would mark a primary partnership. The relationship occupies the same space in the subject's life that his Wakanda lab occupies in his professional life: real, intact, drawn upon, not the daily ground.

This is consistent with his trait structure. The subject's mature attachment style permits — perhaps *requires* — a partner whose own life is autonomously full, whose claims on his time are not constant, and whose presence does not pre-empt his structural role in the Khan-centered field. Kareem, who has his own theater of operations and his own commitments, fits this profile exactly. It is a sustainable arrangement, and it is also, observably, an arrangement that *protects against intimacy escalating to a level that would require him to choose*.

The current-state read on this attachment: stable, mature, partially defended, not the place where his deepest material is being processed. He is loved here, competently, by someone who does not demand he relocate his center of gravity. He has accepted this and has not pushed for more. Whether more is wanted and suppressed, or genuinely not wanted, is — again — undecidable from canon. Both are consistent with the longitudinal pattern.

---

## 5. Vick, the family system, and the parentification residue

Vick Carrelli, across the recent window, has stabilized — adult, employed, no longer the chaos engine of the early Wilson run. This is a quiet and underweighted development in the file. For the first time in the subject's life, the *original* parentification load is no longer active. His brother does not need him. His parents, still thinly drawn in canon, are not in acute crisis.

The psychological implication is significant. A parentified child whose ward grows up does not simply *relax*. The vigilance circuitry, having no remaining domestic object, redistributes. In the subject's case, the redistribution has been observable across two channels: an intensified investment in *infrastructure-providing* for Kamala and the broader peer group (engineering for the team, lab work for the cause), and — emerging more recently — a thin but consistent thread of *mentorship-coded* behavior with younger characters in Kamala's orbit. The parentification has been generalized into a vocation rather than retired.

He is, at the time of this observation, *no one's required caretaker in his family of origin* for the first time since middle school. He has not noticed. The behavior has not adjusted. The vigilance has simply found other surfaces to land on.

---

## 6. Somatic current state

**The hand.** Compression glove or low-profile brace, depending on artist. Function: stable at its post-2016 baseline; no documented further deterioration; no documented restoration. He has not pursued — at least not on-page — any of the available restorative interventions that would be plausibly within his canonical reach (Wakandan medical infrastructure, X-side biotech, Stark-adjacent prosthetics). This is a *choice*. The injury has been integrated into his identity to a degree where its removal would itself be destabilizing. He has built a working life around the hand he has. He does not want a different one.

**Sleep.** Chronically curtailed. The bags-under-eyes signature persists across artists. There is no indication that he has, at any point in the recent window, prioritized sleep restoration. The pattern is now lifelong.

**Substance use.** Still negligible. He may, in the post-21 window, consume alcohol socially; nothing in the record indicates a shift from his adolescent abstinence pattern toward anything approaching use-as-coping. Consistent with the trait structure.

**Cardiovascular / general fitness.** Ordinary; he is not athletic and does not present as having taken up any compensatory physical regimen. He is the friend who walks places, who carries things, who can be on his feet for a long shift, and who has no particular relationship to his own body beyond *it works, mostly*.

**Affect somatics.** The containment is total enough that an observer would describe him as *calm* rather than *suppressed*. The distinction matters only on the longitudinal scale, where the cost of the containment is legible. In any single panel he reads as a young man in possession of himself.

---

## 7. Where he is, now

Geographically: based primarily in Jersey City again, with sustained working ties to Wakanda and intermittent travel. He has not relocated permanently a second time. The Wakanda interval has been re-zoned in his life as *professional asset* rather than *escape route*, which is itself a form of mature integration of a defense that had once been more primitive.

Vocationally: working scientist, early-career, post-academic or late-academic depending on the interpolation. The Wakandan credential is now part of his standing CV; he operates as a peer to senior engineers rather than as a prodigy. He has technical authority that is recognized without his needing to assert it.

Relationally: Kamala — restored, transformed, embedded in a new field, contacted regularly but no longer the daily ground; Kareem — sustained, distended, real; Vick — adult sibling, no longer ward; Mike — historical, civil, not present; the Khan family — still a primary anchor, with Aamir and Muneeba in particular treating him as something close to extended kin; the broader peer group — respected, slightly apart, the one others go to.

Psychologically: stable on every metric available to a diagnostic instrument; carrying an unmourned death-and-resurrection, an unmourned hand, an unmourned recategorization of the most important relationship of his life, and an unmourned end-of-parentification — none of which has surfaced as symptom. The containment continues to hold.

He is, at present, the steady one. He has been the steady one since he was a child. The question this file has been asking for ten years remains the operative question, sharpened now by the additional load of the recent window: **what happens, eventually, to a person whose reliability has never been allowed to fail, and on whom the costs of that reliability have continued, year over year, to compound silently.**

He has not answered the question. He is not going to answer it voluntarily. The recommendation for ongoing observation is therefore identical to the recommendation that has stood since 2017: maintain coverage, watch for the first crack, do not mistake the absence of a crack for the absence of pressure.


## Medical History

# MEDICAL HISTORY — SUBJECT: BRUNO CARRELLI

**File section:** 02 / Medical
**Compiler note:** Subject is a non-powered human in a population baseline saturated with the superhuman. The medical file is therefore short on exotica and long on the *unglamorous* — the soft-tissue, sleep-debt, posture, and one catastrophic peripheral nerve injury that have shaped a body trained from middle school onward to absorb cost without complaint. What follows is reconstructed from longitudinal observation across the Wilson, Ahmed, and Saladin runs, cross-referenced with depicted somatic detail by Alphona, Miyazawa, Leon, and successor artists.

---

## 1. CONSTITUTIONAL BASELINE

**Anthropometry (estimated, longitudinal).** Mesomorph-skewing ectomorph. Adolescent intake (2014) approximately 5'8", 135 lb; adult (late-run) approximately 5'10", 155 lb. Growth completed by approximately age seventeen with no apparent pubertal delay or anomaly. Build is lean and slightly under-muscled relative to age cohort — consistent with a sedentary technical hobbyist who does not lift, run, or train, but who is on his feet on a Circle Q shift four to six days per week and who walks the Jersey City grid rather than driving.

**Skin.** Mediterranean light-olive; tans readily, burns at extremes. No noted cutaneous conditions. Hands characteristically show small, accumulated burn scars and solder pitting along the volar surfaces of the fingertips and the first web space — the occupational stigmata of a self-taught electronics worker who started young and was never taught to wear gloves at a bench.

**Dentition.** Unremarkable; no orthodontia depicted. Mild bruxism implied by jaw set under stress (a clenching pattern repeatedly drawn during high-tension exchanges with Kamala from #5 onward).

**Vision.** Spectacles-wearer from early adolescence; mild to moderate myopia with probable astigmatism, corrected to functional. Lens prescription evidently updated at least twice across the run (frame style changes correspond to depictions of squinting at close work in immediately prior issues). Reading distance held conspicuously close at lab bench — consistent with near-point fatigue from sustained microsoldering and PCB inspection, *not* with any progressive pathology.

**Hearing, voice, gait (pre-injury).** Unremarkable across all three.

**Cardiopulmonary.** No documented disease. Recovery from physical exertion (chase sequences across the Wilson run) is slower than the action-adolescent norm — he is winded where Kamala is not, even accounting for her elasticity. Suggests VO₂ max in the lower half of age-matched norms; consistent with a non-athlete whose only sustained physical activity is shift work and stair-climbing.

**Allergies, immunizations, congenital findings.** No depicted allergies. Childhood immunization status presumed complete (lower-middle-class Catholic family with consistent school enrollment). No congenital findings, no family history of inherited disease on record. Notably: no Inhuman gene expression. Bruno has been physically adjacent to Terrigen exposure events and to the Mist itself and has not transformed — confirming a negative Inhuman screen by exposure rather than by serology.

---

## 2. CHILDHOOD AND PRE-CANON MEDICAL SUBSTRATE (inferred)

No documented serious childhood illness, hospitalization, or surgery. The absence is itself informative: a financially fragile household with thin parental supervision and a younger sibling who repeatedly injures himself and others would, statistically, have generated at least one pediatric ER visit on Bruno's chart. That none surfaces in dialogue or flashback suggests either (a) genuine somatic luck or (b) the more probable reading — that Bruno has, since approximately age ten, *not gone to the doctor for things*. Pattern of under-utilization of medical care is established early and persists.

Vick-related secondary exposures are likely: a household with a chronically delinquent younger brother is a household with secondhand bruises, broken-furniture lacerations, and the small constant low-grade injury load of being the one who pulls the other one out of trouble. None of these would chart. All of them shape the somatic disposition: *injury is normal, injury is private, injury is something you ice yourself in the back room.*

---

## 3. ACUTE INJURY LOG, ADOLESCENCE — CANON ERA

### 3.1 Pre-CWII (2014–2016): the accumulation phase

Across the first two volumes Bruno sustains an extended sequence of minor-to-moderate injuries in service of Kamala's operations. None individually chart; cumulatively they form a pattern.

- **Blunt trauma, multiple, to torso and face**, sustained variously during the Inventor arc (*Ms. Marvel* 2014 #8–11), the Loki encounter, the Last Days tie-in, and several Jersey City street-level incidents. Drawn consistently as a split lip, a periorbital contusion, a favored left side in the days after. Recovery managed at home; no professional care depicted.
- **Near-asphyxiation / submersion**, Inventor arc (#10–11). Bruno is captured, threatened, and physically endangered while retrieving Vick. Mechanism includes restraint and water hazard. No documented sequelae but the event would, in a real chart, generate a note for aspiration risk and an observation period he certainly did not receive.
- **Multiple lacerations**, hands and forearms, from glass, debris, and bench accidents across the Wilson run. Healed by secondary intention. Small scars accumulate on the dorsum of both hands and along the left forearm.
- **Repetitive strain**, bilateral wrists and right thumb, from sustained fine-motor work. Drawn as a habitual shake-out of the right hand between bench tasks from #5 onward — a soft tell, easy to miss, that the dominant hand was already being asked to do more than its tissue allowed long before it was structurally damaged.
- **Chronic sleep curtailment** (see §5).

**Psychological metabolism of the accumulation phase.** Bruno does not narrate these injuries, does not display them to Kamala, does not request care, does not modify behavior to avoid recurrence. The pattern that will define the central event is rehearsed here in miniature: *the body absorbs, the mouth does not speak, the bench is returned to in the morning.*

### 3.2 The hand injury (Civil War II tie-in, *Ms. Marvel* 2015 #12, 2016)

The defining medical event of the file. Sustained during the warehouse confrontation in which Bruno attempts to intervene in Kamala's pursuit of pre-crime detentions sourced from Ulysses's predictive profiling — a course of action he has correctly identified as ethically corrupt and personally corrosive to her.

**Mechanism.** Crush-and-blast composite injury to the right (dominant) hand and distal forearm, sustained at close range during a structural collapse / energetic discharge sequence. Damage is depicted as extensive across the soft-tissue and neurovascular structures of the hand without complete amputation of any digit. Functional reading consistent with:

- Comminuted fracture of multiple metacarpals, probable involvement of the carpus;
- Crush injury to the intrinsic musculature of the hand (thenar and interosseous compartments);
- Significant peripheral nerve damage — most likely a high median nerve lesion with probable ulnar contribution, given the subsequent depicted loss of fine pinch, opposition, and precision grip;
- Vascular compromise sufficient to require urgent reperfusion; ischemic time likely on the threshold beyond which full functional recovery becomes impossible.

**Acute management.** Hospitalized; surgical intervention implied but not depicted in detail. The post-acute image — splinting, then a long-term brace/glove — is consistent with multiple surgical revisions, probable internal fixation, and an attempted nerve repair or graft.

**Long-term sequelae (chronic, life-long as of latest canon).**
- Permanent partial loss of fine motor control in the right hand.
- Reduced precision grip; pinch strength markedly diminished; opposition compromised.
- Probable chronic neuropathic pain and dysesthesia, suggested by the silent reflex of the left hand cradling the right when he is tired or thinking.
- Cold intolerance (vasomotor dysregulation typical of significant peripheral nerve injury) — consistent with his persistent indoor-glove wear even in seasons that don't require it.
- Adaptive equipment: the brace/glove serves both protective and proprioceptive function.
- Adaptive technique: shift to verbal direction of others' hands at the bench; left-hand dominance acquired by necessity for fine work; jig-and-fixture-heavy workflow that substitutes engineered stability for the precision his fingers no longer provide.

**What the injury did to the substrate of his identity.** Bruno's self-concept is load-bearing on his hands. The hands made him useful; the hands made the gadgets that made Kamala safer; the hands were the medium through which a parentified boy bought his place in every room he entered. The injury is therefore *not a hand injury*. It is an attack on the somatic basis of self-worth, sustained in the act of being right about an ethical question the person he loved would not hear. The medical literature on hand trauma in young adults documents elevated rates of post-injury depressive episode, body-image disturbance, and vocational re-identification crisis. Bruno meets none of these criteria *as expressed.* He meets all of them as *suppressed* — see §6.

**The non-discussion.** In the entire post-injury canon, Bruno has not — to file knowledge — initiated a single conversation about the hand. He answers when asked, briefly and without affect. He does not refuse care; he does not seek it. He does not appear to attend follow-up beyond the medically essential. The hand is the largest unspoken thing in his life, and the silence around it is the central diagnostic finding of this section.

### 3.3 Post-CWII injuries (2017–present)

Reduced in frequency and severity, consistent with reduced operational tempo and geographic relocation. Periodic minor trauma associated with continued (lower-intensity) involvement in Kamala's orbit and with field work attached to the Wakandan academy. No second catastrophic event on record. The hand remains the watermark.

---

## 4. TRANSFORMATIONS, ENHANCEMENTS, EXOTIC EXPOSURES

**None.** This is, in this universe, itself a medical finding worth recording.

- **Terrigen exposure:** subject has been proximate to Terrigen Mist events and has not cocooned. Negative Inhuman screen by exposure.
- **Power transfer / accidental enhancement:** none documented despite extensive proximity to enhanced individuals, Asgardian artifacts, and Wakandan research environments.
- **Cybernetic augmentation:** declined or never offered, despite an unambiguous functional indication post-injury. The Wakandan placement would have provided ready access to prosthetic, exo-glove, or neural-interface technology of a kind that would meaningfully restore function. He has not pursued it. The refusal is not stated; it is enacted. Inference: accepting restorative augmentation would require *naming the loss*, and the loss is the thing he does not name.
- **Pharmacological enhancement:** none.

The pattern across this entire category is consistent: Bruno is the human in the room, and he is keeping it that way. The body remains the only currency he is willing to spend in public.

---

## 5. SUBSTANCES, SLEEP, NUTRITION, ROUTINE SOMATICS

**Alcohol.** Never depicted consuming. At social occasions where alcohol is present, he is the one not drinking. Operative reading: the parentified child's vigilance set is incompatible with voluntary disinhibition. He cannot afford to not be the steady one, even hypothetically.

**Tobacco, cannabis, illicit substances.** None.

**Caffeine.** Almost certainly the primary psychoactive of his life. Convenience-store access, late-bench work, the consistent depiction of a cup or can within arm's reach at the lab. Probable intake in the 300–500 mg/day range during high-work periods. Subclinically relevant to chronic sleep curtailment.

**Sleep.** Chronically curtailed. Depicted across multiple artists with periorbital shadowing, micro-yawning at the counter, and a habit of working through the back-room nights at Circle Q. Estimated five to six hours, irregular timing, sleep-debt accumulating across school weeks and being repaid (incompletely) on weekends. The Wakandan period appears to have temporarily improved sleep architecture (better light environment, residential proximity to work, removal from the convenience-store night shift) — observed somatically as reduced periorbital shadowing and a slight increase in baseline color in early Ahmed run depictions.

**Diet.** Mediterranean-Catholic household substrate plus convenience-store top-up. Adequate caloric intake, micronutrient profile probably borderline (high sodium, high processed carbohydrate, intermittent protein, vegetable intake almost entirely dependent on what enters the household). No eating-disorder pattern. He eats when reminded, often by Kamala. He does not cook for pleasure.

**Hydration.** Adequate; convenience-store environment is incidentally protective.

**Exercise.** None deliberate. Incidental ambulation only. Posture deteriorates predictably across the run — a forward head and rounded shoulders consistent with thousands of hours hunched at a bench, drawn with increasing prominence by later artists. Probable early-onset cervical and upper-thoracic myofascial pain by the late-run period, almost certainly unaddressed.

**Sexual health.** No documented concerns. Relationships (Mike, Kareem) depicted as age-appropriate and emotionally serious; somatic-sexual content off-page and not relevant to the file beyond noting that intimacy itself is not a domain in which he appears dysfunctional.

---

## 6. THE PSYCHOLOGICAL TOPOGRAPHY OF THE BODY

Read across the longitudinal record, Bruno's medical history is the somatic transcription of his psychological structure. Three findings are decisive.

**First: the body is the unit of payment.** From middle school onward, Bruno has paid for membership in his own social world in somatic currency — sleep, time-on-feet, accumulated minor trauma, eventually the hand. He has never paid in *demand*: he does not ask, does not invoice, does not extract reciprocal accounting. The body is what he is willing to spend because spending it is invisible to the people he is spending it for. The hand injury is the catastrophic instance of a lifelong micro-economy.

**Second: the silence around the hand is the most important clinical fact in the file.** A normative adolescent response to a permanently disabling injury to the dominant hand — particularly one sustained in the service of, and in disagreement with, the most important person in one's life — would include some combination of expressed grief, expressed anger, treatment-seeking behavior, and identity-renegotiation in dialogue. Bruno expresses none of these. He adapts behaviorally, accepts the brace, retools his workflow, relocates, forms a new attachment, and continues. The integration is real; the suppression is also real. He has not grieved the hand out loud, and the file should not pretend otherwise. The cost of that un-grieved loss will not surface as psychiatric symptom — see the Psychiatric section — but as ongoing structural self-erasure, of which the unattended posture, the unrepaired sleep, the un-augmented hand, and the un-pursued surgical options are all surface expressions.

**Third: he refuses the exits the world offers him.** Wakanda could give him his hand back, in any number of technological registers. He has not asked. Catholic culture offers him a confessional grammar for unspoken pain; he has the moral vocabulary but does not appear to use the sacrament. Friends offer concern; he redirects. Kamala has, at multiple points, opened the door to the conversation about the hand; he has closed it gently every time. The refusal is the diagnosis. He is keeping the wound because the wound is the proof that he was right, and being right alone is the only form of self-assertion his structure permits.

---

## 7. PROGNOSTIC AND FORWARD-LOOKING NOTES

Short-term: stable. Bruno's somatic baseline is sustainable into early adulthood with no anticipated decompensation absent new trauma.

Medium-term (five to fifteen years): vulnerabilities to monitor.
- **Cervical and upper-thoracic musculoskeletal pain syndrome**, near-certain by the late twenties given current posture and bench hours.
- **Progressive overuse of the left (compensating) hand**, with elevated risk of carpal tunnel, lateral epicondylitis, and de Quervain's tenosynovitis. A second hand injury — even a mild one — would be psychologically catastrophic in a way the first was not, because the compensatory architecture would collapse.
- **Visual decline** secondary to sustained near-work without ergonomic correction.
- **Sleep-debt sequelae**: metabolic and mood implications if the pattern persists past adolescence into a working-adult schedule without correction.
- **Late-onset depressive episode** triggered by any event that re-opens the un-grieved hand: a second injury, a relational loss of comparable magnitude, the failure of a workaround. Probability non-trivial; presentation, when it comes, will be quiet and easily missed.

Long-term: the body of a man who has been the steady one since he was a child eventually presents the bill. Bruno's bill is being deferred, not waived. The file's standing recommendation, if a handler existed who cared about him as such, would be: get him to grieve the hand out loud, once, to someone, before he is thirty.

---

**End Section 02 / Medical.**
**Cross-reference:** §3 Psychological (defensive structure, sublimation, suppression); §4 Psychiatric (adjustment disorder, post-injury, provisional); §5 Personality (self-concept organized around usefulness, pressure point: loss of technical competence).


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS — SUBJECT: BRUNO CARRELLI

*Compiled from longitudinal observation, photographic record, and inferred microbehavioral mapping. Cross-referenced against Wilson, Alphona, Miyazawa, Leon, Ahmed, and Saladin-era visual documentation, 2014–present.*

---

## 1. BUILD, FRAME, AND BASELINE

Subject stands approximately 5'10" by late adolescence, lean-mesomorph trending slim; shoulder set narrow rather than broad, with the soft musculature of a teenager who walks Jersey City constantly and lifts inventory at the Circle Q but who has never trained. Resting weight estimated 150–158 lbs across the 2015–2020 observation window, with a modest dip (perhaps 6–8 lbs) in the post-injury / pre-Wakanda interval consistent with stress-related undereating and disrupted sleep.

**Skin:** Mediterranean olive, prone to under-eye darkening that is structural (genetic, deepening with fatigue) rather than pigmentary. Acne presentation typical of a working adolescent who washes hastily — concentrated along the jawline and hairline, consistent with cortisol load and pillow contact rather than dietary. Forearms show small, healed burn scars from soldering iron contact and one longer linear scar (lateral left forearm) consistent with a chemical splash, untreated by professional dermatology — he addressed it himself with cold water and a rag and went back to work.

**Hands (pre-injury):** Long-fingered, with the slight callusing on pad of thumb and side of index that characterizes regular precision-tool use. Nail beds short, kept short by biting rather than clipping (see §6, Oral Habits). Knuckles unmarked — he has never punched anything.

**Hands (post-injury, 2016–present):** Right hand carries permanent fine-motor deficit. Surface presentation in resting state appears nearly normal; the deficit emerges in *task*. Fingers 2, 3, and 4 of right hand show subtle hypotonic curl at rest, the resting posture slightly more flexed than the left. He wears a brace intermittently — fingerless, neoprene-and-Velcro, dorsal stabilizer bar — applied for tasks demanding sustained grip and removed for everyday motion. Even unbraced, observable tells: when he reaches with the right hand, the wrist leads slightly ahead of the fingers, as though he is *aiming* the hand rather than allowing it to fall naturally onto a target. He has rewired most fine work to the left.

**Hair:** Dark brown to near-black, fine, mildly wavy; cut in a forgettable utility shape — slightly longer in front than is fashionable, because he gets it cut when his mother says he looks shaggy rather than on a schedule. Owl-cowlick at right crown, never tamed. In Wakanda-era documentation the cut is sharper and shorter, consistent with access to a professional barber in a structured living environment for the first time in his life.

---

## 2. POSTURE AND CARRIAGE

**Default standing posture:** Weight set slightly back on the heels, shoulders rolled forward maybe ten degrees from neutral — the bench-and-counter posture of someone who has spent more cumulative hours leaning over a work surface than standing socially. Head carriage tends to drop the chin a hair, so that he addresses most rooms from a position of *looking up under the brow* rather than at level eye-line. With Kamala, the chin lifts; he meets her gaze. With strangers, it stays down.

**Seated:** Forward-perched at counters and benches; spine flexed, elbows on the surface, forearms taking weight. At rest in a chair (couch, classroom) he migrates toward corners and walls — he sits at the *end* of the booth, the *edge* of the bed, the *corner* of the couch, never the middle. This is not visibly an anxious avoidance; it reads as *yielding the central seat to whoever needs it more*. He has done it his whole life.

**Gait:** Quick, economical, near-silent in sneakers. Stride length moderate, cadence brisk; he does not amble. Walks with hands in pockets or one hand wrapped around the strap of his bag, rarely swinging free. After the hand injury a subtle protective posture appears: the right elbow drifts inward toward the ribs in transit, the forearm carried at a slight angle across the body, as though shielding the hand from being jostled by passing crowds. He is not consciously aware of this.

**Threat posture:** Does not adopt a fighting stance. Under threat he turns his body fractionally to interpose himself between the threat and whoever he is with (Kamala, Vick, Mike). The shoulders square forward, the chin drops further, the hands come out of pockets and stay open at hip level — never closed into fists. The whole presentation is *blockade* rather than *combatant*.

**Intimacy posture:** Loosens at the shoulders; sits straighter when Kamala is across from him at a table (the spine remembers it is being looked at). With Kareem in Wakanda-era documentation, observable shift to a posture more *received* than *vigilant* — he sits back into chairs, leans against walls, accepts physical proximity without bracing.

---

## 3. GAIT, MOVEMENT, AND ROUTE-PATTERN

**Daily route, Jersey City baseline (2014–2017):** Home → Coles Academic → Circle Q → home. Roughly triangular, total daily ambulation 3–4 miles. He takes the *same* side of the same streets; observable preference for the building-side of any sidewalk over the curb-side. He cuts through the same alley behind the Circle Q to take out garbage, always around 8:15 PM on weekdays.

**Stair behavior:** Takes them two at a time going up when in a hurry, one at a time going down, always with right hand on the rail (pre-injury) or left hand on the rail (post-injury — adaptive switch noted).

**Door behavior:** Holds doors. For everyone. Without performative gesture. He does not announce the hold; he simply waits with the door open and does not move on until the person behind him is through. Diagnostic of the parentified vigilance set.

**Transit micro-pattern:** On Jersey City light rail and PATH, he stands rather than sits even when seats are available — *unless* he is exhausted, in which case he sits at the end of a row, against the window or wall, and works on a phone or tablet. Reads in transit. Does not look at other passengers.

---

## 4. HANDS, GESTURE, AND MANIPULATION

**Pre-injury (2014–2016):** Hands in near-constant motion when working, near-perfect stillness when listening. Gesture vocabulary while speaking is minimal — he is not a talker-with-his-hands. The hands earn their movement; they do not perform it. At a bench, fingertips lead — he picks up small objects pad-first, never claw-grip. Soldering iron held in three-finger precision grip, like a pen.

**Post-injury (2016–present):** Right hand goes still at conversational baseline — actively held still, not naturally still. He stabilizes it on the table, on his thigh, against his other forearm. When the right hand is needed in conversational gesture (pointing, reaching for something across a counter), there is a half-beat of cognitive initiation — a microsecond of *deciding* to use it — that was not present before.

**Self-touch tells:**
- *Thinking:* Pre-injury, right thumbnail to lower lip; mild pressure, no biting. Post-injury, this has migrated to the left thumbnail, same gesture, mirrored. The migration was unconscious.
- *Embarrassment / being seen:* Hand to back of neck, ruffling the hair upward at the nape. Almost always the dominant-side hand pre-injury; now the left.
- *Concentrating / problem-solving:* Index finger taps once, twice against the workbench or table edge, then stops. Not a sustained drum — a discrete *full-stop* tap.
- *Suppressed reaction:* Brief, almost imperceptible squeeze of his own opposite wrist with the dominant hand, under the bench or under the table. Diagnostic micro-tell of internalized affect. Frequency increases dramatically in Kamala's presence post-2016.
- *Post-injury specific:* Light, absent rubbing of the dorsum of the right hand with the left thumb, in moments of conversational silence. Reads as soothing rather than examining. He does not know he is doing it. He has never been asked.

**Object handling:** Gentle with everything, including objects that do not require gentleness. Sets a coffee cup down without sound. Closes doors with two-stage pressure (latch, then release). Hands tools to other people *handle-first*, every time, including pens.

---

## 5. FACE, GAZE, AND EXPRESSIVE PATTERN

**Resting face:** Mild, slightly mournful baseline — the corners of the mouth at neutral or fractionally turned down, the eyes attentive. Not depressive; *watchful*. He has the resting face of someone who is processing the room without contributing to it.

**Smile:** Two distinct registers.
- *Social smile:* Closed-mouth, brief, polite, ends quickly. Deployed for customers, classmates, teachers, strangers, Mike's parents.
- *Real smile:* Asymmetric — pulls higher on the left — open enough to show teeth, crinkles the outer corners of the eyes (orbicularis oculi engaged; Duchenne-positive). Reserved almost exclusively for Kamala in the 2014–2016 corpus; expands to include Kareem, Mike (occasionally), and Vick (rarely, when Vick is doing well) in later eras.

**Laugh:** Rare. Short, a single exhaled *huh* through the nose for most situations; an actual audible laugh — open-mouthed, head dropped forward — perhaps three or four times per observed year, almost always Kamala-initiated. He laughs *with* her, not *at* jokes generally.

**Gaze pattern:** Strong sustained eye contact with intimates (Kamala, Vick, Kareem); fleeting, drop-and-return pattern with strangers and authority figures. With Kamala specifically, a documented micro-tell: he looks at her *while she is not looking*, drops his eyes the instant her head turns toward him. This pattern persists, attenuated, into the Ahmed/Saladin eras.

**Blink rate:** Within normal range at rest (15–20/min). Suppresses to noticeably below baseline during precision lab work — the fixed engineer's stare. *Elevates* sharply (25–30/min) in two specific contexts: (1) when Kamala discusses a plan he believes is dangerous, and (2) when his hand is being looked at or discussed by another person.

**Brow:** Slight default furrow between the brows — not scowl, just *attention*. Lifts symmetrically in surprise; lifts asymmetrically (left only) in skepticism, which is his closest approximation to publicly disagreeing with someone.

**Crying:** Not observed on-page. Inferred from absence: when situations that would warrant tears occur (the hand, the rift with Kamala, leaving for Wakanda), the documented face is *blanker* than baseline, the breath held shallow, the gaze fixed on a middle-distance object. The grief is happening; it is happening *inward*.

---

## 6. ORAL, GROOMING, AND MICRO-HABIT

**Nail biting:** Persistent, low-grade, since childhood. Concentrated on thumbs (both) and index of dominant hand pre-injury. Increases under stress; he has, on observed occasion, drawn blood from the cuticle of the right thumb and continued working without comment.

**Lip:** Slight pressing-together of the lips when concentrating; full lip-bite (lower lip, slightly off-center to the right) when actively suppressing a verbal response — most often when he has decided not to say something to Kamala.

**Throat-clear:** Single soft cough/clear before initiating speech in a group of more than three people. Absent in dyads.

**Grooming baseline:** Adequate but not invested. Showers daily but quickly. Wears the same three or four t-shirt/hoodie combinations on rotation through high school — the lab-stained one for the workshop, the cleaner ones for school. Owns one dress shirt, kept on a hanger in his closet, deployed perhaps annually. In Wakanda the wardrobe expands and standardizes — he begins to dress, mildly, *like an adult*. The shift is observable and unremarked-upon by him.

**Scent:** Soap (institutional, whatever is in the family bathroom — Irish Spring or equivalent), faint solder-flux residue on workshop days, cheap drugstore deodorant. No cologne, ever. The Carrelli household scent profile bleeds through — tomato, garlic, old cooking oil — into the fabric of his clothes through middle adolescence; fades after Wakanda.

**Eating in public:** Quiet, efficient, no commentary. Eats whatever is provided; preferences not voiced unless directly asked. Has been observed eating around the unfamiliar ingredients in Kamala's mother's cooking with visible care not to give offense, including consuming items he plainly does not enjoy with a flat polite face.

---

## 7. INGESTION AND APPETITE

**Diet baseline (Jersey City):** Catholic-Italian household food at home (pasta-heavy, weekly fish, Sunday meal as anchor), supplemented by Circle Q convenience inventory during shifts — pre-packaged sandwich, occasional hot dog from the roller, coffee. Coffee consumption begins around age fourteen, escalates through high school; black with sugar, two cups before noon by the post-injury period.

**Hydration:** Inadequate. Forgets water during long lab sessions; rehydrates with coffee or whatever soda is near the bench.

**Appetite under stress:** Suppresses. Does not eat the day of the hand injury, does not eat the morning of the Wakanda departure (inferred). Reverses to normal within 24–48 hours; not a sustained pattern.

**No alcohol** observed at any age, including in contexts (parties, Wakanda academy social events) where it would be unremarkable. The abstention is not advertised. He drinks water or soda and does not explain. Likely a confluence of Catholic-cultural baseline, parentified-vigilance unwillingness to relinquish control, and a quiet awareness that his father (inferred) may have a relationship with alcohol he does not wish to replicate.

**No drug use** of any kind on record or inferred. He works in a convenience store; he knows where everything comes from.

---

## 8. SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

**Quantity:** Chronically insufficient. Estimated 5–6 hours/night through high school, with one or two true sleep nights per week of 8+. The under-eye darkening is a structural readout.

**Pattern:** Late to bed (1–2 AM typical, working on a project or finishing homework after a Circle Q shift), early to rise (6:30–7 AM for school). Naps short and rare; he does not nap by choice but has been observed asleep at his workbench with his head on his forearm, woken by Kamala or Vick.

**Position:** Inferred curled-side-right pre-injury; shift to curled-side-left post-injury, to protect the hand. Pillow-contact acne tracks the side change.

**Wakanda-era correction:** Documented improvement in sleep — structured dormitory schedule, no Circle Q shift, no Vick to monitor at 2 AM. Under-eye darkening visibly lighter in mid-2017 documentation. Returns to baseline insufficiency on every visit home.

**Dreaming:** Not documented. Not discussed.

---

## 9. SEXUAL AND INTIMATE BEHAVIOR

**Baseline expression:** Restrained, courteous, not performatively chaste but not initiating. Across the entire observed adolescent corpus, Bruno has never made a first physical move on any partner that is shown on-page. With Mike, the physical relationship is depicted as comfortable, mutual, gentle — hand-holding, brief kisses, sitting close — and *Mike sets the pace*. With Kareem, same pattern, though the documentation is sparser.

**Tells of attraction (Kamala-directed, pre-confession era):** The looking-while-she-doesn't-look pattern. A specific micro-lean *toward* her in shared seating that he corrects within a second of noticing. Coffee delivered to her unprompted with the exact preparation she likes — affection routed through service. Tone-modulation in her presence: voice drops a quarter-step, slows, softens. He speaks to her *quietly* in a way he does not speak to anyone else.

**Tells of attraction (Mike-directed):** More physical, more openly affectionate, less worshipful. The body relaxes around Mike in a way it does not around Kamala. The smile is the closed social one more often, but the posture is more open. This is the somatic signature of a relationship he can *be in* rather than *protect*.

**Tells of attraction (Kareem-directed, Wakanda era):** Documented increase in sustained eye contact, mirrored seating posture, willingness to be touched first. The intimacy register here is the most *adult* of his observed corpus — the body has learned, by this point, that it is allowed to be received.

**Arousal/embarrassment response:** A fast, light flush along the upper cheekbones and tops of the ears, ears specifically pinking before the cheeks. Recovered quickly; he turns the head fractionally away and resumes the prior activity. Does not stammer; does *go quiet*.

**Private sexual behavior:** Not documented and would not be, but the inferred profile is consistent with the rest of the somatic record — private, infrequent, unaccompanied by ritual or compulsion, occurring in stolen windows of a heavily-scheduled life.

---

## 10. STATE-DEPENDENT SHIFTS — INTEGRATED READ

**CALM (Circle Q on a weekday afternoon, lab session alone, walk home in good weather):** Posture relaxed-forward, hands occupied with a task or pocketed, breath slow and unmonitored, blink at baseline, micro-tells (wrist-squeeze, lip-bite) absent. The most himself he gets when no one is watching. Hums occasionally — barely audible, no identifiable melody.

**ENGAGED (with Kamala, in conversation about a problem):** Postural lift, chin up, sustained eye contact, blink slightly elevated, hands stilled and attentive on the table, voice softened. The Duchenne smile available. The wrist-squeeze tell active if she is describing a plan he disagrees with.

**STRESSED (Vick in trouble, Kamala in danger he cannot reach, hand giving him grief):** Posture *more upright* not less, hands going to opposite-arm grip or pocket, jaw set, blink suppressed, breath shallow-and-held rather than fast. He does not pace. He goes still and *thinks*. The voice does not raise; it gets quieter and more clipped. People who do not know him read this as calm. It is the opposite of calm.

**THREATENED (direct physical danger, his own or another's):** Interposition stance, hands open at hip level, chin down, gaze tracking the threat, breathing controlled. Will move *toward* the threat to put his body between it and a loved one. Will not strike first, will not strike at all if a non-violent option exists. Voice in this state is the steadiest it ever gets — the parentified child's wartime register.

**GRIEVING / WOUNDED (post-injury, Wakanda departure, Kamala-rift):** Affect *flatter* than baseline, not more expressive. Eats less, sleeps worse, works more. The compensatory mechanism is *increased function*, not decreased. Withdrawal masquerading as productivity. The body absorbs what the mouth will not say.

**INTIMATE (with Kareem, with Mike, in rare unguarded moments with Kamala):** Shoulders drop, spine relaxes against the chair-back, hands come to rest open on the thighs or table, breath audible and slow, the asymmetric real smile available, eye contact sustained. This is the state his body is built for and the state his life has most rarely allowed him.

---

## 11. INTEGRATED PATTERN

The Carrelli body, read longitudinally, is a body trained to *take up less room than it occupies*. It is quiet, gentle with objects and people, vigilant without performing vigilance, expressive only with intimates and only at low amplitude. It absorbs damage — soldering burns, chemical splashes, a permanent hand injury, chronic sleep debt — without converting damage into complaint. The somatic signature of parentification is written across every system: the forward-leaning bench posture, the door-holding, the end-of-the-booth seating, the abstention from intoxicants, the routing of affection through service, the silence of the right hand after 2016.

The single most diagnostic somatic finding in the entire file is *what the body does not do*. It does not rage. It does not weep. It does not collapse. It does not announce its injuries. It adapts — switches the wrist-squeeze to the other hand, switches the sleeping side, switches the country — and continues. The cost of this is not visible on any single frame. It is visible only when frames are stacked across years, and the stack shows a young man who has been the steady one since he was a child, whose body has learned every economy of self-erasure, and whose reliability has, to date, never been allowed to fail.

What that body would look like the day it failed is not in the record. It is the question the record is for.


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# UATU DOSSIER — SUBJECT: BRUNO CARRELLI
## Section 6: Attachment & Relational Patterns

---

### 6.1 The Foundational Template — Parentification as Original Bond

Every attachment Bruno Carrelli has formed in observable canon, from his earliest appearance on the Circle Q register through his Wakanda transfer and his post-return reintegration into the Jersey City cohort, is a variant on a single template laid down in the Carrelli household before he was old enough to consent to it. To map his relational style without first mapping that household is to misread every gesture that follows.

The Carrelli household, as it appears in fragments across the Wilson run (*Ms. Marvel* 2014 #1–19; *Ms. Marvel* 2015 #1–19), is a structurally thin caregiving environment. The mother is depicted on-page in only a handful of panels across the entire Wilson run, almost always tired, almost always in transit between shifts; the father is more absence than presence, registered through implication and Bruno's offhand references rather than through scenes. Vick, four to five years younger, is the chaos generator — truant, susceptible, eventually drawn into the Inventor's labor cell. Into this configuration Bruno arrives temperamentally suited to absorb the load: high conscientiousness, high agreeableness, strong cognitive control, and a moral seriousness that reads as innate but is more likely the early calcification of a child who learned that the household held together because *he* held it together.

The result is what developmental literature recognizes as **instrumental parentification with successful adaptation**: the child takes on caregiving and household-management tasks beyond age-appropriate scope, develops precocious competence as compensation, and — critically — internalizes the role as identity. By the time Bruno is sixteen and clerking at Circle Q on a school night while his peers attend a waterfront party, he is not experiencing this as deprivation. He is experiencing it as *who he is*. The bond between Bruno and his family is therefore not the standard child-to-parent attachment with secure base behavior; it is **inverted**, with Bruno functioning as the secure base for Vick and, by quiet extension, for the entire household economy.

This inversion is the master template. Every subsequent relationship of significance will be assessed, unconsciously, against the question: *who in this dyad is carrying it?* And Bruno will, every time, volunteer to be the carrier — not from masochism, not from low self-worth (he has stable self-worth), but because *being the carrier is the role in which he knows how to love at all*.

---

### 6.2 Attachment Classification — Earned-Secure with Dismissing-Avoidant Decompensation Under Threat

In Ainsworth/Main terms, Bruno presents at baseline as **earned-secure**. He can initiate closeness, sustain it across long absences, tolerate conflict without rupture, repair after rupture, and form new attachments after loss (Mike, Kareem). He shows no fearful-avoidant doubling, no disorganized fragmentation, no preoccupied clinging. In low- to moderate-stress conditions he is, by every observable measure, securely attached.

The decompensation pattern is specific and reproducible. When his own needs come into direct collision with the needs of an attachment figure — when the system cannot satisfy both — Bruno reliably **shifts into a dismissing-avoidant posture toward his own demand**. He does not withdraw from the other person's needs; he withdraws from *his own*. The bid he suppresses is always his own bid. Observable instances:

- **#3 (2014), discovery of Kamala's powers:** Bruno's first words are not about himself ("you scared me," "what is happening to *me*, watching this") but about her ("are you okay?"). The self-referential bid is foreclosed in real time.
- **Vick arc (#8–11, 2014):** Bruno conceals the scope of the problem from Kamala for as long as he can, attempts solo resolution, and only escalates when forced. The bid for help is deferred past the point of personal safety.
- **Pre-Civil War II romantic foreclosure:** Bruno dates Mike rather than confess to Kamala while Kamala is unattached and (later) attached to Kamran. The bid for romantic reciprocity is rerouted into a parallel relationship.
- **Post-hand-injury silence:** Bruno does not narrate the injury to Kamala, does not assign cost, does not ask for acknowledgment. The bid for repair is converted into geographic exit.

The clinical signature is consistent: under threat, the *other* remains a secure base; the *self* is treated as the demand that must be quieted so the bond can continue. This is not avoidant attachment in the textbook sense (avoidants disengage from the other). It is something rarer and more specific — **earned-secure attachment with a parentified suppression bias**, in which the bond is protected by erasing one half of its accounting.

---

### 6.3 How He Bonds — Slow Onset, Service-Mediated, Asymmetric by Design

Bruno does not bond through self-disclosure. He bonds through **acts of useful presence**. The medium of intimacy, for him, is the favor delivered before it was asked for: the soldered repair, the cup of coffee already poured when the person walks in, the door propped open, the alibi pre-engineered, the gadget already prototyped against a need the other person had not yet articulated. His love language, in the lay register, is anticipatory service.

This has three operational consequences. **First**, his bonds form slowly from the outside, because acts of service take time to accumulate into legibility — but they are unusually stable once formed, because they are grounded in pattern rather than declaration. **Second**, his bonds are *legible to the recipient only retrospectively*; Kamala does not understand the architecture of Bruno's devotion until late in the Wilson run, and arguably not fully until after the Wakanda departure. **Third**, the bond is **structurally asymmetric from inception** — Bruno is the giver, the other is the receiver, and Bruno arranges the relationship to make this asymmetry invisible by minimizing his own visible needs.

The asymmetry is not accidental and not, in Bruno's own experience, painful. It is the form in which loving feels safe to him. A symmetric bond — one in which he was equally a recipient of care — would require him to be the kind of person who *asks*, and the parentified child's most deeply trained reflex is the suppression of asking.

---

### 6.4 The Kamala Khan Bond — Master Case

The relationship with Kamala Khan is the master case of Bruno's relational template, the one in which every feature is fully expressed and the one against which every other bond can be calibrated.

**Phase 1 — Substrate (pre-#1 through #3, 2014).** Pre-existing friendship, calibrated as long-running but undeclared. Bruno already loves Kamala before the series begins; Kamala reads him as a friend. The asymmetry is foundational and predates the powers.

**Phase 2 — Operationalized devotion (#3–#11, 2014).** Bruno becomes Kamala's technical and ethical support infrastructure. Builds her costume iterations, troubleshoots her physiology, runs ground-level reconnaissance, holds her secret without negotiation. Observable micro-behaviors: positions himself between Kamala and physical threats reflexively; speaks her name with a softer prosody than he uses for other names (a registerable tell across the Alphona issues, in which body language is given unusual interpretive weight); is the only character whose facial affect changes measurably when she enters a panel.

**Phase 3 — Romantic disclosure and foreclosure (Last Days arc, 2015, and immediately post).** Bruno tries to confess; the timing is wrong; Kamala is preoccupied with the imminent incursion. The confession is converted, by Bruno, into withdrawal and the eventual pursuit of Mike. Critically: Bruno does not blame Kamala for the foreclosure. He absorbs it as a fact about the world rather than a fact about her.

**Phase 4 — Rupture (Civil War II, *Ms. Marvel* 2015 #8–13, 2016).** The ethical disagreement over Ulysses's predictive profiling is the only sustained instance in canon of Bruno *holding his ground against Kamala*. He is right; she is wrong; he says so. The hand injury follows. Kamala's response — defensiveness, then guilt, then deflection — is the closest she comes to actively damaging the bond. Bruno's response is not retaliation. It is the **conversion of grievance into geography**.

**Phase 5 — Exile (Wakanda, 2017).** Distance as the only available form of self-protection. Note the *form* of the withdrawal: Bruno does not cut off contact, does not refuse calls, does not articulate the breach. He simply *removes his body from the room* and lets the relational asymmetry collapse under its own weight without ever naming it.

**Phase 6 — Return and professionalization (Ahmed run onward, 2019–).** Bruno returns. The friendship is restored in form. The *quality* is different — there is a measured distance, a slight formality at the edges of warm exchanges, a refusal to re-enter the position of confidant-primary. He is friendly; he is not *available* in the unlimited way he once was. This is not coldness. It is the residue of a person who has learned exactly where the line was, the hard way, and will not cross it again.

The Kamala bond demonstrates the full template: service-mediated formation, asymmetric devotion, foreclosed romantic bid, principled disagreement under stress, somatic cost absorbed silently, geographic flight as substitute for confrontation, and partial reintegration with permanent recalibration. Every other significant bond in his life is a variation on a subset of these moves.

---

### 6.5 The Vick Carrelli Bond — Parent-Sibling Inversion

With Vick, Bruno occupies the parental role the parents do not fill. The bond is characterized by **chronic disappointment held in a frame of unconditional reception**. Vick fails, Bruno absorbs; Vick relapses, Bruno rescues; Vick endangers Bruno, Bruno does not punish.

The pattern of concealment is diagnostic: Bruno hides Vick's Inventor entanglement from Kamala for as long as he can manage, not because he doubts Kamala's discretion but because *exposing Vick's failure feels like a failure of his own custodial duty*. The shame is Bruno's, not Vick's, in Bruno's internal accounting. This is classic parentification — the parentified child carries the sibling's moral debits as if they were his own.

Notably, Bruno does not appear to *enjoy* Vick. The relationship has the texture of duty rather than delight. There is affection underneath, but the affect Bruno brings to Vick is most often tired patience, occasionally surfacing as the brief exasperation of a person who has been managing this specific failure mode for years.

---

### 6.6 The Mike Miller Bond — Displacement Done Gently

The relationship with Michaela Miller is the most ethically interesting bond in the file because it tests a hypothesis: if Bruno's relational template is to give more than he receives and absorb the cost silently, would he *use* a person to displace longing for someone else?

The answer the canon supplies is: **yes, but with unusual care**. Mike is genuinely well-treated. She is not deceived in any sustainable sense — she perceives Bruno's situation with Kamala more clearly than Bruno himself does, and her exit (eventually amicable) is precipitated by *her* clarity rather than his cruelty. Bruno's affection for Mike is real; the displacement is real too; the two coexist, neither cancels the other.

The bond demonstrates a second-order pattern: **Bruno is capable of partnership when the dynamic is not pre-loaded with a rescuer-debt structure**. With Mike, there is no asymmetric crisis demanding his service; the relationship is permitted to operate closer to equilibrium. The fact that it nonetheless terminates is information — Bruno does not *know how* to fully invest in a relationship that does not run on his standard architecture. The egalitarian relationship is the one he does not know how to keep.

---

### 6.7 The Kareem (Red Dagger) Bond — Lateral, Competent, Geographically Buffered

The Wakanda-era relationship with Kareem is the canon's evidence that Bruno can form a new significant attachment after rupture. The structural features are revealing:

- **Lateral, not asymmetric.** Kareem is competent, mission-capable, and not in need of rescue. Bruno is not the parent of this dyad.
- **Adjacent to Kamala's orbit but not Kamala.** Bruno moves toward someone who shares the cultural-emotional vocabulary of his pre-injury life without re-entering the specific wound.
- **Geographically buffered.** The relationship is conducted across continents for substantial stretches. Distance is no longer the *solution to* a problem; it is built into the *premise* of the bond.

This is a healthier attachment than the Kamala one ever was, precisely because its architecture forecloses the failure modes Bruno is most susceptible to. He cannot become the sole infrastructure for Kareem's life; the relationship will not collapse into rescuer-debt; the asymmetric bid is structurally prevented. Whether this is growth or evasion — whether Bruno is *learning* a new way to attach or simply *selecting* environments that don't demand he learn — is the question the longitudinal record cannot fully resolve.

---

### 6.8 How He Distrusts — Quietly, Patiently, Without Theater

Bruno's distrust does not announce itself. He does not confront, accuse, or test. When trust erodes — as it does, partially, with Kamala post-CWII; as it does briefly with certain new figures in the Ahmed run who attempt to recruit Kamala into ethically dubious projects — the marker is a **withdrawal of unprompted service**. The favors stop coming. The anticipatory presence dials back. The intimacy of the unspoken contract is replaced by polite, transactional engagement.

This is *legible only to people who have known him in his open mode*. To a stranger, professionalized Bruno looks like normal-friendly Bruno. To Kamala, post-2017, the change is unmistakable: he is warm, he is present, he is *not the same person*, and the difference is in the volume of what is no longer offered.

He does not betray. There is no instance in canon of Bruno acting against the interests of someone he is bonded to, even after the bond is damaged. The closest analogue is the Ulysses confrontation, which is a refusal to *participate* rather than a betrayal — he will not collaborate with what he believes is wrong, even if the cost is the relationship. This is principled non-cooperation, not betrayal. The distinction matters and Bruno would insist on it.

---

### 6.9 How He Is Betrayed, and How He Repairs

Bruno has been betrayed in the canon — by Vick (repeatedly, in the small-stakes sense of broken trust); by Kamala (in the CWII sense of pursuing a course he had identified as harmful, and getting him injured in the process). His repair pattern is consistent and somewhat unusual.

**He does not require apology to repair.** He requires *the relationship to be possible again on a recalibrated basis*. With Vick, the recalibration is downward — expectations are lowered, monitoring is increased, the bond is sustained at reduced intimacy. With Kamala, the recalibration is structural — the role of primary confidant is vacated, the geography is changed, the intensity is throttled. The relationship continues because Bruno does not believe in the cleanly severed bond; he believes in the relationship that *adapts to what the other person has shown themselves to be*.

This sounds generous and is partly generous. It is also a defense — the refusal to demand apology is a refusal to *make his hurt the other person's burden*, which is the parentified child's master move. He repairs by absorbing the recalibration cost himself.

---

### 6.10 Intimacy and Dependency — The Receiving Problem

Bruno gives intimacy fluently. He receives it badly. Across the canon, the pattern is consistent: when someone attempts to care for him — Kamala bringing food to his lab, Mike asking how he is, Aamir Khan offering counsel — Bruno's response is a smooth, almost reflexive conversion of the received care into either (a) deflection toward the giver's own situation ("how are *you*?"), (b) minimization ("I'm fine, just tired"), or (c) instrumentalization (turning the received care into a task he can perform in return, thereby canceling the debt).

He **cannot tolerate undischarged debt of care**. To owe and not repay is, in his internal economy, a destabilizing state. The Wakanda transfer follows, among its other functions, this logic: in Wakanda he is a *student*, a *peer*, no one's primary support — and therefore no one to whom he owes the impossible reciprocation of being cared for in the home environment where his identity is *being the carer*.

Dependency, in the directed sense — needing another person — appears in his behavior as **structural absence**. He does not call for help. He does not lean. He does not delegate emotional load. The closest he comes to dependency is the steady, unspoken presence of Kamala in his pre-CWII years as the figure his entire affective life is organized around. That is dependency in the form he can metabolize: dependency by *orientation*, not dependency by *request*.

---

### 6.11 The Template Repeated — A Single Pattern, Variably Expressed

Pulled back to altitude, every Bruno Carrelli relationship in the longitudinal record is a permutation of the same underlying template:

1. **Identify the person's needs faster than they do.**
2. **Position himself as quiet infrastructure for those needs.**
3. **Suppress his own bids inside the relationship to keep the asymmetry stable.**
4. **Absorb costs — physical, emotional, opportunity — without ledger.**
5. **When the asymmetry becomes unsustainable, withdraw geographically or functionally rather than confront.**
6. **Permit the relationship to continue in recalibrated form, with the recalibration cost paid by him.**

With Vick: the template runs in parental register, indefinitely. With Kamala: the template runs at maximum amplitude, breaks under load, recalibrates downward. With Mike: the template is partially suspended (no crisis to support), and the relationship cannot survive the absence of its usual fuel. With Kareem: the template is structurally prevented from full activation by geography and Kareem's self-sufficiency, and the relationship is healthier for it. With the post-return Jersey City cohort: the template runs at deliberately throttled volume, the lesson of the hand installed as a permanent governor.

The operational implication, for any party reading this file with an eye to predicting Bruno's behavior in novel relational configurations, is this: he will, by default, take the carrier position. He will not ask to be relieved of it. He will not signal when it is becoming unsustainable. He will leave before he will fight. And he will, with extraordinary grace, continue to love the person who never knew what he was carrying — because in his original household, the love and the carrying were never separable, and he has not yet learned, and may never learn, that they were supposed to be.


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# UATU DOSSIER — SUBJECT: BRUNO CARRELLI
## Section 6: Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

---

### 6.0 Framing

What follows is a stratified inventory of the defensive architecture observable across approximately a decade of longitudinal record (Wilson 2014 onward, through Ahmed, Saladin, and the mutant-cohort era). The framework is broadly Vaillantian — mature → neurotic → immature → pathological — adapted to fit a subject whose defensive repertoire is, in clinical terms, *unusually high-functioning*, with the consequence that his pathology hides inside the maturity of his defenses rather than beneath it. Each mechanism is described operationally: what triggers it, what it looks like in observable behavior, what it costs him, what it protects, and where in the canon it can be tracked.

A central interpretive point governs the whole section: **in Bruno, the defenses are not failing. They are working too well.** A defense that succeeds at preventing acute distress can still, over years, hollow out the person it is protecting. The dossier's task is to map that hollowing.

---

### 6.1 Mature Defenses (Vaillant Level IV) — The Visible Architecture

These are the defenses he is *known* by. They are also the ones that make him legible as a "good boy," "the responsible one," "the one who can be counted on" — labels that have functioned, across his life, as both true description and load-bearing trap.

#### 6.1.1 Sublimation — Primary, Continuous, Identity-Constitutive

The dominant defense of the entire profile. Bruno converts affective load — longing, fear, helplessness, grief — into technical work. The conversion is so total and so habitual that it is almost certainly invisible to him as a defense at all; he experiences it as *who he is*.

**Behavioral signature:** Whenever an emotional pressure approaches threshold, the observable response is a redirection of attention into a fabrication task. After Kamala's first transformation, his processing of the metaphysical shock is to begin building her gear. After the Vick arc nearly kills him, he is in the back room of the Circle Q soldering. After the hand injury — the injury that destroys the *medium* of the defense — he adapts the defense to one-handed work and verbal direction of others' hands rather than abandoning it. In Wakanda, the academy slot is itself a sublimative structure: pour the unmetabolized grief into rigorous coursework.

**What it protects:** the experience of helplessness. As long as there is a project, he is not powerless.

**What it costs:** the affect never gets processed in its own register. It exits the system disguised as a working circuit board. The grief over the hand, the grief over Kamala, the fear during Vick's near-loss — these all have a *technical residue* but no *emotional residue*. Externally elegant; internally, the ledger never closes.

#### 6.1.2 Altruism — Genuine and Strategic Simultaneously

Bruno's altruism is real. He does not fake care for Kamala, for Vick, for Mike, for Kareem, for the Circle Q regulars. *And* the altruism performs a defensive function: by occupying the giving end of every transaction, he forecloses the structural possibility of needing to ask for anything himself.

**Behavioral signature:** He volunteers before being asked. He anticipates needs. He drafts solutions and presents them as already-existing options ("I made you a thing"), which removes the awkwardness of his recipient having to request help and incidentally removes any moment in which he is owed anything explicit. The gift is structured so that no debt is contracted on either side. He is famously the friend who shows up without being called and leaves before being thanked.

**What it protects:** the vulnerability of asking.

**What it costs:** he never learns to receive. Across the canon there is no scene in which Bruno is the one being cared for and accepts it without converting it into a debt to be repaid by future service. When Kareem cares for him in Wakanda, the relationship works partly because Kareem doesn't *need* him in the way Kamala did — but even there, Bruno's intimate move is to *make Kareem useful tools*, not to ask Kareem to make him anything.

#### 6.1.3 Suppression — Conscious Shelving, Chronically Deployed

Suppression is the mature cousin of repression: the person knows what they feel and decides, deliberately, to set it aside for now. In Bruno it is the **single most pervasive defense in the file**, and the one that has done the most subtle damage.

**Behavioral signature:** The hand. The romantic disappointment. The Wakanda decision. Kamala's repeated near-deaths. The Civil War II rupture. Every one of these is met with a verbal and behavioral pattern of *decline to discuss, return to function*. He does not deny — he is too truthful for denial — and he does not repress — the material is available to him. He simply *declines the agenda item*. Asked directly about the hand, he changes the subject with a small joke about needing better tools. Asked about Kamala, by Kareem, he gives a clean, honest, structurally incomplete answer.

**What it protects:** the operational tempo. Suppression is what keeps him functional in the moments immediately following loss.

**What it costs:** when suppression is *episodic* it is mature; when it is *chronic* it becomes indistinguishable from a low-grade dissociative posture toward one's own life. Bruno has shelved so many agenda items that his interior has the structure of a back room of the Circle Q at closing — orderly, dark, full of boxes that were going to be unpacked later, later never having arrived.

#### 6.1.4 Anticipation — Structural, Pre-Conscious

He runs scenarios. He pre-fabricates the gear for the mission Kamala does not yet know she will need. He has the conversation with Vick's pursuers planned three exchanges deep before he opens his mouth. He sees the Ulysses problem before Kamala does.

**Behavioral signature:** Solutions appear suspiciously fast. Tools appear suspiciously ready. This is not magic; it is constant background simulation. His sleep is curtailed in part because the simulator never powers down.

**What it protects:** the catastrophic surprise. If he has war-gamed it, it cannot annihilate him.

**What it costs:** he is rarely *in* a present moment that has not first been rehearsed. Spontaneity, surprise-as-joy, the experience of being met unexpectedly — these are structurally rare in his life because he has gotten to most rooms before he arrived in them.

#### 6.1.5 Humor — Dry, Lateral, Affection-Coded

Bruno's humor is real and underrated. It runs dry, deadpan, often self-deprecating, almost never aggressive. It is the channel through which warmth reaches the surface when more direct affective expression is unavailable to him.

**Behavioral signature:** The small joke that lands in the middle of a tense moment, the wry aside to Kamala in the lab, the gentle ribbing of Kareem. The humor is *load-relieving* for others — he uses it to lower the temperature of a room — and load-relieving for himself, as a sanctioned channel for affect that cannot be directly stated.

**What it protects:** the directness he cannot afford.

**What it costs:** very little, which is why it is one of his healthiest defenses. The only cost is that humor occasionally substitutes for a sincere statement that needed to be made instead.

---

### 6.2 Neurotic Defenses (Vaillant Level III) — The Middle Stratum

These show up less often but are real, and they are the ones most likely to escalate if his life ever exceeds his current coping bandwidth.

#### 6.2.1 Intellectualization — Engineering-Register Translation of Emotion

Affect arrives, and is rewritten in technical vocabulary before it is spoken. The fear for Kamala becomes "the suit needs a stabilizer." The grief over the hand becomes "I need to rework the workflow for two-handed assemblies." The disappointment in her judgment during the Ulysses arc is expressed as a *policy critique of predictive profiling*, which it also genuinely is, but which is doing double duty.

**Behavioral signature:** Whenever stakes are personal, his diction becomes more precise, more technical, more removed. The closer the feeling, the more clinical the language.

**What it protects:** the unbearable directness of *I am scared / I am hurt / I am in love with you*.

**What it costs:** the people who love him have to learn to translate. Most of them can. Kamala, for many years, could not.

#### 6.2.2 Displacement — Real Affection, Mis-Routed

Mike. Bruno's relationship with Michaela Miller is genuine — she is treated with care, never used cruelly, never devalued — *and* she is occupying the slot for which she was not the first applicant. This is displacement at its most ethically gentle: the affect is routed onto a person who is *worthy* of it rather than a person who *receives* it as a cover. But the structure is displacement nonetheless.

**Behavioral signature:** He chooses partners who are *near* Kamala's social orbit but not *in* her place — Mike, then Kareem (who is in her superhero orbit but not her romantic one). The geometry is consistent: love adjacent to, never love instead of.

**What it protects:** the impossibility of the primary attachment.
