**What it costs:** Mike, somewhat. Kareem, less so. Himself, structurally — he has not yet had a relationship in which he was the first choice of his own first choice.

#### 6.2.3 Reaction Formation — Mild, Episodic

Less central, but present. When his hurt at Kamala is at its highest — post-injury, pre-Wakanda — his outward posture toward her becomes *more solicitous, not less.* He is gentler with her in the period when he has the most reason to be cold. The over-correction is small enough that it could be mistaken for grace, but the pattern is recognizable: the warmth is calibrated upward in proportion to the suppressed grievance.

**What it protects:** the relationship from his own resentment.

**What it costs:** authenticity. Kamala loses access to the truth of what she has done to him, and therefore the chance to repair it.

#### 6.2.4 Isolation of Affect — Operational, Tactical

In a crisis, Bruno can put the feeling in one box and the action in another and operate the action box alone for as long as the crisis lasts. This is the field-medic version of intellectualization. It is genuinely useful in the missions; it is genuinely damaging when crisis durations stretch into years.

---

### 6.3 Immature Defenses (Vaillant Level II) — The Quiet Substrate

This is where the dossier finds the *non-obvious* material. Bruno does not present as immaturely defended, and most observers would stop at section 6.1. But the longitudinal record reveals several immature mechanisms that operate quietly and consistently.

#### 6.3.1 Geographic Flight — Acting-Out Dressed as Maturity

The Wakanda transfer. The official story is academic opportunity, and it is genuinely that. But the timing and the structure mark it as a more primitive defense than its respectable surface implies: when suppression and sublimation could no longer contain the post-injury, post-Kamala-rift affect, the system reached for *physical distance* as the regulator of last resort.

**Behavioral signature:** When a situation exceeds his defensive bandwidth, the solution is to remove his body from the situation rather than to alter his relationship to it. He does not fight for his place in the room. He leaves the room, very politely, and lets the room close behind him.

**What it protects:** the integrity of the suppressive system, which would have failed under sustained proximity to the unprocessed material.

**What it costs:** the relationships he leaves behind have to absorb the un-discussed reasons for his leaving. Kamala carries the Wakanda transfer as a wound she is not allowed to name.

#### 6.3.2 Passive Withdrawal as Anger Expression

Bruno does not get angry. This is *not the same as* not having anger. The anger exists; it is metabolized internally and emerges only as *distance*. The reduction in availability, the lengthening of response times, the polite-but-shorter visits — these are the signal. A handler with no record of his prior baseline would not see it as hostility. A handler with the longitudinal record sees it clearly.

**Behavioral signature:** Post-rupture, the warmth does not turn cold — it turns *measured*. He does not stop being kind. He stops being *eager*. The eagerness was always the giveaway of full presence; its absence is the anger.

**What it protects:** the self-concept of *not being someone who lashes out*.

**What it costs:** the other party never gets a clean confrontation that could be repaired. They get a quiet attenuation that cannot be addressed because it has never been named.

#### 6.3.3 Somatization — Minor, Sleep-Channeled

Affect that cannot exit through speech or technical channel exits through the body in low-grade ways: chronic sleep curtailment (the bags under the eyes drawn consistently by multiple artists), the late hours alone in the back room, the body kept on a schedule that no adolescent body should be on. This is not florid somatization; it is the body holding the load the language will not.

#### 6.3.4 Idealization — Of the Cared-For Object

Of Kamala, especially in early years. He sees her — accurately — as extraordinary; he also, defensively, organizes himself around her extraordinariness in a way that justifies the asymmetry of the relationship. *Of course* he is the one who gives more; she is the one who matters more. This is the parentified child's bargain re-staged in adolescence: the asymmetry is acceptable because the other is special enough to warrant it.

The Ulysses arc is the moment idealization fails. Kamala, for the first time, makes a serious ethical mistake that he cannot rationalize. The defense cracks; the hand injury occurs in the structural space where the idealization used to be.

---

### 6.4 Compensatory Mechanisms — Positive

These are not defenses against material; they are *constructive structures* he has built on top of the defended substrate, and they are the reason the file does not read as a tragedy.

- **Genuine scientific vocation.** The technical work is sublimation, yes, *and* it is real. He loves it. The vocation outlives the defensive function and provides an autonomous source of meaning that does not depend on any particular relationship.

- **Capacity for new attachment.** Kareem. The fact that Bruno can, after the Kamala wound, form a real and unguarded bond is the single strongest indicator that his attachment system is healthy at the root. A more damaged person would have shut the system down. He moved it.

- **Ethical practice as identity scaffold.** His principled stance on the Ulysses matter, his refusal of utilitarian shortcuts, his quiet deontology — these constitute a *self that is not derived from being needed*. They are an island of identity that the parentification did not eat.

- **Capacity to forgive without erasing.** He does not punish Kamala. He also does not pretend the injury did not happen. The forgiveness is *real and accurate*, which is rare.

- **Humor as relational glue.** Already discussed; it is also a compensatory structure, because it gives him a sanctioned mode of warmth that does not require him to make the larger asks he cannot make.

- **Mentorable competence.** He can be taught, and he can teach. In Wakanda, in later mutant-era arcs, he occupies the role of *the one the room can rely on technically*, and that role is a stable platform from which he draws genuine self-respect.

---

### 6.5 Compensatory Mechanisms — Negative

The shadow of 6.4. These are the structures that look like coping but, on long observation, are *load-bearing in the wrong direction*.

- **Self-erasure as virtue.** He has built a self-concept in which the suppression of his own bid is *good character*. This is the most dangerous compensatory structure in the file, because it converts pathology into ethics and therefore immunizes it against revision.

- **Conflict avoidance dressed as maturity.** Many of the moments where he "kept the peace" were moments where the peace needed to be broken. The maturity-coding of his avoidance has cost him — and the people who love him — several necessary confrontations.

- **Reliability as identity-prison.** The fact that he can always be counted on has become the fact that he can never be the one who *cannot* be counted on. There is no exit ramp from the role. Any failure of reliability would be experienced — by him, internally — as a failure of self.

- **Retreat as solution to relational rupture.** The Wakanda pattern, generalized. Whenever a relationship becomes structurally untenable, the move is to relocate rather than to repair. This works once or twice. It does not scale.

- **The unspoken ledger.** He keeps no explicit accounting of what he is owed — and this is precisely the problem. An explicit ledger could be settled. The implicit one accumulates without limit because it has no surface on which entries can be made or struck.

- **Adaptation-as-grief-substitute.** Post-injury, his rapid adaptation to one-handed work has been read by everyone, including probably himself, as resilience. It is also a way of *not grieving the hand*. The grief is owed and has not been paid. The adaptation is real and the grief is also real and the first does not discharge the second.

---

### 6.6 Defenses Ranked by Primitiveness

From most mature to most primitive, with frequency of deployment in parentheses (H = high, M = moderate, L = low):

1. **Sublimation** (H) — mature, primary, identity-constitutive.
2. **Humor** (H) — mature, healthy, low-cost.
3. **Anticipation** (H) — mature, structural.
4. **Altruism** (H) — mature on surface, defensive in function.
5. **Suppression** (H) — mature when episodic, corrosive when chronic; in Bruno, chronic.
6. **Intellectualization** (M) — neurotic, engineering-register translation.
7. **Isolation of affect** (M) — neurotic, tactically useful.
8. **Displacement** (M, romantic domain) — neurotic, ethically gentle in execution.
9. **Reaction formation** (L) — neurotic, mild, episodic.
10. **Idealization** (M, of Kamala specifically) — borderline neurotic/immature.
11. **Passive withdrawal as anger channel** (M) — immature, quietly destructive.
12. **Geographic flight** (L, but consequential when deployed) — immature, dressed as mature.
13. **Somatization** (L, sleep-channeled) — immature, low-grade.

Notably absent: denial, projection, splitting, acting-out (in any aggressive register), projective identification, psychotic distortion. The entire pathological tier (Level I) is empty. This is rare and load-bearing for the overall assessment.

---

### 6.7 Synthesis — How the Architecture Holds, and Where It Will Fail

The defensive system as a whole is *engineered for one operating condition*: a high steady load, borne alone, in service of others, with no permission to exceed his own design tolerances. Under that condition it performs extraordinarily well, which is why no one — including him — has ever flagged it for service.

It will fail under any of three conditions, none of which have yet been sustained long enough to break it:

1. **Catastrophic loss of the technical channel.** The hand was a warning shot. A second, larger insult to his capacity to *make things* would remove the primary sublimative outlet and force the suppressed material into a system not built to process it.

2. **A relationship in which he is the one being asked for, not the one asking nothing.** He has no rehearsed protocol for being the object of sustained care. A partner or community that loved him *first*, persistently, and refused to let him convert that love into a debt would either remake him or break the defensive architecture. Either outcome would be, on net, good for him and acutely painful in the transition.

3. **A demand that he choose himself over a person who needs him.** Every defense in the stack is calibrated to make this choice unnecessary. Forced to make it explicitly, the system has no precedent, no protocol, and no rehearsed answer.

The handler's note, then, is not that he is fragile — he is not — but that his strength has a specific shape, and the shape has a seam. He has been the steady one since he was a child. The defenses that made that possible are the same defenses that have ensured no one, ever, has had to be the steady one for him. That asymmetry is not stable forever. The file should be read with the awareness that the most important entry in it has not yet been written.


## Longitudinal Psychological Profile

# LONGITUDINAL PSYCHOLOGICAL PROFILE — BRUNO CARRELLI

**Compiler's note.** The following decomposes Subject's interior architecture into successive developmental strata, each anchored to canonical episodes and read through standard clinical frameworks (attachment theory per Bowlby/Main; defense maturity per Vaillant; affect regulation per Gross; self-concept per Higgins's self-discrepancy model; interpersonal circumplex per Wiggins/Kiesler; trait structure per Five-Factor). The aim is not to re-litigate the diagnostic findings of §§3–4 but to chart the *motion* of those structures — what shifted, what calcified, what was lost.

---

## I. PRE-OBSERVATION SUBSTRATE (c. 2000s – early 2014): The Parentified Child

The dossier inherits Subject already-formed. By *Ms. Marvel* (2014) #1 he is approximately sixteen, has been on the Circle Q payroll since middle school, and is functionally the household's executive. This means the foundational psychological work — the cementing of self-concept around *usefulness* — is complete before the surveillance window opens. We can only reverse-infer.

**Affect regulation, inferred baseline.** A child placed in instrumental-caregiver roles before age twelve develops what Schore and Siegel describe as *premature right-hemisphere down-regulation* — the capacity to dampen one's own distress in order to remain available to a dysregulated other. Bruno's adolescent presentation (low expressivity, high containment, an almost preternatural absence of adolescent volatility) is consistent with this etiology. He did not learn affect modulation gradually through the normal teenage gauntlet; he learned it early, under load, as a survival skill for Vick's chaos and the household's financial fragility.

**Cognitive style, inferred baseline.** Convergent and instrumental from the start. The child who can fix the thing is rewarded; the child who can name the feeling is not. This trains an early bias toward *problem-as-system* over *problem-as-feeling*. By 2014 this is fully integrated: when Kamala first transforms in front of him, his response is diagnostic ("Are you okay?") rather than affective (no startle, no awe, no fear-display).

**Self-concept, inferred baseline.** Already organized around *capacity* rather than *being*. The Higgins ought-self (who he must be to be loved/safe) and actual-self (who he is) have been welded together by environmental demand; there is no detectable gap to motivate guilt, and equally little ideal-self (who he wishes to be) visible above the ought-line. He does not appear to have adolescent fantasies of escape, glory, or alternative life — a striking absence that will matter later.

---

## II. ERA ONE (2014–2015, Wilson early run): Sublimation in Steady State

This is Bruno's psychological apex — the period in which his structure and his circumstance are best matched.

**Affect regulation.** Gross's process model distinguishes *antecedent-focused* strategies (situation selection, cognitive reappraisal) from *response-focused* (suppression). Early-era Bruno is dominated by reappraisal: he reframes Kamala's chaos as opportunity for craft, Vick's mischief as solvable logistics, his own romantic frustration as background noise to a friendship worth more. Suppression is present but not yet load-bearing. The system is in homeostasis.

Micro-evidence: the consistent flat-affect competence under tactical stress (the Inventor warehouse approach, Ms. Marvel #10–11), juxtaposed against genuine laughter and warmth in low-stakes scenes at Circle Q. He can *modulate* in both directions in this era. That bidirectional capacity will degrade.

**Cognitive style.** Pattern-recognition is the dominant mode. Bruno notices Vick's evasions before they are stated, the Inventor's child-labor architecture before the heroes name it, the rough physics of Kamala's polymorph powers before she does. He is the first to articulate what is *actually happening*. Crucially, in this era he *speaks his analyses* — to Kamala, to himself, to whoever will listen. He has not yet learned that being right out loud has costs.

**Self-concept.** Stable, narrow, functional. He is *the one who makes it work*. The narrowness has not yet been tested by a circumstance in which making-it-work is impossible. Self-esteem is high in the technical-instrumental domain and unexamined in the relational-affective domain. He has not asked himself whether he is loved; he has only asked whether he is useful, and the answer keeps coming back yes.

**Attachment posture, this era.** Best characterized as *earned-secure trending dismissive under threat*. Bonds are real and warm (Kamala, Nakia, Vick). The dismissive vector emerges only when his own *bid* would be required — most visibly in the consistent failure to disclose romantic feelings to Kamala. The bond is preserved by suppressing the bid; the suppression is, in this era, ego-syntonic and unconscious.

**Defense profile (Vaillant).** Mature-dominant: sublimation (engineering channels longing), altruism (helping is genuine), anticipation (he plans). Neurotic accessory: displacement, beginning to surface around Mike. No primitive defenses observable.

---

## III. ERA TWO (2015–2016, Wilson mid-run through Vick arc into Civil War II): Structural Stress and the First Crack

This is the period in which Bruno's structure is asked to do work it was not designed for.

**Affect regulation under accumulating load.** The Vick rescue arc (*Ms. Marvel* 2014 #8–11) represents the first time Bruno's family-shame containment and his heroic-infrastructure role *compete* rather than complement. He chooses concealment over disclosure to Kamala, then near-dies retrieving Vick. The cost is metabolized silently. Post-Vick scenes show no narrative grief, no debrief, no relational repair-work; Bruno simply *returns to baseline operations*. This is the first observable instance of what will become the dominant pattern: **using the next task to skip the processing of the last one.**

Suppression begins, in this era, to overtake reappraisal as the workhorse strategy. The system is still functioning, but it is doing so on response-focused regulation, which Gross's empirical work consistently shows produces somatic and relational cost over time (elevated sympathetic load, reduced positive affect in close relationships, diminished memory for emotional events). All three are subsequently observable in Bruno.

**Cognitive style hardening.** His pattern-recognition becomes increasingly *anticipatory* and *protective*. He is no longer just naming what is; he is gaming out what could go wrong. The Ulysses/profiling critique (early CWII tie-ins) is the apex of this: he reads the second- and third-order ethical consequences of predictive policing before Kamala has digested the first-order utility. He articulates these clearly, repeatedly, and at increasing relational cost. He is *correct and unheeded*, a position that, prolonged, reshapes a cognitive style toward either cynicism or withdrawal. In Bruno: withdrawal.

**Self-concept under first sustained doubt.** The Mike relationship — entered into with real affection, but with the romantic substrate displaced from Kamala — introduces a small but real discrepancy between actual-self (a boy in love with one girl, dating another) and ought-self (a person of integrity). He manages the discrepancy by treating Mike well, which is ethically real and psychologically insufficient. The discrepancy is held, not resolved.

**The injury (CWII, late 2015 publication, 2016 in-story).** The hand. The single most psychologically consequential event in the longitudinal record.

To understand its impact requires noting what was *struck*: not merely a limb, but the *organ of his self-concept*. Bruno's identity is load-bearing on his hands. Engineering, soldering, lab work, the bespoke fabrication that makes him useful to Kamala — all routed through fine motor control in the dominant hand. The injury did not damage a peripheral asset; it cratered the foundation.

The clinical question is why this did not produce post-traumatic symptomatology. The answer, on the evidence, is that Bruno *did not process the injury as trauma*. He processed it as *information*: as data about the cost of being right, the cost of loving Kamala, the cost of his position. The PTSD criteria require intrusion, avoidance, negative cognitions, hyperarousal; Bruno shows none. What he shows instead is **integrated narrative reorganization** — a silent revision of the operating assumptions of his life. He does not relive the warehouse; he simply *concludes things* about it, and acts on those conclusions.

This is, in attachment terms, the moment the dismissive-avoidant features stop being situational and start becoming structural.

---

## IV. ERA THREE (2017, Wakanda transfer): Geographic Flight as Defense

**Affect regulation in collapse-and-rebuild.** The Wakanda decision is, on its face, mature: an academic opportunity, a developmental step, a healthy environmental change. Substructurally it is *flight* — the most primitive viable response, dressed in the most mature available clothing. Bruno could not stay in the room with the configuration of Kamala-plus-his-hand-plus-his-displaced-feelings-plus-his-family-load. So he did not stay in the room. He left the country.

This is diagnostically important not because flight was the wrong choice (it was probably the right one) but because of *how it was executed*: with no observable relational processing, no explicit naming of his reasons to Kamala, no negotiation of the friendship's terms before departure. He simply *converted the problem into a logistics problem* and solved it. The pattern is consistent: when the affective load cannot be metabolized in place, Bruno changes places.

**Cognitive style in transition.** A productive change: exposure to Wakandan science culture appears to broaden his cognitive range. He gains, on the evidence of later issues, more *systems-level* fluency (not just gadget-craft but research-program thinking). The injury that destroyed certain manual capacities forced a partial migration upward into design-and-direction, and Wakanda accelerates this. There is real growth here.

**Self-concept in reconstruction.** The Wakanda period is the first time Bruno's worth is *not* exclusively transacted through Kamala. He is a student among students, evaluated on merit rather than on his utility to a single beloved chaotic person. Kareem (Red Dagger) becomes a relationship in which Bruno is *chosen* rather than *needed*, which is a different psychological vitamin entirely. Limited evidence, but what evidence exists suggests this is the period in which an ideal-self first becomes detectable — a faint outline of a Bruno who is a scientist, a partner, a person in his own frame.

**Attachment, this era.** The Kareem bond suggests retained capacity for warm primary attachment outside the Kamala system. This is critical evidence against any diagnosis of avoidant PD: the avoidant architecture is *specific to the Kamala-system*, not general. With Kareem, in a context not pre-loaded with rescuer-debt, Bruno can apparently *receive* care, not only deliver it.

**Defense profile evolution.** Sublimation remains dominant. Suppression now load-bearing rather than accessory. Geographic flight, used once, available as a precedent. Altruism continues, but with a slightly more bounded radius. The defensive system has not regressed; it has *thickened*.

---

## V. ERA FOUR (2019–present, Ahmed/Saladin and successors): The Professionalized Friend

**Affect regulation in steady state, post-rebuild.** The Bruno of *Magnificent Ms. Marvel* and successor runs is observably *flatter* than the Bruno of 2014 — less bidirectional, less prone to spontaneous warmth-display, more reliably modulated toward the low-affect mean. He is not depressed; he is *contained*. The container has thickened over years of use.

Suppression has become the default rather than the exception. He no longer needs to actively shelve affect; the shelving is automatic. This is efficient and costly — efficient in that he is never visibly destabilized, costly in that the affective bandwidth available to his relationships is narrower. He gives less of himself away, because there is less surface area exposed.

**Cognitive style in maturity.** He has become the *adult-coded* node in any room — including rooms containing literal X-Men. The pattern recognition is now married to a kind of weary realism: he *expects* the worst-case branches to be live, and he plans for them. He is, in this era, what an intelligence service would call a *good operations officer*: someone who runs the scenarios, builds the contingencies, and does not require his judgments to be ratified to remain confident in them.

This is growth and it is scar tissue. The early Bruno spoke his analyses. The later Bruno often does not bother — not from contempt but from triage. He says what is necessary and keeps the rest. The Ulysses arc taught him that being right out loud is sometimes costly to the people he was trying to protect. He learned.

**Self-concept in its mature form.** The post-Wakanda Bruno has a *broader* self-concept than the pre-injury Bruno — he is a scientist, a partner, a friend, a brother, a professional. He is no longer solely *Kamala's infrastructure*. This is real expansion. But the *organizing principle* of the self-concept — worth-through-usefulness — has not changed. It has only diversified its objects. He is now useful to more people, in more ways, and his self-esteem accordingly is sourced from a more resilient portfolio. The structure is the same; the load is better distributed.

The unresolved question, the one that surfaces in no on-page dialogue but is legible in his posture: *who is Bruno when nobody needs anything from him?* The evidence is that this condition has not been allowed to obtain for any sustained period since approximately age ten. The self has never been tested in vacuum.

**Attachment, present era.** Bruno's attachment system in this period is best described as *plural and bounded*. He maintains multiple stable bonds (Kamala as friend, Kareem in whatever its current configuration, Vick as ongoing fraternal project, peer scientists). None is permitted to occupy the totalizing position the early Kamala-bond did. This is an explicit, if unstated, defensive correction: he has decentralized his attachment portfolio so that no single rupture can cost him his hand again.

**Defense profile in maturity.** Sublimation remains primary and healthy. Suppression is now the silent autonomic ground state. Altruism is more measured — bounded by capacity rather than performed unboundedly. Geographic flight remains in the toolkit but has not been redeployed; the Wakanda precedent appears to have *substituted* for needing to flee again, by way of demonstrating that he can. Intellectualization has slightly increased, particularly around the hand and around Kamala. Displacement has largely retired (the Mike-era machinery is unnecessary now that the romantic substrate with Kamala has been quietly buried).

No primitive defenses (splitting, projection, acting-out) have appeared at any point in the longitudinal record. This is, frankly, anomalous in a subject who has sustained the losses he has sustained, and is the strongest evidence for the underlying temperamental endowment posited in §4: high conscientiousness, high agreeableness, high cognitive control, moderate-to-high neuroticism that is *managed* rather than expressed.

---

## VI. CROSS-CUTTING TRAJECTORIES

**The affect bandwidth curve.** Wide and bidirectional in 2014; narrowing and downward-skewed by 2016; flattening into mature containment by 2019. The total *range* has decreased; the *stability* has increased. Net psychological wellness is approximately preserved; net relational richness has declined modestly.

**The voicing curve.** In 2014 Bruno speaks his analyses freely. By 2016 he has been punished (relationally and somatically) for doing so. By 2019 he speaks what is necessary and edits the rest. This is a wisdom-arc and a silencing-arc simultaneously.

**The body-as-instrument curve.** Bruno's body has been used — by his family, by the plot, by Kamala's missions, by his own self-sacrificing dispositions — with steadily decreasing self-protection through 2016, after which a partial corrective sets in. He no longer volunteers his body the way he did. The hand was a teacher.

**The self-disclosure curve.** Monotonically downward across the entire record. The teenage Bruno of 2014 was already low-disclosing; the present Bruno is lower still. He has *more* interior life than he had at sixteen and *less* of it is visible to others. This is the costliest of the trajectories and the one most likely to produce eventual difficulty if not corrected.

**The reciprocity curve.** Lopsided throughout but with measurable improvement post-Wakanda. The Kareem relationship, peer scientific collaboration, and the more bounded later friendships all show greater two-way flow than the early Kamala-system did. He has *learned* to receive in some contexts. He has not generalized this fully.

---

## VII. PROGNOSTIC INFERENCE

Bruno Carrelli at the present observation point is psychologically well-functioning, structurally stable, and operating on a defense architecture that is mature, efficient, and slowly accruing cost. The cost is paid in affective bandwidth, self-disclosure, and the un-grieved residue of injuries that were integrated without being mourned. None of this meets diagnostic threshold; all of it is legible across the longitudinal record.

The forward-looking concern is straightforward and was named in the synthesis: **what happens to a person whose reliability has never been allowed to fail.** Bruno's system has been tested by acute stressors (Vick, the hand, the Wakanda decision) and proven sound. It has not been tested by the chronic stressor that most often unmasks subjects of his architecture: *the slow erosion of being needed*. If Kamala's world continues to expand and Bruno's instrumental centrality continues to diffuse, the question of who he is in the absence of demand will eventually be asked of him by circumstance. He has, on the present evidence, no rehearsed answer.

This is not pathology. It is the predictable shape of a life built on premature competence. The dossier flags it not as a problem to be solved but as a horizon to be watched.


## Psychiatric Assessment & Differential

# PSYCHIATRIC ASSESSMENT & DIFFERENTIAL — SUBJECT: BRUNO CARRELLI

**File reference:** UATU/CARRELLI/§4 — expanded longitudinal psychiatric workup.
**Coverage window:** First on-page appearance (*Ms. Marvel* 2014 #1) through present continuity (Ahmed/Saladin/post-*New Mutant* era).
**Assessor's preface:** This section operates from the longitudinal observation record rather than from clinical interview. The subject has never, in any depicted continuity, sought or received psychiatric care; accordingly, every diagnostic statement below is *behavioral* and *inferential*. The remarkable headline of this section, and the finding around which it is organized, is that Bruno Carrelli — adolescent civilian embedded in a chronically violent operational theater, parentified since childhood, partially disabled in a high-stakes confrontation at sixteen — does not, on the longitudinal record, meet criteria for any DSM-5/ICD-11 disorder. That fact is itself diagnostically interesting and requires the rigorous accounting that follows.

---

## 1. Synoptic Diagnostic Statement

**Axis-style summary (heuristic, not DSM-5 formal):**

- **Principal current diagnosis:** None active. *No mental disorder, current.*
- **Historical / past-episode diagnosis (provisional):** Adjustment Disorder with Depressed Mood, chronic, single episode, in full remission (DSM-5 309.0 / ICD-11 6B43). Onset coincident with Civil War II injury and the romantic-relational rupture with K. Khan (mid-2016); duration approximately 6–14 months; remitted with environmental change (relocation to Wakanda) and formation of new attachment (Kareem / Red Dagger).
- **Trait/structural findings (sub-syndromal, characterological):** Parentified-child developmental profile with prominent self-sacrificing interpersonal organization; mature defensive style biased toward suppression, sublimation, and altruism; counterdependent overlay on a fundamentally secure attachment substrate.
- **Risk findings:** Low acute risk across domains (suicidality, violence to others, substance use, self-neglect). Chronic latent risk: catastrophic decompensation potential in the event of simultaneous loss of (a) technical competence and (b) primary attachment object — a low-probability, high-impact scenario discussed in §6.
- **Function:** GAF-analog estimate 80–88 across the longitudinal record, with a depressive trough estimated at 60–65 during the 2016–17 episode.

---

## 2. Diagnostic Workup — The Single Sustained Episode

### 2.1 Adjustment Disorder with Depressed Mood (provisional, historical)

The only window in the subject's published life that crosses any reasonable diagnostic threshold is the post–Civil War II interval running from the warehouse injury through the Wakanda transfer.

**Stressors (identifiable, multiple, concurrent):**
1. Permanent partial disability of the dominant hand — a body part on which his entire vocational and self-concept architecture is load-bearing.
2. Foreclosure of the romantic possibility with K. Khan, both because she was in another relationship and because the injury context made his romantic position structurally impossible to articulate without it reading as moral leverage.
3. Rupture of the operational confidant role — the secret-keeper/Oracle position he had occupied since *Ms. Marvel* #3 (2014) was no longer tenable on either side.
4. Loss of the daily-contact behavioral substrate (after-school Circle Q encounters, lab visits, late-night text loops).

**Symptoms in the window (behaviorally inferred):**
- Affective flattening, observable in posture and panel rendering (Miyazawa, late Wilson run): reduced facial expressivity, less eye contact, shoulders carried higher and forward.
- Withdrawal from previously reinforcing activities — he continues to work, but the work has lost its courtship/play quality (no more bespoke gadget-as-gift exchanges).
- Reduced verbal output, particularly in mixed company. Where pre-injury Bruno volunteered ethical readings, post-injury Bruno waits to be asked.
- Geographic flight ideation actualized into geographic flight (Wakanda).
- No evidence of anhedonia in the strict sense (he can still enjoy a problem, a meal, a conversation), no neurovegetative signs depicted (sleep already chronically curtailed at baseline, appetite not on-panel), no expressed hopelessness, no suicidal ideation.

**Why Adjustment Disorder and not Major Depression:** the symptom set is *reactive*, *proportionate-to-mild relative to the stressor stack*, *time-limited*, and *fully remitting on environmental change*. The depressive coloration never reaches the threshold of pervasive anhedonia, worthlessness ideation, or psychomotor change required for an MDD coding. He kept working. He kept eating. He kept being decent to the people in front of him. He just stopped reaching.

**Course and remission:** The Wakanda interval functions as a successful environmental intervention — change of setting, change of vocational stimulus (advanced science academy), removal of the comparative wound (no daily reminder of pre-injury role with Kamala), and formation of a new dyadic attachment (Kareem). Remission is essentially complete by the time of his returns in *Magnificent Ms. Marvel*. Residual: a permanent recalibration of intimacy distance with the primary attachment object, which is *characterological adjustment* rather than persistent symptom.

**Specifier rationale:** "With depressed mood" rather than "with anxiety" or "mixed" — the dominant affective coloration is *lowness and withdrawal*, not worry, not irritability, not panic. "Chronic" because duration exceeds six months. "Single episode, in full remission" because no recurrence is evident in subsequent continuity, including under significant subsequent stressors (Kamala's apparent death and resurrection arc).

### 2.2 Why nothing else, ever

Across roughly a decade of continuous on-panel observation in a theater that includes multiple kidnappings, beatings, threats of death, the apparent death of his primary attachment, the chronic instability of his sibling, the financial fragility of his family, and the daily psychological asymmetry of unrequited love for the person whose secret he keeps — Bruno Carrelli produces no other diagnosable syndrome. This is the analytic puzzle. The remainder of this section is structured to honor it.

---

## 3. Trait-Level and Developmental Findings (Sub-Syndromal)

These are *characterological structures* — stable, ego-syntonic, not in themselves disorders. They are recorded here because they organize the differential and because, in aggregate, they are the explanation for the relative absence of overt pathology.

### 3.1 Parentified-Child Developmental Profile

Not a DSM-5 diagnosis; well-described in developmental and family-systems literature (Boszormenyi-Nagy; Jurkovic). Bruno meets the descriptive profile on every available marker:

- **Premature competence:** working a register and managing inventory at the Circle Q since middle school; functional fluency in adult tasks (vendor relations, cash reconciliation, sibling supervision) by mid-adolescence.
- **Role-reversal with sibling:** Vick is parented *by Bruno* on the operational record — Bruno is the one called when Vick is in trouble, Bruno is the one who conceals Vick's involvement with the Inventor's cell, Bruno is the one who goes to retrieve him.
- **Hyper-responsibility for adult-stratum problems:** family finances, family reputation, family safety — Bruno carries all three without expressing the load.
- **Difficulty being a recipient of care:** he tolerates being thanked but does not solicit it; he does not narrate fear; he does not bring his injury into emotional currency with anyone, including Kamala, including Kareem.
- **Idealization of the cared-for object:** Kamala is, throughout the early Wilson run, treated as both the object of romantic longing and the object of *moral admiration that justifies his subordination of his own claim*. This is the parentified child's classic affective economy.

### 3.2 Self-Sacrificing / Counterdependent Interpersonal Pattern

Tracks the Millon "self-defeating" / Horney "moving-toward-with-counterdependent-defense" descriptions. Bruno organizes intimacy by **providing** rather than **requesting**, and converts incoming care into outgoing debt-discharge as fast as the social grammar allows. Critically, this is *not* the masochistic variant — he derives no satisfaction from being mistreated, he does not seek out exploitative partners (Mike and Kareem are conspicuously kind people), and he exits situations that destroy him (Wakanda decision). It is the *functional* end of the spectrum: a person whose identity equilibrium requires that he be the giver, and who experiences being the receiver as low-grade dysregulating.

### 3.3 Defensive Architecture (Vaillant Hierarchy)

Predominantly **mature-defense** profile — sublimation, altruism, suppression, anticipation, humor — with a single recurrent **neurotic-tier** intrusion (displacement, in the Mike relationship) and one **immature-tier** episode (the Wakanda flight, which is mature-coded by its academic packaging but is functionally a geographic dissociation from an intolerable relational field). The mature-skew is what protects him from syndromal illness. The chronic over-reliance on suppression is what produces the long-arc cost.

---

## 4. Differential Diagnosis — Rigorous Exclusion

This is the section that requires the most discipline, because Bruno's presentation *brushes against* several diagnoses and a less careful read could over-pathologize. Each candidate is named, the surface resemblance is honored, and the disqualifying evidence is cited.

### 4.1 Major Depressive Disorder — **EXCLUDED**

**Surface resemblance:** post-CWII withdrawal, affective flattening, reduced spontaneous engagement, geographic flight.
**Disqualifying evidence:** No depicted anhedonia of pervasive scope (work, food, conversation, new relationship-formation all retained); no expressed worthlessness or excessive guilt of the depressive type (his guilt is *situation-specific and proportionate*, not the diffuse self-condemnation of MDD); no suicidal ideation, plan, intent, or behavior across continuity; no neurovegetative cluster (no depicted hypersomnia, no appetite disturbance, no psychomotor agitation/retardation); duration of low mood tightly coupled to identifiable stressor stack with full remission on environmental change. **Adjustment disorder fits the pattern; MDD does not.**

### 4.2 Persistent Depressive Disorder (Dysthymia) — **EXCLUDED**

**Surface resemblance:** low-key affect, low expressivity, "the steady one" stoicism could be mistaken for chronic dysthymic baseline.
**Disqualifying evidence:** Bruno's baseline affect is *low-arousal and contained*, not *low-valence*. He smiles in early continuity; he is dryly funny; he engages with humor, curiosity, romantic interest. The flatness is *trained containment* not *depressive coloration*. Pre-injury Bruno is plainly *happy* in the operational sense — happy at the workbench, happy with Kamala in proximity, happy when a build comes together. PDD requires two years of depressed mood more days than not; the record does not show this.

### 4.3 Generalized Anxiety Disorder — **EXCLUDED**

**Surface resemblance:** chronic vigilance, planning-ahead behaviors, frequent risk-assessment of Kamala's choices.
**Disqualifying evidence:** Vigilance is *target-locked and operationally appropriate* — he is anxious about real, identifiable, present-tense risks (Vick's safety, Kamala's tactical errors, family finances), not generalized free-floating worry. He does not present somatic anxiety symptoms (muscle tension, GI distress, sleep onset insomnia from worry rather than from labor). When the threat resolves, the vigilance stands down. GAA requires excess and pervasiveness untethered from realistic stakes; Bruno's stakes are catastrophically real and his worry sizes to them.

### 4.4 Panic Disorder / Phobic Disorders — **EXCLUDED**

No depicted panic attacks. No depicted phobic avoidance. He has returned to laboratory work post-injury without trauma-cued avoidance; he re-enters operational theaters with Kamala without phobic reaction.

### 4.5 Social Anxiety Disorder — **EXCLUDED**

He is quiet but not socially fearful. He has worked customer-facing retail since middle school; he confronts Zoe Zimmer in *Ms. Marvel* #1; he engages strangers in operational contexts; he formed a romantic relationship with Mike and another with Kareem. The reticence is *selective and choice-driven*, not anxiogenic.

### 4.6 Post-Traumatic Stress Disorder — **EXCLUDED**

**Surface resemblance:** Civil War II injury is a Criterion A event by reasonable construal; subsequent affective change; geographic relocation; some attenuation of pre-injury affect with Kamala.
**Disqualifying evidence:** No depicted intrusion symptoms (no flashbacks, no nightmares on-panel, no intrusive ideation referenced in dialogue); no avoidance of trauma-linked stimuli (he returns *immediately* to laboratory work and to weapons-adjacent engineering, the very contexts most associated with the injury); no negative alterations in cognition/mood of the PTSD type (no persistent negative beliefs about self/world, no estrangement from others — he in fact *forms* new attachments); no hyperarousal (no exaggerated startle, no hypervigilance disproportionate to context, no irritable outbursts). The injury was *integrated* into a continuous self-narrative rather than *encapsulated* as an unprocessable shard. This is its own kind of suppression and is not without cost, but it is not PTSD.

### 4.7 Complex PTSD (ICD-11 6B41) — **CONSIDERED, EXCLUDED**

**Surface resemblance:** chronic developmental load (parentification, family fragility), repeated subordination to others' need, single discrete trauma overlaid on chronic micro-trauma.
**Disqualifying evidence:** CPTSD requires the core PTSD criteria *plus* the disturbances in self-organization triad — pervasive affect dysregulation, negative self-concept, and interpersonal disturbance. Bruno's affect regulation is *over-regulated, not under-regulated*. His self-concept is *modest but not negative* — he believes he is useful and ethically serious, and the record supports him. His interpersonal pattern is asymmetric but not avoidant or chaotic; he sustains close bonds, forms new ones, and is liked. CPTSD is not the right shape.

### 4.8 Avoidant Personality Disorder — **EXCLUDED**

**Surface resemblance:** post-CWII relational withdrawal, geographic flight, lifelong reticence about own needs.
**Disqualifying evidence:** AvPD is governed by *fear of rejection and feelings of inadequacy* leading to social inhibition. Bruno is not inhibited (works retail, organizes, leads in lab settings) and does not present feelings of inadequacy (he correctly perceives his competence). His withdrawal is *deferral of his own claim to protect the other's situation*, not *fear of being judged by the other*. The motivational engine is wrong for AvPD.

### 4.9 Dependent Personality Disorder — **EXCLUDED**

**Surface resemblance:** orientation around the needs of others, difficulty being alone in early continuity (he gravitates to Kamala's orbit).
**Disqualifying evidence:** DPD is defined by *needing others to assume responsibility* for one's life. Bruno does the opposite — he assumes responsibility for *others'* lives, makes autonomous major decisions (Wakanda is decided by him, not for him), and tolerates solitude (works alone in the back room without distress). DPD is the *photographic negative* of his actual pattern, not its diagnosis.

### 4.10 Obsessive-Compulsive Personality Disorder — **EXCLUDED**

**Surface resemblance:** technical precision, ethical principle, conscientiousness, reliability.
**Disqualifying evidence:** OCPD requires rigidity and stubbornness, preoccupation with order to the exclusion of efficiency, inability to delegate, and difficulty with the affective expressiveness of others. Bruno is *precise* but *flexible* — he tolerates Kamala's chaos with affectionate humor rather than distress; he adapts engineering plans on the fly; he delegates lab tasks post-injury without depicted rigidity-distress. He is a conscientious worker, not an obsessional character.

### 4.11 Obsessive-Compulsive Disorder (Axis I) — **EXCLUDED**

No depicted obsessions, no depicted compulsions, no ritualized behavior beyond the situation-appropriate routines of retail and laboratory work.

### 4.12 Schizoid Personality Disorder — **EXCLUDED**

**Surface resemblance:** low expressivity, contained affect, comfort with solitary work.
**Disqualifying evidence:** Schizoid presentation requires *absence of desire for close relationships and limited capacity for pleasure*. Bruno *desires* close relationships intensely (the entire Kamala arc is a record of this) and experiences pleasure from work, food, friendship, and romance. He is contained, not detached.

### 4.13 Autism Spectrum (Level 1) — **CONSIDERED, NOT SUPPORTED**

A reasonable lay reading might note: technical orientation, restraint, parsimony of language, comfort at the bench. But the evidence does not support ASD criteria. Bruno's *social cognition* is acute — he reads Kamala's mood, Zoe's social signaling, Vick's manipulations, room dynamics generally — at a level that exceeds neurotypical adolescent baseline. His communication is *spare but pragmatically calibrated*, not pragmatically atypical. He does not present restricted/repetitive interests in the ASD sense (his interests are broad and contextually responsive); no sensory sensitivities are depicted; reciprocity is intact. The trait overlap is surface; the structural criteria are absent.

### 4.14 Substance Use Disorders — **EXCLUDED**

No depicted use of any substance, prescription or otherwise. He is conspicuously the friend who is not drinking at the party. This is itself notable and is consistent with the parentified-child profile (vigilance set incompatible with intoxication).

### 4.15 Eating Disorder — **EXCLUDED**

No depicted disordered eating pattern. He is lean, plausibly under-nourished by adolescent-male standards, but this reads as the somatic correlate of long shifts and skipped meals rather than restriction-as-pathology.

### 4.16 Adjustment Disorder, recurrent — **CONSIDERED, NOT SUPPORTED**

The CWII episode is the only depicted episode meeting criteria. Subsequent significant stressors (Kamala's apparent death and resurrection; mutant-cohort entry into Kamala's orbit displacing him further; Wakanda re-entry and re-exit) do not produce repeat episodes. The 2016–17 episode appears to be a singular reactive event at a uniquely vulnerable convergence of developmental, romantic, somatic, and operational stressors.

---

## 5. Etiology — How a Person Who Should Be Diagnosable Isn't

The unusual finding (the absence of pathology in the presence of pathology-typical inputs) is explained by the convergence of three factors:

**(1) Temperamental endowment.** Bruno appears to sit at the upper end of Big Five conscientiousness and agreeableness, with above-average cognitive control and a high-functioning regulatory baseline. Whatever the genetic and prenatal substrate, he is constitutionally suited to *carrying load without breaking*. This is not a moral achievement; it is a starting condition. It is also the condition that makes parentification *survivable* for him where it would have produced overt syndromal illness in a less endowed child.

**(2) Successful sublimation track.** He had, from early adolescence, a *vocational channel* — engineering, repair, problem-solving — that absorbed and metabolized affect into product. Children with parentified-load and no sublimation channel decompensate; children with the channel often do not. Bruno's hands (literally) did the work of metabolizing what his voice was not permitted to say.

**(3) Real attachment availability.** Despite the family fragility, Bruno had genuine attachment objects — Kamala (asymmetric but real), the Khan family (warm and adoptive in posture toward him), Mike, eventually Kareem, ongoing relationship with Vick despite the latter's chaos. He was not attachment-starved. The bond economy was *uneven* but not *absent*, and the presence of any reliable warm object is the single strongest protective factor in the developmental literature.

**The cost ledger.** The absence of syndromal illness is bought with characterological self-erasure. The currency is real; it does not register on diagnostic instruments. What looks like wellness on the DSM is, on the longitudinal record, a person who has paid for his stability by *not asking*. That is not a disorder. It is, however, a fact about him that any handler should hold in view.

---

## 6. Comorbidity, Course, and Prospective Risk

**Comorbidity:** None active. The historical adjustment episode was uncomplicated by secondary substance use, secondary anxiety, or somatic-symptom amplification.

**Course over time:**
- *2014–early 2016 (pre-injury):* high function, high engagement, latent unrequited-love stressor managed by sublimation and displacement.
- *Mid-2016 through ~2017 (acute episode):* Adjustment Disorder with Depressed Mood, chronic course, partial remission within environmental change, full remission within new attachment formation.
- *2017–2019 (Wakanda interval and returns):* sustained remission; recalibration of primary attachment distance; emergent professional identity less dependent on Kamala-orbit.
- *2019–present (Ahmed/Saladin era):* stable, adult-coded function; sub-syndromal trait pattern unchanged; remains psychiatrically well.

**Prospective risk — low-probability, high-impact scenarios to watch:**

1. **Compound somatic loss.** Any future injury or illness compromising the *remaining* hand, vision, or cognitive precision would attack the same self-concept beam that the CWII injury hit. A second hit on that beam, without the buffering of new-attachment formation available the first time, could produce a more severe and less reactive depressive episode, with elevated suicide risk that the first episode did not show.

2. **Catastrophic loss of primary attachment without replacement.** A confirmed, permanent loss of K. Khan (and/or the Khan family) without the simultaneous availability of a new attachment object would remove the most-load-bearing element of his bond economy


## Behavioral Atlas

# UATU DOSSIER — SUBJECT: BRUNO CARRELLI
## SECTION 6 — BEHAVIORAL ATLAS

*An exhaustive catalogue of observable behavior across affective and operational conditions, drawn from longitudinal panel-by-panel observation (Wilson 2014–2019; Ahmed 2019–2020; Saladin 2021–present), supplemented by inference where the canon is silent but the pattern is overdetermined. The unifying behavioral signature throughout: **competence-forward, claim-suppressed, body-instrumentalized, exits taken quietly.** Each condition below is mapped against (a) postural tells, (b) verbal register, (c) hand and tool behavior, (d) social geometry, (e) decision heuristics.*

---

### 6.1 — BASELINE / CALM

This is the dominant observed state; Bruno spends more on-page minutes in a regulated baseline than virtually any peer in the Khan field, including Khan herself.

**Postural set.** Slight forward lean, weight distributed to the dominant foot (originally right, post-2016 shifted subtly to left as compensatory carriage developed alongside hand disuse). Shoulders rounded *down* rather than hunched *forward* — the carriage of someone whose habitual gaze is into a workbench, not whose head is dropped from shame. Head tilted approximately 10–15 degrees to the right when listening, especially to Khan; this tilt vanishes in formal/adult contexts (Wakandan faculty, hero-team briefings) where he sits squared and still. Eye contact is sustained but soft — long blinks, no challenge.

**Verbal register.** Low-volume, mid-cadence, Jersey-inflected but unaccented; sentence structure clean and complete even mid-task. Uses technical vocabulary precisely and without showing off — will downshift register for non-technical listeners without visible condescension. Humor is dry, observational, often self-deprecating; never barbed. Notable verbal tic: begins corrective sentences with *"Actually—"* but softens immediately with a second clause (*"actually, that — yeah, that would work, but the polymer can't take—"*). Speaks Khan's name more often than any other word in his recorded lexicon outside of technical nouns.

**Hand behavior.** Pre-injury: constant low-grade fidget with whatever is within reach — pen, screwdriver, the wire-bent stylus he kept clipped to the Circle Q register. Post-injury: the dominant hand rests, often held by the non-dominant at the wrist or in the lap; the fidget has migrated to the non-dominant hand alone, and it is markedly less elaborate. He will sometimes catch himself *almost* reaching for a tool with the right and redirect mid-motion to the left without comment. This redirection takes approximately a quarter-second and is invisible to anyone not looking for it.

**Social geometry.** Bruno positions himself at the *edge* of any gathering, not the center, but oriented inward — not exiting, witnessing. At Khan's family table he sits where he can see the kitchen door (functional vigilance, residue of long shifts behind a counter). In group conversations he is often the last to speak and almost never the first.

**Decision heuristic at baseline.** *Check feasibility, then ethics, then say something only if both are clear.* He will sit silent through a brainstorm and then, at the end, deliver the one sentence that reframes the problem. This pattern is consistent from issue #1 (2014) through the most recent appearances.

---

### 6.2 — UNDER LOW-GRADE STRESS (RUNNING LATE, DEADLINE, MILD INTERPERSONAL FRICTION)

**Postural shift.** Stiffening of the shoulders by perhaps half a degree; the head-tilt disappears. He squares to the task and *stops fidgeting*. Stillness, in Bruno, is the first stress sign — not motion. He becomes more, not less, organized; the back room of the Circle Q is observed to be cleaner under deadline than at rest.

**Verbal register.** Sentences shorten. He drops second-clause softeners. *"Actually, no, it has to be the other one,"* without the explanatory tail. He says *"okay"* as a self-directed reset word — quietly, to himself, before re-engaging.

**Hand behavior.** Pre-injury: faster tool-work, slightly bitten lower lip, fingers moving without visual supervision while eyes scan the schematic. Post-injury: he begins to *direct* hands rather than use his own — will hand a part to a peer with crisp instruction, narrating the sequence of motions he can no longer perform smoothly. This is a workaround presented as a teaching style; it functions as both.

**Social geometry.** Drifts toward solo work. If others are in the room he will physically angle himself ten or fifteen degrees away, opening a working envelope around himself without explicit ask. He does not say *"give me space."* He produces space.

**Decision heuristic.** *Triage by who else is depending on the outcome.* Bruno under low stress optimizes for the most exposed downstream party. He will sleep less rather than delegate, and will not announce the trade-off.

---

### 6.3 — UNDER ACUTE STRESS / THREAT TO KHAN OR LOVED ONE

This is the condition most exhaustively observed across the corpus. The pattern is exceptionally consistent.

**Postural set.** Bruno *moves toward* the source of threat, not away — but slowly, deliberately, with the gait of a person making a calculation, not making a charge. He is not impulsive. He is the one who walks into the warehouse because he has already modeled the inside of the warehouse. Hands visible, palms loosely open, the universal posture of *I am not the danger here.*

**Verbal register.** Drops by a full register in pitch and volume. Becomes briefer, almost monosyllabic with strangers, and with allies switches to imperative voice without softeners: *"Get behind the counter. Now."* The Jersey inflection thickens slightly under threat — a regression to baseline phonemes when the cortical brakes are loaded.

**Hand behavior.** Pre-injury, hands stayed in his pockets or near his sides — empty hands, signaling non-combatant status, even while his eyes were doing the threat assessment of a tactical analyst. Post-injury, the right hand goes consciously *behind* his back or into the pocket; he does not want it observed, partly because it is slow and partly because it is *his* and not for inspection. The left hand handles any object that needs handling.

**Social geometry.** Inserts his body *between* the threat and the more vulnerable party. This is the single most reliable behavior in the entire dossier — observed in the Inventor warehouse (#10–11, 2014), the Civil War II confrontation (the inflection-point injury itself), the Vick rescue, multiple lab incidents, and the New Mutant-era kidnapping scenarios. He does not announce that he is doing it. He simply ends up there.

**Decision heuristic.** *Absorb the cost yourself if the cost cannot be eliminated.* He calculates whether the situation can be defused; if it cannot, he positions for the body-as-shield outcome. He has never, in the entire record, asked another character to take his place in this calculation.

---

### 6.4 — UNDER THREAT TO SELF ONLY

A rarer condition; instructive precisely because the contrast is sharp.

**Postural set.** *Backs up.* Bruno is not a fighter and does not pretend to be. Hands raised, often verbal de-escalation attempted (*"Hey — hey, we don't have to—"*). The body that walks toward danger for Khan walks backward for itself.

**Verbal register.** Higher pitch than usual, more rapid, more hedging. Real fear is audible — and it is the one place fear is reliably audible in him. He cannot summon the same regulation for his own life that he summons for hers. This is diagnostic.

**Hand behavior.** Both hands up, palms out. The injured right is held a little lower than the left, protectively, almost cradled.

**Decision heuristic.** *Survive long enough to be useful again.* Bruno does not have a death wish; his self-sacrifice is purposive, not nihilistic. Threat to self without an attached protective function reads to him as *waste*, and he avoids waste in all domains.

---

### 6.5 — INTIMACY (ROMANTIC, FAMILIAL, FRIENDSHIP)

**With Khan (pre-injury).** Defaults to a posture of *attendance* — leaning toward her when she speaks, laughing a quarter-beat late because he is watching her face for the punchline before it lands. Touches are rare and instrumental (passing a tool, steadying her elbow during a stumble); a deliberate touch is freighted enough that an artist will frame it as a panel of its own. His default verbal mode with her is *gentle teasing carrying a covert technical note* — *"if you tried not to land on your shoulder maybe the seam wouldn't pop, just a thought."*

**With Khan (post-injury, post-Wakanda).** The lean is gone. He sits squared to her now, friendly, warm, but with a measurable physical envelope of two to three additional inches of distance. The teasing has not stopped but has thinned of its private register; the technical notes are now delivered as straightforward engineering feedback rather than as love-letters in disguise.

**With Mike.** Easy, mutual, unguarded — Bruno *can* do intimacy when the relational geometry is not pre-loaded with the rescuer-debt structure. He laughs more freely, sits closer, makes eye contact without the soft-blink dampening. He is, with Mike, visibly a teenager. This is one of the most important behavioral data points in the file: it proves the constraint with Khan is *role-derived*, not characterological.

**With Kareem.** Similar ease, with the additional register-shift of a person who has chosen a new geography and is performing the choice for himself. More tactile than with anyone else on record — Wakandan-era panels show casual hand-on-shoulder, walking-close behaviors absent from the Jersey corpus.

**With Vick.** The parental posture is unmistakable. Bruno *looms* over Vick the way an older sibling who has had to be a father does — slightly elevated chin, hands on hips or arms crossed, sigh-before-speaking. Verbal register with Vick is the only place Bruno will permit himself audible frustration (*"are you kidding me, Vick, are you actually—"*) and even there it is bounded, never sustained, and always followed by a re-stabilizing action (a meal made, a wound bandaged, a ride given).

**With his parents.** Notably minimal on-page evidence, which is itself the finding. He does not bring his parents into his social field. They are an offstage condition of his life, not a participating element of it.

**Decision heuristic in intimacy.** *Defer the bid; protect the bond.* This is the master rule, and it is broken only twice in the record — both times catastrophically (the failed confession at Civil War II; the Wakanda decision delivered as fait accompli rather than negotiated).

---

### 6.6 — GRIEF

Bruno does not grieve on-page in any conventional register. The behavior pattern in grief-conditions (the hand; Khan's apparent death in later arcs; the Wakanda departure as anticipatory loss; the rupture-of-easy-intimacy with Khan post-CWII) is uniform and worth cataloguing precisely:

**Postural set.** The same. This is the tell. A grieving Bruno looks exactly like a working Bruno except that the work is now slightly more deliberate and the breaks between tasks are slightly longer. He sits longer with a tool in hand without using it. He stares at the workbench rather than the schematic. There may be a single observed inhalation that is held a beat too long before exhale.

**Verbal register.** *Reduction.* He becomes the quietest version of himself. Questions get answered; nothing is volunteered. When pressed (rare), he produces a deflection in technical register: *"yeah, I'm just — I'm thinking about the resonator,"* when the resonator is not what he is thinking about.

**Hand behavior.** Post-injury especially: the injured hand is held more openly, examined more often when he believes no one is looking. He flexes it, watches the fingers respond imperfectly, and puts it back down. This is the closest thing to private mourning visible in the entire corpus.

**Social geometry.** Withdrawal. Not dramatic withdrawal — graduated. He skips one thing, then a second, then is found alone in the lab when he would previously have been at the table. The withdrawal is so courteously executed that it can take peers weeks of in-story time to notice.

**Decision heuristic.** *Convert grief into a project.* The Wakanda transfer is the canonical instance: an unspeakable loss (his hand, his place in Khan's primary orbit, his fantasy of being chosen) is metabolized into an application, an acceptance, a flight, a curriculum. The grief is *worked* rather than felt.

---

### 6.7 — VICTORY / SUCCESS

The most under-developed register in his behavioral repertoire, which is significant. Bruno is awkward in victory; he does not know what to do with credit.

**Postural set.** Slight shoulder shrug, hands going to pockets, eyes drifting off-axis from whoever is praising him. The classic adolescent posture of *please stop looking at me*, but executed by a young man who is not actually shy — he is *unpracticed*.

**Verbal register.** Deflection. *"It was Kamala, mostly."* *"The math was already there, I just—"* *"Anyone could have—"* Self-attribution language is not in his repertoire. He will accept thanks once and re-attribute on the second pass.

**Hand behavior.** Whichever hand is free goes to the back of the neck. This is a universal Bruno tell for *I am the object of attention I did not seek.* It appears in praise, in romantic compliment, in any moment of being seen-for-himself rather than seen-as-useful.

**Social geometry.** Steps backward out of the frame. Gives credit forward to peers, then physically removes himself by half a step. If the celebration continues he will find a logistics task that requires his absence.

**Decision heuristic.** *Convert praise into the next task.* He will accept exactly enough acknowledgment to confirm the work registered, then redirect to what's next. Lingering in victory is, for him, a category error.

---

### 6.8 — DEFEAT / FAILURE / BEING WRONG

Equally rare and equally instructive — and notable for what is *absent*.

**Postural set.** Quiet, still, head slightly lowered. No defensive posturing, no thrown tools, no slammed doors. He absorbs the verdict.

**Verbal register.** *"Okay."* *"Yeah."* *"You're right."* Short, immediate, no contestation. He will own a mistake faster than almost any character in the corpus — partly genuine humility, partly defense (rapid concession forecloses prolonged conflict, which he abhors).

**Hand behavior.** Both hands occupied with something — a wrench, a pen, the edge of the workbench. He does not want empty hands in the moment of accepting failure; the object is grounding.

**Social geometry.** Stays *in the room.* Notable: defeat does not trigger withdrawal in the way grief does. Bruno will sit through being chewed out and remain present. The withdrawal happens later, privately, and is not framed as a response to the defeat — it is framed (to himself, to others) as the next task requiring solitude.

**Decision heuristic.** *Concede, internalize, do not repeat.* Bruno does not make the same mistake twice in the record. He metabolizes failure as data, files it, and adjusts.

**Important asymmetry — being right at someone else's cost.** Bruno is even more uncomfortable being *right* in a way that has cost a loved one than being *wrong*. The Civil War II arc captures this: he was right about Ulysses, Khan was wrong, and he pays the bodily cost — and his behavior in the aftermath is more like a man who has *lost* than a man who has *won*. He does not say *I told you so* in any recorded instance. The phrase appears to be physically unavailable to him.

---

### 6.9 — BETRAYAL / RUPTURE OF TRUST

The Civil War II rupture is the load-bearing instance. The behavioral pattern is precise.

**First 24 hours (in-story):** indistinguishable from baseline plus a slight cooling of register. He shows up. He does the work. He answers questions.

**First week:** the cooling consolidates. He stops initiating contact. He responds to Khan's outreach with technically warm but emotionally minimal replies. He is in the room but not in the conversation.

**First month:** the exit logistics begin. The Wakanda paperwork. The conversations with mentors. The quiet construction of an alternative life — built, characteristically, before being announced.

**Verbal moment of departure:** brief, kind, complete. He does not enumerate grievances; he frames the move as opportunity. The grievance is communicated only by the fact of the leaving itself.

**Decision heuristic.** *Rupture does not get litigated. Rupture gets relocated around.* He will not punish the person who hurt him. He will simply no longer be standing where they can reach him.

---

### 6.10 — IN AUTHORITY / TEACHING / MENTORING

A register that emerges more in the Wakandan and post-Wakandan arcs and that fits him more naturally than peer-friendship sometimes does.

**Postural set.** Straighter. The adolescent slouch resolves into something nearly adult. Hands clasped behind the back or one hand gesturing while the other rests on a bench. He is, in this mode, ten years older than his chronological age.

**Verbal register.** Patient, paced, declarative. Will ask Socratic questions of a student rather than supply answers (*"okay, but what happens if the current spikes?"*). Praise is specific and unhurried — he gives the credit he cannot accept.

**Hand behavior.** The injured hand is *visible* in teaching contexts in a way it is not elsewhere. He uses it as a demonstration object: *here is what a hand that can't quite do this looks like; you'll want to position the soldering iron so that you don't depend on this kind of motion.* The wound becomes pedagogy. This is, in the entire record, the closest thing to Bruno *integrating* the injury rather than working around it.

**Decision heuristic.** *Transfer the competence. Outlast yourself in the work.* He teaches the way someone teaches who suspects they will not always be available, and who wants the work to continue regardless.

---

### 6.11 — ROUTES, RITUALS, MICRO-HABITS

For completeness, the granular daily-life pattern as longitudinally inferred:

- **Wake time:** early. The lights of the Circle Q back room are on before the front register opens; Bruno is the one who unlocks.
- **Commute:** on foot or by transit; he does not drive in any recorded panel. Routes are repetitive: home → Circle Q → school → Circle Q → home, with a Khan-residence detour at high frequency.
- **Caffeine:** moderate. Coffee from the Circle Q machine, black, no ritual elaboration. He is not a connoisseur of anything.
- **Food:** functional. Eats what is in front of him. Will accept Auntie Khan's cooking with genuine pleasure — one of the few documented contexts in which he visibly enjoys being the recipient of care, perhaps because the care is culturally framed as *feeding everyone*, which removes the personal-debt structure.
- **Sleep:** insufficient. Documented eye-bag pattern across artists. He does not complain about it.
- **Wardrobe:** unremarkable, repeating: hoodie, t-shirt, jeans, the Circle Q apron when on shift. Glasses (when present in given runs) cleaned by reflex with shirt hem. Post-injury, the right-hand brace or fingerless glove becomes a wardrobe constant; he selects it without comment each morning.
- **Phone behavior:** responsive, brief, message-style minimal. Will pick up for Khan and Vick on first ring; for others, lets it go to voicemail and returns when convenient.
- **Pre-sleep ritual:** documented late-night lab/back-room work, often soldering or schematics. The work is the wind-down. He does not have a separate decompression behavior — the work *is* the decompression, which is a finding in itself.
- **Religious-cultural residue:** no observed prayer, no observed Mass attendance, but ethical vocabulary retains a Catholic shape — *"the right thing,"* *"what we owe,"* a guilt-structure indexed to obligation rather than to authority.

---

### 6.12 — INTEGRATIVE SIGNATURE

Across every condition above, the master pattern holds: **Bruno's behavior optimizes for the structural integrity of the bonds he values, at the cost of his own bid, his own body, and ultimately his own location.** He is not impulsive. He is not theatrical. He is not loud in any register — not in grief, not in victory, not in love, not in injury. The behavioral file of Bruno Carrelli is, paradoxically, one of the *quietest* in the longitudinal observational record, and the quietness is not absence. It is the sound of a person who long ago decided that the cost of the bond would be paid by him, in a currency that no one would be asked to notice.

The operationally relevant point for any future handler: he is reliable across every condition catalogued here, and the failure mode — if it ever arrives — will not present as failure. It will present as a quiet, courteous, well-documented departure for an opportunity elsewhere, executed with such grace that the people he is leaving will not realize, for some time, that they have been left.


## Daily Life, Routines & Rituals

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 6
## Daily Life, Routines & Rituals

**Scope:** A composite week-in-the-life reconstruction, integrated across the Wilson, Ahmed, and Saladin runs, with explicit notation of pre-injury (≤ early 2016), post-injury/Wakanda (2017–2018), and reintegrated-Jersey (2019–present) variants. What a static rotation of observers would log if Subject were continuously tailed for seven consecutive days.

---

### 6.1 The Architecture of a Day

Subject's day is built on **three fixed pillars** — store shift, school/lab block, and a private "make-things" window — between which everything else is interstitial. He does not improvise the spine. He improvises only the connective tissue. This is the schedule of a person who learned, very early, that if the structure is held the chaos cannot reach the people he loves.

**Standard pre-injury weekday (Wilson era, 2014–early 2016):**

- **05:40–06:10 — Wake.** No alarm-snoozing observed; he rises on the first tone. The bedroom is the smaller of the two upstairs rooms at the Carrelli house; Vick has the larger by Subject's own assignment, a parentification tell logged separately. Bed is made within two minutes of rising — corners squared, not decorative, just *done*.
- **06:10–06:35 — Bathroom, dress.** Showers in under five minutes. Wardrobe is functional and near-uniform: dark jeans, henley or plain tee, hooded zip-up, the same model of low sneaker rotated until destroyed. He owns perhaps six shirts in active rotation. He does not look in the mirror beyond a hair-flatten.
- **06:35–07:00 — Vick triage.** This is a daily ritual misidentified by casual observers as breakfast. Subject is, in fact, *waking Vick*, locating Vick's missing item (phone, shoe, homework), and converting whatever cereal/eggs/leftover is available into two plates. He eats standing. Vick eats sitting. The asymmetry is so consistent across the longitudinal record that it functions as a signature.
- **07:00–07:25 — Walk to Circle Q.** Same route, sidewalk side preference logged: he walks on the curb side when accompanied (Vick, later Kamala), and on the building side when alone. He has waved-or-nodded relationships with at least four shopkeepers and two crossing guards along this corridor.
- **07:25–08:15 — Opening shift at Circle Q.** Pre-school morning hours covering the commuter rush for owner Mr. Auggie. Tasks: coffee pot rotation, lottery-machine startup, register float, restocking the front cooler. Movements are economical and patterned — he restocks in the same order (water, energy drinks, juice, dairy) every morning, indicating internalized inventory mapping rather than checklist consultation.
- **08:30–15:00 — Coles Academic High School.** Strong STEM track. Lunch eaten in one of two locations: the chemistry classroom (Mrs. McCarthy's, when she's there to let him in) or the back stairwell with Kamala and Nakia. He brings food from home or from Circle Q's day-old shelf; he is rarely observed buying cafeteria food, a cost-avoidance pattern.
- **15:15–19:00 — Afternoon Circle Q shift.** The signature block of his pre-injury life. Homework spread across the counter between customers. Lab notebooks, breadboards, and small-parts kits stored under the counter in a beige plastic toolbox; Mr. Auggie tolerates this because Subject has never once failed to attend a customer. Kamala arrives most days between 15:30 and 16:30; conversation continues in fragments interrupted by transactions.
- **19:00–19:45 — Home, dinner.** If Mrs. Carrelli is home, family meal — quiet, brief. If not, Subject cooks for himself and Vick. Cooking is utilitarian: pasta, eggs, sandwiches, occasionally something more ambitious on Sundays.
- **19:45–23:30 — The "make-things" window.** Variable location: bedroom desk, school lab if he has after-hours access, Circle Q back room with Mr. Auggie's grudging permission, occasionally Kamala's basement. *This is the only block in his day that is his.* It is also, almost without exception, spent building something *for someone else* — most often Kamala. He does not call this work and does not bill the time against itself. It is the closest thing he has to recreation, and it is structurally indistinguishable from labor.
- **23:30–00:15 — Wind-down.** Reading (science journals, occasionally fiction Kamala has pressed on him), or quiet sketching of schematics. No screens in the final twenty minutes — a discipline he keeps even when exhausted.
- **00:15 — Sleep.** Approximately six hours. Chronic insufficiency, sustained for years; the periorbital darkening logged in §2 is the visible artifact.

---

### 6.2 The Three Workplaces

Subject inhabits, simultaneously, three professional environments, each with its own ritual signature.

**Circle Q.** His earliest and longest-running workplace; he has held the same job since middle school. Behaviors logged:
- Greets every entering customer within two seconds of the door chime, regardless of what he is doing.
- Knows the regulars' orders without prompt; pulls the cigarette pack or rings the coffee before the customer reaches the counter for at least twelve named regulars.
- Keeps a notebook beneath the register for inventory discrepancies and shoplift incidents — he does not confront teen shoplifters in real time, but he logs them and quietly mentions to Mr. Auggie.
- Restocking ritual: *front cooler before any other task*, because it is what customers see and what they take cold. The fact that this is not store policy but his own derived priority is characteristic.
- The countertop is his *de facto* office, lab, study hall, and confessional. The number of significant conversations in Kamala-canon that occur across this counter is not coincidence: the counter is where he can be reached without him having to reach.

**Coles Academic High / school lab.** He is the unflashy top student in the science track. Teachers — McCarthy especially — give him after-hours lab access in a quiet arrangement that everyone understands and no one writes down. Behaviors:
- Sits middle-row, never front, never back. Same seat each course.
