- Volunteers answers approximately 30% of the rate his demonstrated knowledge would justify — he yields floor to peers, especially less able ones, and only answers when no one else will or when the teacher specifically asks.
- Lab partner of choice: Kamala when possible, Nakia otherwise, anyone-quiet as fallback. He will not partner with chronic non-contributors and is willing to spend social capital to avoid it — one of the few areas where he protects his own time.
- Cleans his own station and one other before leaving. Every time.

**Home workshop / wherever he is building.** A migratory third workplace. The toolset is portable by design (the beige toolbox at Circle Q is one node; the bedroom desk is another; the school lab is the third). Behaviors:
- Tools laid out in identical configuration every session — soldering iron upper-right, flush cutters left of iron, helping-hands center, components in segregated trays by value. The reproducibility of this layout across locations is itself the ritual.
- Talks to himself in low murmurs while working — half-formed sentences, the audible edge of a continuous internal monologue. Volume rises slightly when a step is going wrong; this is the closest he comes to externalized frustration.
- Drinks water, not coffee, while soldering. Coffee is for the counter; the bench is hydration only. This is a safety-derived habit (caffeine tremor) that has hardened into ritual.
- Will not eat at the bench — food is taken in a deliberate break, at a different surface. Discipline maintained even when working through dinner.

---

### 6.3 Post-Injury Modifications (2016–present)

The hand injury rewired the daily architecture without changing its outline. Surveillance differential:

- **Wake time pushed back ~30 minutes** during the worst of recovery; subsequently returned to baseline but with morning hand exercises added (a routine of stretch, grip, and fine-motor drills, performed silently, typically while waiting for coffee or while Vick is in the bathroom).
- **Brace/glove donning** as a new morning ritual. Performed before leaving the bedroom — he does not let the household watch him put it on. By the time he is downstairs the hand is configured.
- **Tool layout reorganized for left-hand primacy** on fine work. The right hand becomes the *holding* hand; the left does the precise actuation. Observers familiar with the pre-injury layout will note the mirror-flip of the bench as the single most visible behavioral marker of the post-injury era.
- **Verbal direction of others' hands** — a new skill. When Kamala (or later, Wakandan classmates) is present, he will walk them through a procedure he cannot perform alone. He has gotten very good at this, and it has subtly broadened his pedagogical capacity.
- **One-handed typing** at speed competitive with his prior two-handed rate by mid-2017. Adaptation curve consistent with sustained, undiscussed practice.
- **Photography of completed work** — newly introduced post-injury, ostensibly for documentation, in practice (UATU read) a substitute for the tactile satisfaction he can no longer fully access. He keeps a phone gallery of finished builds that he does not share.

The Wakanda interval imposed an entirely new schedule (academy cohort, dormitory rhythm, Kareem-anchored social life) but the *underlying* habits — early rise, food standing, work-as-rest, log-everything, decline to discuss the hand — transferred intact. He is exportable. The structure travels.

---

### 6.4 The Weekly Cadence

**Monday–Friday:** the architecture in §6.1, modulated by school-day variance.

**Saturday:** Longest Circle Q shift, typically 09:00–19:00. The day on which Subject is most reliably locatable by anyone seeking him; Kamala, Bruno-pre-injury, would often *find* him here rather than text him. Saturday evening is the only block he reliably reserves for non-instrumental social time — historically a movie or a walk with Mike (pre-2016), later video calls with Kareem (2017+), later still a low-key hang with the broader friend group.

**Sunday:** Reduced shift or off. Sunday morning the closest he comes to a sabbath: he sleeps until 08:00, sometimes 09:00. Mass attendance is sporadic and trending toward zero across the longitudinal record — he is a culturally Catholic boy whose actual religious practice is a residual once-or-twice-a-year drift, usually accompanying his mother. Sunday afternoon is *cooking* (the more ambitious meal of the week, often the only one Vick eats willingly) and Sunday evening is *prep* — backpack repack, schematic for the week's build laid out, brace cleaned. The Sunday-night ritual is the keystone of the architecture; if it is skipped, the following week visibly deteriorates.

---

### 6.5 Habits of Place

Subject has a small number of anchor locations and almost no incidental ones. A surveillance map of any given month would consist of perhaps eight named nodes:

1. **Carrelli house** — sleep, Vick-management, bench-2.
2. **Circle Q** — primary workplace, social interface, study, bench-3.
3. **Coles Academic High** — school, lab, bench-1.
4. **Khan residence (basement, kitchen)** — secondary social/work site; access intermittent but long-running.
5. **The Jersey City waterfront walk** — his thinking route. He does it alone, after closing shifts, when something is unresolved. The walk is the *one* place he is observed to externally pace a problem rather than internalize it.
6. **A specific halal cart** — patronized at least weekly, the operator knows him by name and order.
7. **The Holland Tunnel-adjacent diner** — used for occasional late-night meetings with Kamala in costume-aftermath situations, chosen for its 24-hour status and inattentive staff.
8. **Post-2017 only:** the Wakandan academy lab and dormitory, then on returns, a rotating apartment of Kareem's family network.

He does not frequent parties, clubs, bars, or any venue organized around social performance. He has been to perhaps four parties in the entire canonical record and at each one is logged as the person managing a friend's drink, calling a ride, or leaving early to walk someone home.

---

### 6.6 Habits of Time

- **Punctual to within three minutes** for any commitment. The variance is on the early side; he is almost never late.
- **Replies to texts in clusters**, typically at shift-end and pre-sleep. He does not text-and-walk; he does not text on the counter during transactions. The discipline is consistent.
- **Sleep debt accumulated weekly, partially repaid Sunday.** Net negative; the periorbital signature persists.
- **Birthday and anniversary recall is near-total** for people in his close circle. He remembers Kamala's mother's birthday. He remembers Mike's dog's name years after the breakup. The memory is not effortful; it is what attentive people who organize their world around others' needs accumulate as a byproduct.

---

### 6.7 Micro-Rituals & Tells

These are the granular signatures a sustained tail would acquire after a fortnight:

- **The two-tap.** When closing his lab notebook or toolbox, he taps the lid twice — once at the latch, once at center. Origin unknown; possibly a checksum gesture inherited from a teacher. Consistent across years and locations.
- **The brace adjustment.** Post-injury, when concentrating, he will reseat the brace on his right wrist with his left thumb. He does this perhaps thirty times a day; it is the somatic equivalent of a sigh.
- **The pre-speech pause.** Before saying anything that matters — an objection, a confession, a hard piece of news — he draws a half-breath, holds it for roughly one second, then speaks. The pause is observable in panel beats across multiple artists' renderings. It is a *deliberation tell*; he is checking the sentence before releasing it.
- **The counter lean.** At Circle Q he leans with both forearms on the counter when engaged in conversation; he stands upright when a customer approaches. The reset between postures is automatic and instantaneous.
- **The notebook habit.** He carries a small notebook (later supplanted by a phone-notes app but the physical notebook never entirely disappears). Entries: schematics, inventory deltas, reading-list items, and — UATU infers from negative space — occasional one-line emotional log entries that he does not reread.
- **The thank-you under-acknowledgment.** When thanked, he says "yeah, no worries" or "of course" — never "you're welcome." Subtle but consistent. He cannot quite accept the framing in which the gift was his to give.
- **The food-offer.** When seated with anyone — friend, sibling, near-stranger — he will offer the first bite or the larger portion. This is so ingrained that he does it unconsciously and is mildly confused on the rare occasions it is refused.
- **The shutdown sequence at Circle Q.** Same order every night: wipe counter (left-to-right, two passes), top off coffee filters for morning, count register, pull notebook out from under register, kill front lights, kill back lights, lock the back, exit through the front, double-tug the front door handle to confirm. The double-tug is the night's version of the two-tap.
- **The phone discipline.** Phone face-down during conversation, every time. He has been observed flipping it down without breaking eye contact mid-sentence; the gesture is reflex.
- **Headphones, never earbuds, when walking alone at night.** Single headphone on the curb-side ear, so traffic remains audible on the open side. Safety-rationalized; situational-awareness-trained.

---

### 6.8 Downtime — What He Does With Time That Is His

This is the section the file struggles to populate, because **there is almost no time that is purely his.** What other adolescents would log as recreation, Subject logs as either (a) work-for-someone, (b) maintenance of a relationship, or (c) sleep. The genuine personal-leisure footprint:

- **Reading.** Science journals (he has a free *Nature* digest subscription via the school), occasional sci-fi paperbacks, anything Kamala recommends. Reading is the one activity he does *for himself* and even this is partially relational (the Kamala recommendations).
- **Walking the waterfront.** §6.5 node 5. The one true solitary leisure.
- **Sketching.** Schematics primarily, but UATU has logged a small number of non-schematic drawings — a bird, the storefront, once a hand (his own, pre-injury; this drawing is dated to roughly six months before the injury and has accreted a retrospective gravity he cannot have intended).
- **Cooking on Sundays.** The closest thing to a hobby in the conventional sense; an activity with a sensory and aesthetic dimension undertaken at his own pace.
- **Long-form conversation with one person.** Mike, then Kareem, occasionally Kamala on a good night. He does not enjoy group socializing; one-to-one is his medium.

He does not game. He does not binge television. He does not scroll. He does not, in the technical sense, *waste time* — and this is, in UATU's read, less a virtue than a symptom: the parentified child whose adult-load arrived early does not develop the muscle of unstructured leisure, and Subject has not retrofitted it.

---

### 6.9 What a Week of Surveillance Would Conclude

A seven-day rotation would produce a file of striking redundancy. The variance week-to-week is low; the same nodes, the same hours, the same gestures recur with near-liturgical fidelity. An analyst skimming the logs would, by day three, be able to predict day five with 85%+ accuracy on location, 70%+ on activity, 60%+ on companion.

The interesting data would not be in the activities but in the *deviations*, and the deviations are diagnostic:

- A skipped Sunday prep predicts a difficult Monday.
- An unplanned Khan-house detour after closing shift predicts that something is wrong with Kamala that he has not been told about but has inferred.
- An extended waterfront walk predicts unresolved internal content — the longer the walk, the larger the content.
- A canceled shift predicts a Vick incident, a Kareem call requiring time-zone accommodation, or, rarely, a hand-pain day he will not name.
- Silence on the brace — i.e., no adjustment, no reseat, for an unusually long period — predicts that he is in flow and should not be interrupted.

The portrait that emerges is of a young man whose days are a tightly engineered scaffold built to hold other people's lives steady, maintained by a discipline so consistent it has become invisible to him, and costing him — in sleep, in solitude not taken, in leisure muscle not developed, in a body worked past the point its owner will admit — a quiet, sustained tax he has been paying since before he was old enough to know he had a choice.

He has not, in the entire longitudinal record, taken a day off for no reason. The file would note this. The file would, eventually, recommend that someone tell him he is allowed to.


## Relationships I — Family & Origin Bonds

# UATU DOSSIER — SUBJECT: BRUNO CARRELLI
## Section 6 — Relationships I: Family & Origin Bonds

*Classification note: This section maps the primary kinship vectors that constitute Bruno Carrelli's developmental substrate. The Carrelli household is the negative space against which every later relational pattern in his life renders visible. The subject does not speak about his family. This is itself the dataset.*

---

### 6.1 — VICTOR "VICK" CARRELLI (younger brother; the primary attachment)

**Relational topology.** Vick is, functionally and emotionally, the most important person in Bruno's life until at least Kamala's revelation in *Ms. Marvel* (2014) #3, and arguably remains so under the surface for considerably longer. The fraternal bond is the *original* relationship — older than the Circle Q shift, older than the friendship with Kamala, older than any conscious memory of being a separate person from his role in the family system. Bruno did not choose to parent Vick; he was conscripted, somewhere between ages six and nine by inference, and the conscription was never rescinded.

**History and pattern.** Across the Wilson run Vick is established as the chaos-generator of the Carrelli household: school discipline issues, social drift, eventually entanglement with the Inventor's youth-labor cell (*Ms. Marvel* 2014 #8–11). Bruno's documented responses across this arc form a precise behavioral fingerprint: (1) he learns of the problem before the parents do; (2) he attempts a unilateral fix; (3) he conceals the full magnitude from Kamala for as long as plausible; (4) when concealment fails, he understates rather than overstates; (5) he physically goes after Vick, alone, into a confrontation his somatic baseline does not equip him for, and nearly dies. This is not a one-time crisis response. This is a *protocol* — and protocols imply repetition, which means we should infer a long pre-canon history of smaller versions: Vick caught shoplifting and Bruno paying the storekeeper; Vick truant and Bruno forging the note; Vick in a fight and Bruno walking him home the long way so the bruise wouldn't be seen at dinner.

**Dynamics.** The asymmetry is total. Vick takes; Bruno gives. Vick is allowed — by the family system, by Bruno himself — to be a child past the point of childhood, because Bruno is doing the structural work of being-adult on his behalf. Crucially, Bruno does not resent this in any depicted moment. The resentment, if it exists, has been processed so far upstream of consciousness that it presents as nothing at all — which is diagnostic rather than reassuring. A boy who is not allowed to resent the brother who is wrecking his adolescence will, by necessity, route that affect into something else; in Bruno's case, into work, into hyper-competence, into the silent assumption that this is simply what older brothers *are*.

**Evolution.** Post–Inventor arc, Vick's depicted screen-time drops sharply, but the *fact* of Vick remains a constant in Bruno's calculation of risk. When Bruno transfers to Wakanda, one of the unspoken questions — never asked aloud in canon — is *who watches Vick now.* The most honest read is that Bruno had to allow himself to believe Vick was stable enough to leave, because the alternative was that the Wakanda transfer was selfish, and Bruno's self-concept cannot tolerate that framing. In later runs (Ahmed, Saladin) Vick is offstage; Bruno's references to him are sparse and tonally neutral, which under the subject's coding conventions reads as *active suppression of a still-live concern* rather than resolution.

**Trust / safety.** Bruno trusts Vick *with* nothing operationally and *for* nothing emotionally. The trust is purely structural — Vick is family, therefore Vick is non-optional, therefore the bond persists regardless of behavior. This is not the trust of a peer; it is the unconditional trust of a parent for a child, and it is mis-aged. Safety, in either direction, is minimal. Vick has put Bruno in physical danger more than once; Bruno cannot be candid with Vick about his own interior life because the role-asymmetry forbids it.

**Failure mode.** The bond fails — has already partially failed — by Bruno's *inability to require anything of Vick.* He cannot say *I need you to stop costing me my body and my time.* He cannot say *I went to Wakanda partly to stop being your scaffolding.* The relationship will continue to function in its lopsided form indefinitely, because both parties have organized around it. The catastrophic failure mode is a future Vick crisis — adult, larger-stakes, addiction or legal — that Bruno cannot fix from a continent away and cannot forgive himself for not having prevented.

**Leverage.** Vick is the single highest-leverage person in Bruno's life for any actor seeking to move him. A credible threat to Vick — physical, legal, financial — would pull Bruno from any commitment, on any continent, within hours. He would not weigh it; he would not consult; he would not tell Kamala. He would *go.* This is the oldest reflex in his nervous system and the one most resistant to revision.

---

### 6.2 — MRS. CARRELLI (mother; the structuring absence)

**Relational topology.** The mother is canonically thin on the page — referenced more than depicted, present in the household more in function than in scene. This thinness is itself the information. In a domestic system that produced a parentified eldest son, the parent who is *absent in function* is by definition the parent whose absence created the vacuum he filled.

**Inferred history.** Working mother, almost certainly working long or irregular hours, in a Jersey City Italian-American family whose financial baseline reads as fragile-working-class. Whether the absence is shift-work, second-job, exhaustion, depression, or some combination is not specified in canon; the operational outcome is identical. From Bruno's earliest memory she has been a person whose love is not in question but whose *presence* is rationed, and whose capacity to manage the household's emotional and logistical load is exceeded by the household's needs.

**Dynamics.** Bruno's posture toward his mother is — by inference from every adjacent depicted behavior — *protective rather than demanding.* He does not bring her his problems. He does not bring her Vick's problems until they are unmanageable, and possibly not even then. He brings her competence, the gift of a son who never adds to the load. The transaction is: she does not have to worry about him, and in exchange he does not get to be worried about. This is not consciously brokered; it is the equilibrium the system settled into.

**Evolution.** No depicted rupture, no depicted reconciliation, no depicted scene of substantive emotional disclosure. The Wakanda transfer would, in a normal family, occasion a charged conversation; in Bruno's family it appears to have occasioned logistics. The relationship is stable in the way a load-bearing wall is stable: nobody examines it, and it holds.

**Trust / safety.** Bruno trusts his mother's *love* completely and her *capacity to receive his interior life* not at all. He has trained himself, over a decade and a half, to translate his needs into forms she does not have to absorb. Safety is high in the sense that she will never harm him; low in the sense that she cannot be the one he goes to when something breaks.

**Failure mode.** The bond does not fail by rupture. It fails — has been failing, slowly, since he was small — by *attenuation*: by Bruno's increasing fluency in not needing her, until the relationship is a warmth at a distance rather than a working channel. A medical crisis or financial collapse on her end would activate every parentified reflex he has; he would route money and presence to her and would feel, at some level he would not name, *vindicated* by being able to give back what he had been giving all along.

**Leverage.** High but slow. Threats to her wellbeing would pull him home; opportunities to provide for her would pull him toward income, toward stability, toward any institutional offer that included a salary line he could remit. An intelligent handler who wanted to *retain* Bruno over years rather than move him in a moment would underwrite his mother's security and let him know it had been done. He would never speak of the obligation, and he would never forget it.

---

### 6.3 — MR. CARRELLI (father; the minimal presence)

**Relational topology.** Even thinner on the page than the mother. The father is canonically a near-cipher — referenced, occasionally framed, never developed. In the negative-space methodology applied to the mother, the father reads as an even more profound absence, because there is no clear *labor* explanation deflecting the question of where he is.

**Inferred history.** Working-class, Italian-American, Jersey City. Whether he is emotionally remote, physically often absent, depressive, drinking, or simply temperamentally minimal is not specified; the operational signature is again the same. The father is not a source of guidance, not a source of pressure, not a source of modeling. He is a presence one navigates around, not toward.

**Dynamics.** Bruno appears to have constructed his masculinity *without reference* to his father — which is rarer than it sounds and almost always means the father was, in some way, a model the son decided early not to follow. The decision is unlikely to have been conscious. The evidence is in the assembled portrait: Bruno is *exactly* the man his father, by inference, is not — verbally precise, emotionally attentive (even when not expressive), reliably present for those who depend on him, refusing the cultural script of the gruff distant working-class Italian father even while inheriting the work ethic. The negation is so clean it implies an original.

**Evolution.** Static. There is no depicted arc of reconciliation, conflict, or evolving understanding. Bruno appears to have made his peace with his father long before the canon opens, and the peace is the peace of low expectations honored.

**Trust / safety.** Trust is procedural — the father will not harm him, will not interfere, will not show up in a destabilizing way. Safety is the safety of a known minimum. Bruno does not bring his father anything because there is no demonstrated capacity to receive it.

**Failure mode.** The relationship fails by having never quite begun. The risk is not rupture but *retrospective grief* — a future moment, likely after the father's death, when Bruno realizes he organized his entire adolescence around a man whose absence he had stopped registering as a wound. He will not cry at the funeral. He will fix the logistics. He will sit with it, alone, for years.

**Leverage.** Low in the short term, high in a specific window: a father's illness or death would activate Bruno's *unfinished* relationship with him in a way no other event could, and the resulting grief — because it would be the grief of a thing he never had — would be disorienting in proportion to how successfully he had previously suppressed the absence. A handler observing such an event should anticipate two to six months of degraded affective availability and a hardening, not softening, of the suppression reflex.

---

### 6.4 — THE EXTENDED FAMILY (the Italian-American cultural surround)

**Relational topology.** Bruno's canon does not foreground extended family — no depicted grandparents, aunts, uncles, cousins of operational significance — but the *cultural substrate* is unmistakable and shapes his behavioral baseline in ways that read as familial even where individual relatives are absent.

**Substrate inheritance.** Catholic-cultural rather than Catholic-devotional: he has the moral grammar (obligation, sacrifice, the duty of the eldest, the unspoken contract that family is the floor under which one does not fall) without the active metaphysics (no depicted Mass attendance, no rosary, no invocation of saints under stress). Italian-American working-class Jersey: the food, the neighborhood density, the assumption that the corner store is a node of community rather than a transaction point — all of this is in his comportment at the Circle Q, where he is not just a clerk but a *fixture*, a person who knows everyone's name and order.

**Dynamics.** The extended family is, on inference, a network that exists but is not heavily drawn upon. The Carrelli nuclear unit appears to manage its difficulties internally — which in this cultural context usually means a combination of pride, privacy, and a quiet conviction that asking is admitting. Bruno absorbed this fully. He does not ask.

**Trust / safety / failure / leverage.** Functionally the extended family operates as a *background tone* rather than as a set of actionable bonds. They are unlikely to be either resource or threat in any operational sense, but the *script* they encoded in him — eldest-son duty, silent endurance, family-as-floor — is one of the most durable behavioral structures he carries.

---

### 6.5 — THE CARRELLI HOUSEHOLD AS A SYSTEM

**Topology.** Two minimally-present parents; one chaos-generating younger brother; one parentified eldest son holding the structural load. This is a textbook configuration, and the textbook predicts exactly the personality assembled in §3–5: precocious competence, hyper-responsibility, suppressed bid, difficulty receiving care, idealization of the cared-for object, geographic flight as the only available exit.

**Domestic micro-pattern (inferred, granular).** Bruno almost certainly: cooks or assembles dinner for himself and Vick on irregular evenings; tracks Vick's school schedule more reliably than the parents do; knows the household's bills by category and approximate amount; has a mental ledger of which appliance is failing and which can wait; keeps the small repairs (loose hinge, blown bulb, slow drain) handled before anyone notices they were problems. None of this is depicted on-page in detail; all of it is implied by the consistency of his competence everywhere else and by the absence of any depicted adult performing these functions.

**Speech pattern at home.** Almost certainly quieter than at the Circle Q or with Kamala. The home is the site of the original suppression; the public spaces are where his verbal life expanded. A surveillance file would note that Bruno's word-count per hour is markedly lower in the Carrelli apartment than in any other location he occupies, and that the topics discussed are overwhelmingly logistical.

**Failure mode of the system.** The system has already failed in the only way it could: it produced a child who turned out *well* by every external metric and at the cost of an interior life he has never been able to articulate to anyone in the family that produced him. He left. They did not, on any depicted evidence, ask him to stay in a way that would have required them to see what they had been taking. The Wakanda transfer is, among other things, the moment the Carrelli household lost its load-bearing wall and discovered — quietly, off-page — whether it could stand without him. Canon does not tell us. Bruno does not ask.

---

### 6.6 — THE DEAD AND THE NEAR-DEAD

**Status.** No depicted parental death, no depicted sibling death, no depicted extended-family death of operational weight. The Carrelli ledger of canonical loss is, by superhero-adjacent standards, unusually clean.

**What this means.** Bruno has not yet been tested by a death in the family he was the steady one for. Every adaptation he has built — the suppression, the competence, the geographic distance, the refusal to grieve out loud — has been built against losses that were *relational* (the rift with Kamala, the loss of his hand's function, the foreclosure of the romantic possibility) rather than *terminal*. The grief instruments have never been calibrated to a real death.

**Predicted failure mode at first family death.** When it comes — and the actuarial likelihood across a decade-long published life is high — Bruno will handle the logistics with unnerving precision, will not cry in any setting where he can be observed, will increase his work hours, and will go quiet for a period of months. The closest people to him will not be told the depth of it. Whoever is his partner at that time will experience the death as a *withdrawal of him* rather than an opening into him. This is the single most predictable, and most preventable, future failure in the file.

**Leverage.** Anticipatory care — a handler, partner, or close friend who *insists* on being present for him at the first such death, who does not accept "I'm fine" and does not let the suppression complete — could rewrite the script that has governed him since childhood. It is the one intervention in the entire family-relations matrix that could produce a structural change rather than a marginal one. The window will be narrow. The cost of missing it will be another twenty years of the same pattern, harder.

---

*End Section 6. Continues in Section 7 — Relationships II: Chosen Bonds (Kamala Khan, Mike Miller, Kareem / Red Dagger, and the Jersey City peer field).*


## Relationships II — Allies, Chosen Family & Mentors

# RELATIONSHIPS II — ALLIES, CHOSEN FAMILY & MENTORS

**Scope note.** This section maps the *non-romantic, non-familial, non-adversarial* relational field of Bruno Carrelli — the people through whom his life is structurally held together outside the Khan house, the Carrelli house, and the romantic register. Where overlaps exist (Kamala is also his oldest friend; Kareem is also a peer-collaborator), the relational vector treated here is the *non-romantic axis* of the bond; romantic content is referred out to Relationships I. The subject's chosen-family field is unusually narrow for a young man of his social position — a function of his temperament (low pursuit, high reliability) and of the parentified pattern documented in §3. He does not collect people. People collect him.

---

## 1. KAMALA KHAN — primary attachment, asymmetric chosen-family

**History.** Pre-canonical friendship of unspecified duration — by *Ms. Marvel* (2014) #1 the two are operating with the worn ease of a years-long bond. They are middle-school classmates who became high-school confidants; Bruno is the friend her parents trust, the only one Aamir Khan has ever spoken of with anything resembling approval, the boy who has been in and out of the Khan kitchen since before Kamala had a phone. He is the first non-family person to whom she discloses her powers (#3, 2014), and he is the *only* peer who saw her Inhuman before she chose to show him. That sequencing — *witnessed before told* — sets the relational geometry permanently. He cannot un-know; she cannot un-be-seen; their intimacy is therefore foundational and involuntary at once.

**Dynamics.** Functionally: she is the principal, he is the entire support structure. He builds the gear, sews the costume revisions (the original lightning-bolt suit's structural reinforcements are his work), runs the comms, models the trajectories, identifies the villains by chemical signature, and tells her — repeatedly, and without ornament — when she is about to make a mistake. She is the protagonist of her life; he is the protagonist of his life *in service of hers*, and the asymmetry is not, in the Wilson run, perceived by either of them as a problem because both temperamentally accept the arrangement: she because she is sixteen and the world is enormous, he because being needed is the metabolism of his self-worth.

**Evolution across eras.**
- *Early Wilson (2014 #1–7).* Pure best-friend register; sibling-coded affection; comic warmth; the Circle Q as their shared theater. He is helping with chemistry homework in the back room as much as he is helping with super-heroics.
- *Mid Wilson (#8–11, Vick arc).* The relationship absorbs its first stress — he conceals Vick's situation from her for two issues, she discovers it, they fight quietly. Pattern established: rupture, his withdrawal, her pursuit, his quick reconciliation on her terms.
- *Late Wilson into 2015 vol. (#12–11).* The Mike relationship begins; Kamala's obliviousness to Bruno's prior romantic register is total and *he does not correct her*. He chooses, structurally, the version of the friendship in which her ignorance is preserved. This is the period of densest collaboration — lab scenes, gadget builds, the cloning-imposter plot — and the period of greatest accumulating private cost.
- *Civil War II tie-in (2015 #12, 2016).* The confession-attempt and the hand. He tries to tell her he loves her at the precise moment she is making the Ulysses-aligned choice he believes is wrong; the timing forecloses the disclosure; the warehouse confrontation injures him. He neither tells her the confession was real nor invoices her for the hand. She knows both, partially, and cannot find a register in which to address either. Their conversational fluency breaks here and is never fully restored.
- *Post-injury / Wakanda departure (2017).* He leaves. The exit is framed mutually as developmental, privately by him as survival. They keep in contact intermittently; the texture is *care without easy access*.
- *Ahmed / Saladin / Magnificent (2019–present).* He is reintegrated as *a* friend rather than *the* friend; Nakia, Zoe, Mike (in her later configurations), and the mutant cohort crowd the field. He is older-coded than she is now, which is structurally absurd (they are the same age) and emotionally exact. He calls her *Kamala* where he used to call her *KK*; the diminutive is gone from his mouth and she has noticed.

**Trust / safety.** Mutual and total in the domain of *facts* — there is no information either would withhold from the other under duress. Asymmetric and degraded in the domain of *feelings* — she still tells him everything; he tells her a curated subset and routes the rest into the lab bench or into silence. She would die for him. He would die for her and has nearly done so. Neither has yet learned to *live* for the other in a register that costs less than that.

**Failure mode.** He withdraws geographically and emotionally rather than confront. She apologizes too late, too profusely, and without the structural change that would make the apology stick. The failure mode is not betrayal; it is *attrition*. Each rupture leaves a small permanent residue. The hand is the largest of these residues; there will be others.

**Leverage.** Anyone who wants to move Bruno moves him through Kamala. He has demonstrated, repeatedly, that there is no personal cost he will not absorb on her behalf — including injury, exile, romantic foreclosure, and the silent acceptance of being wrong about her in public when being right would humiliate her. An adversary with operational sophistication would not threaten Bruno directly; they would inform Bruno that Kamala was in danger and follow him to where he goes. He has been used in exactly this way at least three times in canon and has not learned the lesson because the lesson is *unlearnable* by him without dismantling the personality.

---

## 2. NAKIA BAHADIR — peripheral-trusted, low-traffic high-bandwidth

**History.** Present from *Ms. Marvel* (2014) #1 as Kamala's other best friend; the triangle of Kamala/Bruno/Nakia is the original social unit. Nakia knows Bruno as long as Kamala has, but the bond between them has always been *mediated through Kamala* rather than developed independently. They are not phone-each-other friends. They are if-the-other-is-in-the-room-warmly-present friends.

**Dynamics.** Mutual respect, low overt warmth, high baseline trust. Nakia reads Bruno faster than Kamala does — she clocks the Bruno-loves-Kamala dynamic in the early Wilson run with a single eyebrow and never mentions it again — and Bruno reads Nakia as the *one peer in the field with adult ethical seriousness comparable to his own.* Their political instincts align (the Inventor's labor exploitation; the Ulysses problem; later, the mutant-policy questions in the Ahmed/Saladin eras). When they disagree it is over tactics, not values, and they resolve it by deferring to the person with domain expertise.

**Evolution.** Steadier than Bruno–Kamala because lower-stakes. The relationship does not pass through the romantic-asymmetry minefield and is therefore not subject to its erosions. Post-Wakanda, they correspond more reliably than Bruno and Kamala do — she sends him real-news updates, he sends her schematics for whatever community-organizing tech she is currently jerry-rigging. In the Magnificent / New Mutant eras she is one of the few people who can summon him back to Jersey City for a non-emergency.

**Trust / safety.** High and stable. He would tell her things he would not tell Kamala — specifically about Kamala — and she has the discretion to receive them without redistributing. She is one of the two people in his life (the other is Mike, treated under Relationships I) who has been allowed to see him *not-coping* without him reflexively reframing it.

**Failure mode.** Distance and inattention. Neither of them initiates contact at rate, so the relationship can go fallow for months without either party noticing. Neither would experience the fallow period as rupture; both would resume on contact as if no time had passed. The risk is therefore not breakage but *atrophy by default*.

**Leverage.** Limited. She is not a primary mover of him. An adversary attempting to use Nakia to reach Bruno would find Nakia herself an obstacle — she would identify the manipulation, refuse the role, and warn him. She is one of the few figures in the field on whom *no leverage operation against Bruno would succeed via her unwitting participation*.

---

## 3. KAREEM / RED DAGGER — peer, partner-in-the-non-romantic-sense, co-professional

**History.** Introduced in the later Wilson run as a Karachi-based vigilante operating in Kamala's extended family-of-origin territory; he and Bruno meet through Kamala and the bond develops independently of her. The Wakanda period and after sees Bruno and Kareem dating (treated under Relationships I); the *non-romantic* axis of the bond — peer-collaborator, fellow-traveler in the Kamala-orbit — is what concerns us here.

**Dynamics.** This is the only peer relationship in Bruno's life in which he is not, structurally, the responsible one. Kareem is older-feeling, more comfortable in his body, more direct about what he wants and how he feels about it; he routinely asks Bruno questions Bruno does not ask himself, and waits for the answers. Bruno's intellectualization defense does not work as well on Kareem as it does on everyone else — Kareem will simply re-ask the question in a non-technical register and look at him until he answers. This is corrective for Bruno in ways nothing else in his life has been.

**Evolution.** Cautious-warm early; physically reserved on Bruno's side (the hand is still tender, the Kamala situation still raw); deepening in the Wakanda academic year. Kareem is the only person in canon who has heard Bruno discuss the hand injury as a *loss* rather than as an engineering problem to be routed around. The relationship survives the Wakanda exit on diminished terms and remains in the chosen-family field even when not active in the romantic field.

**Trust / safety.** High in both directions on emotional disclosure; high in both directions on operational matters. The two have collaborated on tactical problems (the Karachi arcs, later Magnificent-era crossovers) with the easy division of labor of people who do not need to negotiate ego. Bruno will *receive care* from Kareem in a way he will not from almost anyone else, including Kamala — which is itself a small revolution in his interior life.

**Failure mode.** Geographic and temperamental. Bruno's withdrawal pattern under stress is the structural threat; Kareem reads it and tolerates it but does not chase, which is healthy for both and risky for the relationship's continuity. The non-romantic friendship survives the romantic intermissions more reliably than the romance survives the distances.

**Leverage.** Moderate. An adversary who threatened Kareem would move Bruno — not to the extent that Kamala-threat would, but more than any other figure in this section. Kareem is, however, materially capable of defending himself and unlikely to be a soft access point.

---

## 4. ZOE ZIMMER — adversary-turned-friend, low-frequency high-stability

**History.** Introduced *Ms. Marvel* (2014) #1 as the casually-cruel popular classmate whose Islamophobic micro-aggression at the party is the inciting social texture of the series. Bruno's early relationship with Zoe is functional — she shops at the Circle Q, he serves her, they have nothing else. Over the Wilson run she develops, comes out, sheds the early register, and becomes a genuine member of the friend group; in the Ahmed / Saladin eras she is part of the established chosen-family field.

**Dynamics.** Bruno's posture toward Zoe is the clearest single example of his *ethical patience*. He does not punish her for who she was at fourteen. He also does not perform forgiveness; he simply updates his model of her at the rate her behavior changes, and engages with the person in front of him. She, for her part, treats Bruno with a slightly bewildered respect — she has registered that he is the *adult* in the room and does not entirely know what to do with that information.

**Evolution.** Slow-warming over years. Never confidante-level; always *good standing*. By the later eras they are people who will sit at the same diner booth at 1 a.m. and not feel they have to fill the silence.

**Trust / safety.** Stable middle-distance trust. He would tell her facts; he would not tell her feelings. She would not press.

**Failure mode.** Drift. The same risk as Nakia: no one is the initiator.

**Leverage.** Low. She is not a vector by which he can be moved, and an adversary attempting to use her would find she lacks the access required.

---

## 5. MIKE / MICHAELA MILLER — (cross-referenced)

**Cross-reference.** Mike is treated primarily under Relationships I (romantic field). What is relevant here is the *post-romantic-friend* register that persists: Mike remains in Bruno's chosen-family field after the romantic foreclosure, and her presence in his life is one of the small ongoing proofs that he is capable of metabolizing romantic ending into durable friendship without rancor. The decency he showed her *during* the relationship — never weaponizing the Kamala-substrate, never making her the receptacle of a deferred longing she did not earn — is the same decency that lets the friendship survive the ending. *See Relationships I, sub-section 2.*

---

## 6. AAMIR KHAN — quasi-fraternal, intergenerationally-coded

**History.** Kamala's older brother; present across all eras. Bruno has been in the Khan house since middle school and has known Aamir as long as he has known Kamala. The relationship is structurally fraternal — Aamir, more religiously observant and economically precarious in his own way, recognizes in Bruno a fellow over-responsible older-sibling type and treats him as such.

**Dynamics.** Aamir is one of the few people in Bruno's life who *sees the parentification* — recognizes the pattern from the inside, since he is doing a religiously-inflected version of it himself — and treats Bruno with the slightly weary solidarity of a fellow conscript. They do not discuss it in those terms. They simply hand each other tea, watch each other carry things, and occasionally exchange a look across a room when Kamala is doing something rash.

**Evolution.** Steady. Aamir's marriage to Tyesha expands the field; Tyesha and Bruno develop independent low-key warmth. Across the Ahmed/Saladin eras Aamir is one of the *adult-coded* relationships Bruno has in Jersey City and one of the few standing reasons to return.

**Trust / safety.** Quiet, deep, never tested at maximum because never invoked at maximum. He would trust Aamir with Vick if Vick had to be parked somewhere; this is a high bar.

**Failure mode.** They do not initiate; they only *abide*. If geography removes the abiding-in-proximity, the relationship has no engine.

**Leverage.** Low directly; significant indirectly insofar as harm to Aamir would harm Kamala and therefore Bruno via the Kamala channel.

---

## 7. THE INHUMAN / MUTANT COHORT — Lockjaw, Magnificent-era allies, New Mutant teammates

**History.** Bruno's relationship to the broader powered field is structurally distinct from his relationship to people. He treats teleporting bulldogs, sentient swords, and Wakandan academy classmates with the same focused professional warmth he extends to a misbehaving soldering iron: with attention, with curiosity, and without performance.

**Dynamics.** *Lockjaw* in the early Wilson run reads him as safe — animal-pattern recognition of a low-affect-volatility human — and Bruno reciprocates with the practical kindness of a person who has worked retail and knows how to be calm around unpredictable agents. In the Magnificent / New Mutant eras the mutant cohort around Kamala registers Bruno as *the human in the room* in a tone that is half-respectful, half-protective; he does not invite their protection but he does not refuse it either. He is, with X-Men and Inhumans alike, the rare ordinary-human ally who neither resents their power nor idolizes it. They notice. They tend to like him.

**Evolution.** From peripheral civilian in 2014 to *known-reliable* across multiple superhuman polities by the late 2010s. He has standing at Attilan, in Wakanda, and (latterly) with the X-adjacent cohort. None of these standings have been pursued; all have accreted.

**Trust / safety.** Domain-specific. He is trusted to *build*, to *advise*, and to *not-talk* — the third being underrated in this field. He is not in the inner emotional circle of any of these communities, nor does he want to be.

**Failure mode.** Over-utilization. Any sufficiently large powered community will, over time, treat a competent low-drama human technician as infrastructure rather than as a person, and Bruno's defenses are precisely the ones that *invite* this treatment. The Wakanda academy was partly a place that recognized him as a person; some of the later cohorts have not, and he has not protested.

**Leverage.** Distributed and therefore moderate. He has multiple powered communities that would, if asked, intervene on his behalf — which he would never ask. This is operationally significant: his standing protects him in ways he does not know to invoke.

---

## 8. WAKANDAN ACADEMIC MENTORS — first non-familial adults who shaped him

**History.** Established in the Wilson 2017 transfer arc and referenced thereafter. The Wakandan science academy is the first institution in Bruno's life that has *evaluated him as a scientist on his own terms* — not as Kamala's tech support, not as Vick's responsible brother, not as the Circle Q's reliable clerk. The faculty (unnamed in most appearances, gestured at as a cohort) are the first mentors of his life in the proper sense.

**Dynamics.** They give him the thing no one in Jersey City was positioned to give him: *expectation without dependency*. They want him to do good work because the work is good, not because someone needs the work to survive the next Tuesday. This is the most psychologically corrective experience of his post-injury life and is materially responsible for the *professionalized* register he carries into the later eras.

**Evolution.** From overwhelmed transfer student to credentialed practitioner over the academic interval; ongoing correspondence implied if not always shown. He returns to Jersey City a different professional than he left and the difference is the mentorship.

**Trust / safety.** Institutional rather than personal — high trust in the *frame*, moderate-to-warm trust in individual figures. The relationship has the right shape for him precisely because it is not load-bearing on intimacy.

**Failure mode.** Distance and asymmetry of investment — they have many students, he has had few mentors, and the relative weight of the bond is uneven in a direction that does not hurt him because he does not need it to be even.

**Leverage.** Low. The mentors are not vectors. Their gift to him is structural rather than personal and cannot be easily turned.

---

## 9. THE CIRCLE Q OWNERSHIP / NEIGHBORHOOD ADULTS — civilian ground

**History.** The Circle Q owner (under-named in canon; functionally present as employer from middle school onward) is the first adult outside the Carrelli household to give Bruno a regular role, a paycheck, and a place to be that is neither home nor school. Adjacent: the regular customers, the corner-store ecosystem, the Jersey City waterfront neighborhood that knows him by name and face.

**Dynamics.** Low-warmth, high-stability, infrastructure-of-life relationships. The owner trusts him with keys, with closing, with the till; this trust was extended early and never withdrawn. The neighborhood adults — the regulars, the upstairs tenants, the bodega-network across the block — clock him as *one of the reliable young people* and treat him with the particular casual respect older urban residents reserve for the teenagers who have already taken on adult responsibilities.

**Evolution.** Continuous. Even during Wakanda his shifts at the Circle Q are referenced as *held*, the way an adult job is held; he returns to them. The shop is one of the few physical locations in his life that has not changed its meaning across the eras.

**Trust / safety.** Domain-bounded, deep within the domain. He would be trusted by these adults to *manage* — money, the store, a crisis on the block — and would not be trusted (because not invited) into their interior lives. The asymmetry suits him exactly.

**Failure mode.** Erosion by absence. The longer he is away, the more these relationships revert to ambient civic warmth rather than personal recognition. He has accepted this without comment.

**Leverage.** Low individually, distributed. The neighborhood is a *protective* field for him in the older sense — he is *known* there, and known-ness is a low-grade security posture against certain classes of operation against him.

---

## 10. PROTÉGÉS — provisional, latent, structurally inevitable

**History.** Bruno does not yet have formal protégés in the canon as of the most recent runs surveyed. The absence is itself diagnostic: a young man of his technical capacity and ethical seriousness *should*, by his late teens / early twenties, be beginning to teach. He is not. The structural reason is that he is still psychologically organized as the *protégé position himself* — the one being trained, the one being formed, the one whose competence is still being justified to an internal audience that does not yet permit him to occupy the senior chair.

**Latent candidates.**
- *Vick Carrelli.* He has been teaching Vick — life skills, judgment, intermittent technical literacy — since Vick was old enough to receive teaching. This is not formalized as mentorship because the parentified frame forbids the role-recognition. (See Relationships III, family.)
- *Junior members of the mutant / Inhuman cohorts.* In the late-era arcs he is increasingly the person younger powered teenagers come to with technical questions. He answers patiently and without claiming the senior role. The role is forming around him whether he names it or not.
- *Eventual successors at the Circle Q / in the Jersey City civilian field.* The neighborhood teenagers who watch him close the store the way he watched the previous closer do it. The transmission is happening.

**Evolution forecast.** Bruno will become a mentor in his middle twenties whether he intends to or not; the question is whether he will *claim* the role or merely *function in* it. Claiming it would require resolving the parentified self-concept; functioning in it requires nothing and is therefore the more probable path.

**Trust / safety.** Whoever his protégés turn out to be will be unusually well-served. He has the temperamental endowments — patience, technical seriousness, ethical reliability, low ego — that make for a generationally good teacher. His failure mode as a mentor will be the same as his failure mode as a friend: *he will give more than he extracts and will not invoice the difference.*

**Failure mode.** Self-erasure into the protégé's success. He will, if not corrected, make his teaching invisible and thereby deny the protégé the chance to see and refuse the model.

**Leverage.** Currently null; will become substantial as the role consolidates. Future protégés will be high-priority vectors against him precisely because he will not have built defenses against being moved through them — the same architecture that makes Kamala an unsealable channel will make any genuine student of his into one as well.

---

**Section synthesis.** Bruno Carrelli


## Relationships III — Rivals, Enemies & Lovers

# Relationships III — Rivals, Enemies & Lovers

*Subject: Bruno Carrelli. Cross-reference §1 (History), §3 (Psychological), §5 (Personality). This section catalogues those persons who have stood, at any point in the longitudinal record, in adversarial or erotic relation to the subject. Bruno's adversaries are conspicuously few; his lovers are conspicuously fewer; the boundary between "rival" and "intimate" is, in his life, more porous than the file would prefer.*

---

## I. RIVALS

The category itself misfits Bruno. He does not generate rivals — he generates *competitors for shared bandwidth*, which is structurally adjacent but psychologically distinct. A rival, in Bruno's internal map, is anyone whose presence in Kamala Khan's life produces a re-allocation of her attention away from him; the moment he registers this, his trained response is not to compete but to *de-escalate his own claim*. The "rivalries" below are therefore largely one-sided affairs — felt acutely by Bruno, often not recognized by the counterparty as rivalries at all.

### A. Kamran

**History.** Introduced mid-Wilson run as the charming Pakistani-American boy Kamala's family approves of, an Inhuman recruited by Kaboom/Lineage to deliver Kamala to the post-Attilan recruiters. From Bruno's first sighting — at the Khan dinner table, by parental invitation, in a social context Bruno has never been admitted to despite years of friendship — Kamran is encoded as *the thing Bruno is not*: ethnically legible to Kamala's family, culturally fluent, romantically forward, Inhuman, and given the run of a household Bruno has only ever entered through service entrances.

**Dynamics.** Bruno's reaction to Kamran is the most diagnostic single sequence in his romantic record. He does not posture, does not compete, does not surface his own claim. He becomes *more useful* — research on Kamran's background, technical assistance, threat assessment — and silently corrodes. The competence intensifies in exact proportion to the distress; this is the sublimation engine running hot. When Kamran's betrayal is exposed, Bruno does not allow himself the satisfaction of having been right. The "I told you so" is never deployed; the only on-page acknowledgement is a tightened jaw and a faster pivot to the rescue logistics.

**Evolution.** Kamran returns in later runs (notably the *Magnificent* and post-Krakoa eras) in altered moral status, sometimes redeemed, sometimes not. Bruno's posture toward him stabilizes into *cool professional courtesy* — the social mode of a man who has decided that his interior reaction is not the room's business. He does not warm; he does not chill; he treats Kamran as a known quantity to be managed.

**Trust / safety.** Zero erotic-relational threat in current era (Kamala's romantic field has reorganized; Bruno's has too). Residual cognitive threat: Kamran is, for Bruno, the permanent reminder that his own legibility to Kamala's life was always partial. He does not get over this. He stops talking about it.

**Failure mode.** If Kamran were ever again positioned as Kamala's intimate, Bruno's response — based on stable longitudinal pattern — would be to absent himself rather than contest. The withdrawal would be framed as workload, geography, "giving them space." It would be a withdrawal.

**Leverage.** Anyone wishing to displace Bruno from Kamala's inner circle without confrontation need only re-introduce Kamran in a romantically credible configuration. Bruno will move himself.

### B. The Inventor (Thomas Edison clone–cockatiel hybrid)

**History.** Bruno's first adversary of operational scale. The Inventor's recruitment of Vick Carrelli (*Ms. Marvel* 2014 #8–11) collapses Bruno's two organizing concerns — protect Vick, protect Kamala — into a single crisis. The arc ends with Bruno taking a near-lethal energy blast in a warehouse confrontation.

**Dynamics.** The Inventor is, for Bruno, the first time *being smart* is insufficient. Bruno can reverse-engineer the tech, identify the labor pattern, see the scheme — and none of it stops his brother from being inside the cage. The arc trains in him a permanent suspicion of his own cognitive defenses: intellect alone does not save the people he loves. After the Inventor, Bruno's lab work tilts incrementally toward *defensive* engineering (Kamala's suit stabilizers, comms, locators) rather than the exploratory tinkering of the earliest issues.

**Evolution.** Antagonist neutralized; pattern persists. Every subsequent villain-of-the-week — Hijinx, Doc.X, the Lockdown-era ICE-coded enforcers — is processed through the schema the Inventor installed: *what is the labor structure underneath this, who is being used, where is the child in the cage.*

**Trust / safety.** N/A — defeated. Symbolic residue high.

**Failure mode.** The Inventor template (charismatic adult instrumentalizing precarious youth) is the one Bruno cannot see past clearly; he over-rotates toward it. A handler running a non-Inventor-template threat (peer-to-peer, ideological, non-exploitative) might find Bruno late to the read.

**Leverage.** Re-stage a youth-labor exploitation scenario in Jersey City and Bruno will commit before assessing. The Vick wound is unhealed; he will walk into the same warehouse twice.

### C. Josh Richardson

**History.** Zoe Zimmer's on-and-off boyfriend across the Wilson run; jock-coded, Coles Academic peer, generally decent if oblivious. Becomes briefly Inhuman, briefly antagonist-adjacent, briefly hostage-bait.

**Dynamics.** Bruno's "rivalry" with Josh is purely categorical — Josh occupies the *normal high-school boy* slot Bruno's parentified development denied him. They share no significant on-page conflict. Bruno treats Josh with the mild, slightly tired courtesy of someone fifteen years older trapped in the same age cohort.

**Trust / safety.** Neutral. Josh has never read Bruno as competition for anything, which is itself the wound: Bruno is not on the board Josh is playing.

**Failure mode.** None operative.

**Leverage.** None operative. Listed for completeness.

### D. Discovery Channel / Ulysses Cain (proxy adversary, Civil War II)

**History.** Not a person Bruno engages directly; an *epistemic adversary*. Ulysses's predictive profiling is the system Bruno identifies, names, and opposes before Kamala does. The argument over Ulysses is the argument that puts Bruno in the warehouse where his hand is destroyed.

**Dynamics.** This is Bruno's only sustained *ideological* opposition in the record, and it is the most important one. He opposes Ulysses on rights-grounds (see §5: deontological flavor), and he opposes Kamala's deployment of Ulysses on the same grounds, and he is correct on both counts, and he pays for the correctness with his dominant hand. The Ulysses arc is the moment Bruno's worldview crystallizes: institutions that ask people to surrender judgment are the enemy, and the cost of saying so is borne by the body of the one who said so first.

**Trust / safety.** Ulysses is gone; the schema is permanent. Bruno will, for the rest of his life, distrust any system — superhero, governmental, corporate — that promises pre-emptive certainty.

**Failure mode.** Bruno will, if pushed, oppose such systems publicly and unilaterally, and he will not survey the room for backup before doing so. He did not the first time.

**Leverage.** Any predictive-policing, pre-crime, or surveillance-coded apparatus introduced into Kamala's operational theater will trigger Bruno's full opposition stack, including the willingness to absorb personal cost. He has the scar tissue to prove it.

---

## II. ENEMIES

Bruno does not, in the strict sense, *have* enemies — he has people who have hurt him and people he has fought. He generates no personal vendettas, holds no grudges legible to outside observers, and conducts adversarial relationships in the same low-affect register he conducts everything else. The following are persons who have stood, at moments, in a relation to Bruno that crossed the line from opposition into *intent to harm him personally*.

### A. Lineage / Lash / the post-Attilan Inhuman recruiters

**History.** Operatives who attempted to abduct or coerce Kamala via Kamran. Bruno is collateral throughout — beaten, threatened, used as leverage against Kamala.

**Dynamics.** Bruno's body is, in these encounters, *currency*. He is the thing the antagonists hold to extract behavior from Kamala. He registers this and never speaks of it. The somatic effect is a calibration: he begins, post-Attilan-arc, to engineer his own escape kit (lockpicks, micro-tools, the kind of low-visibility infrastructure a hostage builds), and never tells Kamala he has done so. This is the moment Bruno transitions from *helper* to *quietly self-protective operator*. The change is invisible to the rest of the cast.

**Trust / safety.** Hostile actors, neutralized or distant. Schema retained.

**Failure mode.** Bruno will, if taken hostage again, attempt self-extraction before he will permit himself to be used as leverage. He will not radio for help. He will not, if extracted, debrief Kamala on what was done to him.

**Leverage.** His body has been treated as currency by enough antagonists that he has internalized the transaction; any future captor can purchase a great deal of his compliance by threatening *Vick* or *Kamala* rather than *him*.

### B. Doc.X

**History.** Digital antagonist of the Wilson late-run, a viral entity inhabiting devices and persons. Bruno is, by profession, the person in Kamala's circle most exposed to Doc.X — his lab, his comms, his rigs.

**Dynamics.** First adversary Bruno opposes in his *own* operational domain rather than Kamala's. The encounter is a quiet vindication: his technical literacy is the load-bearing element of the defeat. Notable for being one of the few sequences in which Bruno is on-page *competent* in a way the narrative explicitly credits without Kamala mediating it.

**Trust / safety.** Neutralized.

**Failure mode.** Bruno's confidence in his own infrastructure is, post-Doc.X, slightly inflated. He has been compromised once and assumes he will not be again. He will be.

**Leverage.** A sufficiently sophisticated digital adversary can enter Bruno's life through his own workbench, because he no longer fully sandboxes the rigs he builds for Kamala from his personal systems. He has never written this down. It is true.

### C. Becky St. Jude / Lockdown-era enforcers

**History.** *Ms. Marvel* (Wilson, late run): a quasi-fascist youth-vigilante movement in Jersey City, organized around the premise that Ms. Marvel is insufficient and the neighborhood requires harder discipline. Bruno opposes this movement as a citizen of Jersey City as much as a friend of Kamala's.

**Dynamics.** The Lockdown adversaries are the first opponents Bruno encounters who target *the neighborhood itself* as their object of contest. His response is unusually warm by Bruno standards — this is *his* waterfront, *his* bodega, *his* clientele — and he engages with a register of moral anger rarely seen elsewhere in his record. Suggests that the Jersey City attachment is, for Bruno, more affectively loaded than even his attachment to specific persons. Place is, for him, a kind of relative.

**Trust / safety.** Defeated, dispersed. Schema permanent.

**Failure mode.** Any threat to Jersey City as a *place* — gentrification, ICE raids, organized harassment, real-estate predation — will pull Bruno off any other mission. He has not been tested on this; the prediction is high-confidence.

**Leverage.** Threaten the Circle Q, threaten the Khan household block, threaten the Carrelli family's tenuous tenancy, and Bruno is no longer a deliberative agent.

### D. The Inventor's residual network

See §I.B. The Inventor's organizational debris — minor figures who recur as Jersey City small-time antagonists — function as a kind of background hum of opposition. Bruno tracks them without saying so. He has files. The files are not in the cloud.

---

## III. INTIMATES & LOVERS

The smallest category in the record. Three names of significance; two consummated relationships; one love that organized everything and was never named on-page until it could no longer matter.

### A. Kamala Khan — the unconsummated organizing love

**History.** From *Ms. Marvel* (2014) #1 forward. Bruno is in love with Kamala from his first appearance; Kamala is canonically oblivious through the entirety of the Wilson early-to-mid run. He is the first person she reveals her powers to; he is her *Alfred*, her *Oracle*, her ethical sounding board, her engineer, her ride home; he is also, by his own quiet accounting, the boy she does not see.

**Dynamics — pre-injury.** The pattern is fixed by issue #3 and never breaks: Bruno's first question on any Kamala-related stimulus is *"are you okay,"* and his first action is *risk assessment on her behalf*. He does not flirt. He does not posture. He builds — suits, stabilizers, comms, exit routes, alibis, cover stories with her family. The building is the love language; the love language is also the displacement; the displacement is also the actual love. These are not separable in him.

**Dynamics — the confession.** Bruno attempts, across the Civil War II arc, to surface his feelings. The timing is catastrophic: Kamala is already engaged with Bruno-as-conscience on the Ulysses question and cannot metabolize Bruno-as-lover simultaneously. The confession is half-spoken, mis-received, and overtaken by the warehouse. The hand injury arrives in the same operational window as the romantic foreclosure. Bruno does not separate them in his interior accounting and never will. The two losses are *one loss* in his somatic memory: the body that could build for her is gone in the same week as the possibility that the building meant what he wanted it to mean.

**Dynamics — post-injury.** The intimacy *contracts*. Not into hostility — Bruno is incapable of converting Kamala into a hostile object — but into a professionalized warmth, the warmth of a person who has decided that the relationship survives only if he stops asking it to be what it cannot be. He goes to Wakanda. He dates Kareem. He returns. The easy lab-stool intimacy of the early run never returns to full pressure. Both parties notice. Neither names it.

**Dynamics — later eras.** Across Ahmed, Saladin, *Magnificent*, and *The New Mutant*: Bruno is *friend*, not *confidant-primary*. New figures crowd the foreground. Bruno's voice in the room is now the adult-coded one — older than the X-Men, older than Kamala, older than Kamala's parents in some scenes. The love has not extinguished; it has *cooled into a structural feature of his personality*. He will, until he dies, be the person who would have built her anything. He no longer expects, or asks, that this be reciprocated, or even named.

**Trust / safety.** Maximum mutual trust. Asymmetric safety: Kamala is safer with Bruno than Bruno is with Kamala. She has never intended him harm; she has cost him, with appalling consistency, the things he most values, and he has absorbed each cost without invoicing.

**Failure mode.** Bruno's failure mode with Kamala is *self-erasure dressed as maturity*. If she asks him to come, he comes; if she asks him to stay back, he stays back; if she asks for nothing, he provides anyway. The pathological case — already on the record — is geographic flight (Wakanda) as a substitute for the conversation he could not have. A future case in this template will recur if conditions repeat.

**Leverage.** Total. Anyone with sustained operational access to Kamala has, by transitivity, operational access to Bruno. He cannot be coerced through threats to himself; he can be moved at will through threats to her.

### B. Michaela "Mike" Miller — the gentle refuge

**History.** Introduced in the Wilson run as Bruno's girlfriend during the interval in which Kamran is foregrounded with Kamala. Coles peer; warm, witty, observant, a real person not a plot device. Bruno's first and longest fully consummated romantic relationship of the on-page record.

**Dynamics.** The most important fact about Bruno's relationship with Mike is that *it is not bad*. Mike is not a placeholder being mistreated; she is a person Bruno genuinely likes, genuinely respects, and genuinely shows up for. The displacement (see §3) is structurally real — Bruno is dating Mike partly because Kamala is not available — but it is *gentle* displacement. Mike is treated with care, attention, and the same quiet competence Bruno offers everyone he loves. The relationship's failure is not cruelty; it is *thinness*. Bruno is *present* with Mike, but the load-bearing emotional infrastructure of his interior life is in the Kamala-adjacent lab, not the Mike-adjacent date.

**Dynamics — the recognition.** Mike, who is bright, eventually sees this. The relationship's end is conducted with mutual decency — there is no betrayal, no fight, no third-party crisis. Mike names what Bruno cannot, and Bruno does not deny it, and the conversation is short. He thinks about her, longitudinally, with a tenderness the record can detect — Mike is, in his interior accounting, the *evidence that he is capable of being good to someone who chose him*. This is no small thing for him.

**Trust / safety.** Mutual, intact, durable beyond the relationship.

**Failure mode.** Bruno's failure mode with Mike was *not bringing his whole interior into the room*. The defense was unconscious; the cost was hers, mostly, not his. He learned from it. The Kareem relationship is, in part, what Bruno learned from Mike.

**Leverage.** Negligible direct; significant indirect. Anyone wishing to demonstrate to Bruno that he has been emotionally absent in a current relationship can invoke the Mike-template with high effect — he is *susceptible to the accusation of having been not-quite-present*, because he has been, and he knows it.

### C. Kareem / Red Dagger — the partner he chose with both eyes open

**History.** Karachi-based vigilante, introduced as Kamala's Pakistan-arc ally; subsequently re-encountered in the Wakanda/late-Wilson interval. Bruno's relationship with Kareem develops during and after the Wakanda transfer — i.e., during the interval in which Bruno is reconstructing a self-concept that does not depend on Kamala's gaze.

**Dynamics.** The Kareem relationship is, on the longitudinal record, the *healthiest* romantic configuration Bruno has entered. Three structural features distinguish it from the Mike relationship: (1) Kareem is *not* in Bruno's daily orbit — the relationship is conducted across distance and discrete visits, which suits Bruno's containment style without straining it; (2) Kareem is *also* operating in the Kamala-adjacent superhero ecology, which means Bruno does not have to perform normalcy or hide his interior life to be a competent partner; (3) Kareem *pursues* Bruno, which is a novel experience for a person whose lifelong romantic stance has been deferral.

**Dynamics — bisexuality.** The Kareem relationship discloses, on the record, Bruno's bisexuality (or at minimum his capacity for same-sex attachment) without elaborate self-narration. Consistent with his general affective style: it is a fact about him that does not require speech. He does not closet, does not announce, does not theorize. He simply dates Kareem. The unfussiness is itself diagnostic — Bruno's sexual identity, like his disability and his grief, is *integrated rather than narrated*.

**Dynamics — evolution.** The relationship persists, episodically, across the later runs. It is not staged as the great love of his life; it is staged as a *real* relationship in which a real adult is treating Bruno with reciprocity. Whether it endures into long-term partnership is, on the current record, indeterminate. What is determinate: Bruno has demonstrated the capacity to receive care without immediately converting it to debt, and Kareem is the relationship in which this happened.

**Trust / safety.** Mutual, high, distance-mediated.

**Failure mode.** The structural fragility of the Bruno–Kareem configuration is *the distance itself*. Bruno's containment style favors distance; he will not, on his own initiative, close it. If the relationship were to require co-location — Kareem moving to Wakanda or Jersey City, or Bruno to Karachi — Bruno's withdrawal-under-pressure pattern would be tested. Prediction: he would do the move if asked, would do it well, and would silently absorb whatever cost it imposed.

**Leverage.** Through Kareem, modest. Kareem himself is operationally capable and not easily coerced; the Bruno-Kareem link is not a soft target. The more accessible leverage runs the other way — Kareem is one of the few persons through whom Bruno can be *reached emotionally* by another adult who is not Kamala or Vick.

---

## IV. Synthesis — The Pattern Across the Three Categories

Bruno's rivals are people he refuses to compete with; his enemies are people he refuses to hate; his lovers are people he refuses, in two cases of three, to fully arrive for. The through-line is *refusal of escalation* — a temperamental and trained unwillingness to convert interior heat into exterior pressure on another person. In the rival column, this reads as dignity. In the enemy column, this reads as discipline. In the lover column, this reads, on the longitudinal record, as the single most expensive habit of his life.

The operational implication for any handler: Bruno will not, of his own volition, generate adversarial action against a person. He must be *positioned* into opposition by circumstance, and once positioned, he will execute with full competence and no theatrics. He will never tell you why he is doing it. He will never tell you what it cost. The file must therefore be kept by someone else, because Bruno will not keep it on himself — and the central finding of this section is that the absence of self-record is not an absence of injury, it is the *architecture* of the injury, and it is load-bearing on everything else he is.


## Powers, Abilities & Their Limits

# 6. POWERS, ABILITIES & THEIR LIMITS

## 6.0 Threshold Statement

Bruno Carrelli has no powers. This must be stated first because it is the single most operationally relevant fact in his file: he is a non-powered human civilian operating, sustainedly and by choice, inside a theater of Inhumans, mutants, Asgardians, AI predictors, and weaponized child-traffickers. He has been in rooms with the Inventor, Loki, Bruno Horgan's intellectual descendants, Kree, and a national-security apparatus running a precognitive analytic on American teenagers. In every one of those rooms his contribution has materially altered the outcome. The asymmetry — what he produces versus what he is constituted to produce — is the central anomaly of his file and must be read as such.

The catalog below is therefore not a power-set audit. It is a competence audit, longitudinally tracked, with attention to (a) the substrate skill, (b) its specific applications in canon, (c) the ceiling and the failure modes, (d) the way each competence has shifted across the pre-injury / post-injury / Wakanda / professionalized eras, and (e) the way the skill *means* something about the man — the symptom-as-signature reading that closes each subsection.

---

## 6.1 Applied Engineering — Bespoke Fabrication

**Mechanism.** Bruno is a working bench engineer of unusual range for his age. From *Ms. Marvel* (2014) #2 forward he is depicted prototyping in a back-room lab improvised behind the Circle Q and, later, in a school chem-lab he has effectively annexed, and later still in proper Wakandan facilities. Materials competence spans low-voltage electronics, basic chemistry (he synthesizes a polymer compound sufficient to bind to Kamala's morphogenic cell structure — non-trivial biochemistry for a high-schooler), small-scale mechanical assembly, soldering, microcontroller programming, and embedded systems. He works from first principles, not from kits.

**Range.** The bench is the unit. He does not design at scale, does not work in CAD-to-fab industrial pipelines pre-Wakanda, and does not appear to have formal training in any specific engineering discipline before transfer. His range is *what one bright kid with a soldering iron and access to a Jersey City community college's discarded equipment can do.* Post-Wakanda this expands by an order of magnitude — he gets real instrumentation, real materials, real mentorship.

**Signature application: the Kamala-suit.** The custom polymer-weave costume that survives Kamala's embiggening/shrinking transformations is the canonical demonstration. It is a non-trivial materials problem — most fabrics either tear or constrict under the strain her morphogenesis applies — and Bruno solves it iteratively, on a high-school budget, with feedback loops from a single user. He also fabricates her communicator earpieces, location trackers, and a series of one-off gadgets keyed to specific missions (the Inventor arc; the Lockdown arc).

**Ceiling.** He is not Tony Stark, not Riri Williams, not Peter Parker at his web-fluid peak. He is *better than realistic for a Jersey City public-school kid* and *not magical*. He does not invent new physics. His designs are recognizably extensions of available tech, executed with unusual craft.

**Limits, post-injury.** The hand injury (CWII, 2016) is precisely targeted at this competence. Loss of fine motor control in the dominant hand attacks soldering, micro-assembly, manual circuit work — the exact gestures the bench requires.
