He adapts: depicted in subsequent issues working with the brace, using clamps and jigs where freehand once sufficed, verbally directing collaborators' hands (a learned skill, observable in lab scenes from Wilson's late run and Ahmed's run). Output volume drops; output quality recovers slower than volume; the *speed* of iteration — once his signature — never fully returns.

**Symptom-as-signature.** Every gadget he has ever made has been for someone else. There is no on-page artifact of Bruno building something *for himself* — no personal project, no hobby fabrication, no thing he made because he wanted it to exist. The bench is a service. The injury that maimed his service-capacity was suffered while preventing someone he loved from making an ethical mistake. The tool is the man and the man is the tool, and when the tool was damaged he changed continents rather than be a damaged tool in the same room as the person he had been a tool for.

---

## 6.2 Applied Chemistry / Biochemistry

**Mechanism.** Sub-skill of the above but worth isolating. Bruno's polymer work on the Kamala-suit requires real understanding of how a material can interface with a morphogenetic system — he is iterating against a biology none of the literature describes. He also handles improvised pharmacology adjacent to the Inventor arc and demonstrates baseline familiarity with reagent safety, controlled reactions, and the ethics of testing-on-friends (he is visibly uncomfortable with the one-subject sample size and says so).

**Range and ceiling.** Sufficient for the problems put in front of him; not a research chemist. He does not publish, does not synthesize novel compounds for their own sake, and does not show interest in chemistry as a vocation distinct from its instrumental use to Kamala's operations. Wakanda exposure broadens this — he learns formal lab discipline he was operating without.

**Symptom-as-signature.** The fact that his biochemistry was developed for *one user* tells the whole story. He has a sample size of one because he has an audience of one. The competence is intimate before it is scientific.

---

## 6.3 Software / Embedded Systems / Network Work

**Mechanism.** Bruno writes code at a level competent for embedded device firmware, basic network manipulation, and small-scale data work. He has, on-page, traced signals, built tracker firmware, jury-rigged communicator protocols, and at least once tapped into security feeds at a level that is plausibly possible for a determined teenager with no formal training. He is not a black-hat in the Doreen Green / Mockingbird sense; he is a *capable maker who has had to learn enough software to make his hardware do what it needs to.*

**Range and ceiling.** Limited. He is not breaking SHIELD-grade encryption. He is not running offensive cyber operations. He gets into systems that a high-school student plausibly gets into and writes code that runs on the boards he solders.

**Limits, post-injury.** Interestingly, software work is *less* damaged by the hand injury than hardware work — typing is coarser-motor than soldering — and there is a small observable drift in canon toward more software, more direction, more design-on-paper-then-handed-to-others as his output mix in the post-injury era. The hand pushed him uphill into systems work.

**Symptom-as-signature.** He learns the next layer of the stack when the previous one becomes painful. Adaptation as substitution rather than grief.

---

## 6.4 Operational Intelligence — The Oracle Function

**Mechanism.** This is the under-rated competence and arguably his most valuable. Bruno runs *real-time mission support* for Kamala across the Wilson run: monitoring her position, parsing feeds, predicting failure modes, talking her through decisions while she is in the field. The pattern is functionally identical to Oracle for Birds of Prey or Felicia Hardy for various, with the difference that Bruno is sixteen and self-taught and does it from a convenience store back room.

**Sub-skills.** Spatial reasoning over a Jersey City street map he knows by foot; threat parsing from incomplete information; rapid scenario branching ("if you go in the front, the structural column will not support a shrink-then-embiggen there — try the loading dock"); and the *moral* sub-routine that is the heart of his Oracle function: he will refuse to relay an instruction he disagrees with, and he will say so.

**Range and ceiling.** Excellent within Jersey City. Less reliable outside familiar geography. He is information-bottlenecked — what he can see is what someone has thought to send him, and he does not have surveillance infrastructure of his own. Post-Wakanda this expands; the infrastructure becomes available.

**Limits.** He is one person at one console. He cannot run two operations at once. He cannot replace himself. The single-point-of-failure problem is structural to his entire mode and he has never solved it because *being the single point of failure is what he is for.*

**Symptom-as-signature.** The voice in her ear, telling her the truth, including the truths she does not want to hear. He paid the cost of being right about Ulysses with his hand. The Oracle function never lost the willingness to be right at cost. After the injury it lost only the *insistence* — he will tell you the truth once and then let you do what you will do.

---

## 6.5 De-escalation and Conflict Management

**Mechanism.** From his first on-page appearance — defusing Zoe/Kamala over halal in *Ms. Marvel* (2014) #1 — Bruno is depicted as a competent verbal de-escalator. The skill set is recognizable: low-volume voice, deliberate body language (artists consistently draw him leaning slightly back, hands visible, palms-down rather than palms-up — a *calming* posture rather than a *submissive* one), and a tendency to re-frame conflicts into shared-problem language ("look, what do you actually need here?"). The Circle Q is implicitly a training ground — retail desk in a diverse neighborhood, sole adult-coded employee, has been doing this since middle school.

**Range.** Functional from family scale (Vick, repeatedly) up to small-group scale (school halls, party situations, low-grade street confrontations). Does not scale to *combat* de-escalation — he is not pulling weapons out of hostage situations, and on the occasions he has tried to intervene in genuinely violent confrontations he has been hurt.

**Symptom-as-signature.** He learned to settle rooms because his household needed settling. The skill is a parentified-child skill before it is a retail skill. He uses it as freely with strangers as with family because for him *there is no off-duty.*

---

## 6.6 Caregiving and Sibling-Management

**Mechanism.** Distinct competence, separately observable. Bruno manages Vick with a specific repertoire: he covers for him with the parents, runs interference with school, retrieves him from situations Vick has put himself in, and — diagnostically — does *not* lecture after the fact. The post-rescue conversation, when it appears, is brief and forward-looking. He has learned that lecturing does not change Vick and only damages the relationship.

**Range.** Optimized for Vick specifically; transferable to other caregiving contexts (he is patient with Kamala's parents in the limited scenes he shares with them; later, gentle with Kareem during their relationship).

**Limits.** The asymmetry is unsustainable and Bruno knows it on some level but cannot stop. He is not, on the page, ever depicted *requiring* care from Vick or anyone in his family. The traffic is one-way.

**Symptom-as-signature.** Care without reciprocity is the family operating system; he ports it everywhere.

---

## 6.7 Ethical Pattern-Recognition

**Mechanism.** This is the competence that most distinguishes Bruno from a generic smart-teen-sidekick archetype. He sees the *moral* shape of a situation faster than the heroes around him. He names the predictive-profiling problem in the Ulysses arc before Kamala does, in plain ethical language; he reads the labor structure of the Inventor's operation early; he is consistently the voice that asks who is paying the cost of an apparently elegant solution.

**Mechanism, finer.** Deontological by default — he reasons in rights-language, not consequences-language. Asks "who is having something done to them, and did they consent" before he asks "what is the net outcome." This is consistent across arcs and across writers, which suggests it is a *real* feature of the character rather than a writer-specific flourish.

**Range and ceiling.** Excellent at identifying the problem; less reliably good at proposing alternatives. He is a critic more than an architect at the ethical level — he can tell you what is wrong and why, but his constructive proposals tend to be small-scale ("don't do it, then") rather than systemic. This is a real limit, and it is the limit that cost him his hand: identifying the wrong action was not, in that moment, sufficient to prevent it.

**Symptom-as-signature.** His ethical clarity is purchased with social cost. He is willing to be the unpopular voice in the room and willing to pay for it. The willingness does not abate after the injury — it is the *insistence* that abates. He still sees, still says, but says it once.

---

## 6.8 Linguistic, Cultural, and Religious Literacy

**Mechanism.** Bruno is genuinely culturally fluent — he understands Kamala's family context, halal practice, Pakistani-Muslim social grammar, sufficiently to operate inside it without performance or condescension. He learned this on the ground, by being Kamala's friend since middle school. He extends the same fluency to other contexts with reasonable speed (Wakanda assimilation is not effortless but is not flailing). His own Catholic-Italian-American substrate sits lightly — he has the moral grammar without the church practice — which means he is not defending a worldview when he meets others'.

**Range.** Strong within the specific cultural settings he has lived inside. Not magical; he does not, e.g., become a sudden Wakandan expert. He learns by paying attention over time.

**Symptom-as-signature.** Cultural literacy as a function of attentive listening to specific people. He is fluent in Kamala because he has been listening to Kamala for years.

---

## 6.9 Endurance, Pain Tolerance, and the Body as Asset

**Mechanism.** Bruno has been beaten, kidnapped, threatened at gunpoint, blast-injured, and put in chronic-sleep-deprivation states across years of canon. His baseline pain tolerance reads as high, but the more diagnostic feature is his *narration* of pain — there is essentially none. He does not name his pain on-page even in solo scenes (back-of-store, alone, holding the injured hand). The body is treated as instrument: an instrument can be damaged but is not, in his internal account, a *self* that suffers.

**Range.** Ordinary human. He has no enhanced healing, no augmented threshold, no special training. He breaks the way humans break. He just does not *say so.*

**Limits.** The instrument has been permanently degraded once. There is no reason to think it could not be again, and his behavioral pattern offers no protection against this — he will still step in front of the blast.

**Symptom-as-signature.** A body owned by its uses. The hand was the most-used part of the instrument and it was the part that was taken. The grief that has never been spoken is sitting in the brace.

---

## 6.10 Growth Curve, By Era

- **Pre-canon to Wilson early (2014).** Established skill: retail competence, sibling management, baseline electronics. Latent: most of the engineering range.
- **Wilson mid-run (2014–2016).** Rapid expansion: gadget fabrication, polymer chemistry, embedded systems, Oracle function. Peak per-hour output. Sleep curtailment severe.
- **Civil War II / post-injury (2016).** Acute degradation of fine-motor work. Identity crisis sub-vocal. Compensation begins immediately — clamps, jigs, verbal direction.
- **Wakanda (2017–).** Formalization: real training, real instrumentation, real peers. Skill *broadens* (formal lab discipline, exposure to advanced materials science) even as the per-hand output remains below pre-injury peak. New attachment (Kareem) supports re-stabilization.
- **Ahmed / Saladin / Magnificent / New Mutant era (2019–present).** Professionalized steady state. He is the adult-coded technician in rooms full of X-Men. Output is reliable, considered, less frenetic. Oracle function is offered rather than insisted upon. The Wakanda training is integrated; the Jersey City scrappiness is preserved.

The shape of the growth curve is *not* monotonic-upward. It is rising, then sharply notched at 2016, then resuming on a different and gentler slope, with the slope's gentleness itself diagnostic — he is no longer racing to be everything for one person.

---

## 6.11 Failure Modes and Operational Risks

- **Single point of failure.** He has never built a successor or trained a backup. Lose Bruno, lose the function.
- **Self-erasure under load.** He will accept disproportionate cost without flagging it; a handler relying on him should assume his reports understate his strain by a factor.
- **Retreat as resolution.** When a situation becomes untenable he will exit it geographically rather than confront it. Operationally this means: if he disappears, look for the situation he is exiting, not the place he went.
- **Cannot weaponize the relationship.** Will not guilt, will not leverage, will not collect debts. This is an ethical strength and an operational asymmetry — counterparties who *do* weaponize will extract value from him at terms unfavorable to him every time.
- **Refusal to relay against conscience.** Operationally a feature, not a bug; counterparties who want a compliant Oracle will be disappointed. The Ulysses arc is the template.
- **The hand.** Any task requiring sustained dominant-hand fine motor work has a degraded ceiling. Any further injury to the remaining functional hand, or to vision, or to cognition, would hit a self-concept already running thin on substrate.

---

## 6.12 Synthesis

Bruno Carrelli's power is the *exact thing* his psychology says it would be: the capacity to make, fix, see, and steady — on behalf of others, at his own cost, without naming the cost. There is no ability in his catalog that exists for his own benefit. Every competence is a competence-for. The hand injury is therefore not a peripheral biographical event but a structural attack on the only self he has ever allowed himself to have: the self that is *useful to her*. That he survived the attack without psychiatric decompensation, that he rebuilt the skill set on a different continent, that he came back and resumed the function in a quieter register — these are the operational facts. The unspoken question riding underneath them is the one §3 already posed and §6 only sharpens: a person whose every ability is in service to a bond he cannot claim, whose body has already been spent once on that bond, and who has shown no capacity to refuse the next call — what is the load ceiling, and what happens at it. The file does not yet know. The file is watching.


## Operational Profile & Tradecraft

# OPERATIONAL PROFILE & TRADECRAFT — SUBJECT: BRUNO CARRELLI

**Classification:** Civilian technical asset. Non-combatant. Embedded support node, Jersey City theater (2014–c. 2017), subsequently distributed (Wakanda Design Group academy, intermittent JC presence, c. 2017–present). Operational posture: defensive, infrastructural, and consistently *under*-leveraged relative to capability. Self-presentation calibrated to read as a competent teenage shop clerk who happens to be good with electronics; actual capability envelope materially exceeds that presentation, and the gap is itself a tradecraft choice.

---

## 1. DECISION-MAKING ARCHITECTURE

Bruno's decision process is **slow on the front end, fast on the back end** — the inverse of the heroes he supports. Where Kamala Khan operates by impulse and self-corrects in motion, Bruno commits time to upstream analysis (whiteboard, notebook, lab bench) and then executes in a single decisive movement with little revisiting. He does not iterate publicly. He is not seen, at any point in the longitudinal record, *brainstorming* with another person in the way Kamala does; he brainstorms alone and presents conclusions.

The decision tree, reconstructed across roughly a decade of observed behavior, runs in a consistent order:

1. **Threat-to-Kamala assessment.** Every decision is filtered first through the question *does this make her safer or less safe*. This is pre-cognitive at this point; he does not appear to know he is doing it.
2. **Ethical screen.** Once the safety filter is satisfied, he runs a deontological check: *does the proposed action violate a rights-based principle I can name*. He does not run consequentialist arithmetic; he has been observed in *Ms. Marvel* (2015) #8–12 explicitly rejecting the Ulysses-profiling logic on the grounds that *outcomes don't redeem the method*. This is unusually clean moral reasoning for a teenager and indicates a stable internal code rather than situational ethics.
3. **Technical feasibility.** Can he build, fix, or improvise the means inside the time window. Bruno is realistic about his ceiling — he does not overpromise — but the ceiling he acknowledges is several tiers above what his peers credit him with.
4. **Cost-to-self ledger, suppressed.** He runs this ledger silently and then *systematically discounts the value of his own entries.* This is the tradecraft flaw a hostile handler would exploit: Bruno will sign off on a plan whose costs to him are clearly disproportionate because he does not believe his own costs count for as much as the costs to others.
5. **Execute, do not announce.** Once decided, he moves. He does not request permission; he frequently does not even inform Kamala until the action is in motion or complete. The Vick-extraction sequence (*Ms. Marvel* 2014 #8–11) is the canonical example: he handled the situation alone for weeks before bringing it to Kamala, and only then because the operational geometry forced disclosure.

**Decision speed under acute stress:** very fast and very correct. The hand injury sequence (*Ms. Marvel* 2015 #12, Civil War II crossover) shows him making a body-interposition decision in roughly the time it takes Kamala to finish a sentence. Note that this fast decision is *consistent with* his slow upstream analysis — he had already run the moral math on Ulysses-profiling weeks earlier; the in-the-moment choice was a cached execution of a long-prepared judgment.

---

## 2. METHODS & TRADECRAFT

### 2.1 Cover and Concealment

Bruno's primary cover is *being underestimated*. The Circle Q apron, the slouch, the quiet register-clerk affect — these are not performances exactly, but he does not correct the misread when civilians, classmates, or threats assume the apron describes the man. Zoe Zimmer reads him as the shy boy. Vick's associates read him as the soft brother. The Inventor's cell reads him as a non-threat right up until he has reverse-engineered their hardware. This is **passive cover** — he does not lie about what he is; he simply allows the visible role to absorb the inquiry.

He is, accordingly, very bad at *active* deception (lying to Kamala's parents on her behalf reads as visibly uncomfortable, *Ms. Marvel* 2014 #6, #14) and very good at *omission* (he can withhold a fact indefinitely, especially about himself).

### 2.2 Communications

- **Primary channel with Kamala:** in-person, then text. He prefers text to voice — text gives him time to compose, lets him drop a fact without managing his face, and allows him to terminate a thread by not responding. Voice calls he uses only for active operations.
- **OPSEC discipline:** above peer-baseline but well below professional. He uses code phrases inconsistently; he is aware of cameras in the Circle Q but treats his own apartment and the school lab as effectively unobserved (a known vulnerability — Jersey City is not a clean signals environment). After Wakanda exposure he upgrades sharply: his post-2017 communications show evidence of disciplined channel separation (Wakandan academy comms held strictly separate from Jersey City civilian channels).
- **Written record:** keeps engineering notebooks — paper, gridded, dated. These are his primary externalization; emotional content does not appear in them, but design iterations, failure modes, and small marginal annotations to himself ("don't use this on K — heat") do. A surveillance team that obtained one notebook would learn more about his cognition than from a year of his speech.

### 2.3 Surveillance and Counter-Surveillance

Bruno is not a trained operator and does not run formal counter-surveillance. However, he has a strong **environmental baseline** for Jersey City: he knows the Circle Q's sight lines, the back-alley exits along the waterfront blocks, the timing of the PATH and the light rail, the regular customers and their schedules. He notices when something is *off* in his home territory and is reliably the first member of the Khan-adjacent circle to flag a tail, a vehicle out of pattern, or a face that has appeared twice. In unfamiliar territory (Wakanda early on, off-continent excursions in the Ahmed run) this advantage collapses and he becomes an ordinary observer.

He does not sweep for bugs. He does not vary his routes deliberately. His route-variance is incidental, driven by errands rather than tradecraft, which makes him **highly predictable** to a competent surveillant — Circle Q, home, school, lab, repeat, with the lab being the variable that absorbs late hours.

### 2.4 Physical Tradecraft

Bruno does not carry weapons. He is not trained in any combat discipline and does not pretend to be. In confrontations he has been observed to (a) attempt verbal de-escalation first, (b) interpose his body second, (c) improvise a tool from the environment third. He has never been observed to throw the first punch and has never been observed to flee a confrontation in which a person he is responsible for remains in danger. This is operationally **reliable but exploitable** — a kidnapper need only threaten Kamala or Vick to acquire him.

Lock-and-key: competent with electronic locks (he can defeat most consumer-grade systems given five minutes and a multimeter), indifferent with mechanical. He does not pick locks for sport; the skill is incidental to his electronics work.

---

## 3. TECHNICAL CAPABILITY & TOOLKIT

This is the section where the apron stops describing the man.

**Domain:** applied electrical engineering and chemistry, with strong polymath spread into materials, biology-adjacent instrumentation, and embedded software. Self-taught augmented by formal coursework (Coles Academic High School, then Wakanda Design Group academy under post-2017 placement). His Wakandan placement is itself a credential — that academy does not accept the merely promising.

**Signature work-products in the operational record:**

- **Polymer/elastic adaptation for Kamala's costume** (early Wilson run): bespoke fabric work allowing her morphogenesis to coexist with clothing integrity. Non-trivial materials problem; he solved it as a teenager in a back room.
- **Embiggening-stabilizer prototypes**: small wearables and pocket devices intended to dampen, monitor, or augment Kamala's polymorph control. Iterative; some failed in field (the Civil War II warehouse device's failure is partly what put him in the blast radius).
- **Communications and tracking** for Kamala in-field: improvised earpieces, location beacons, encrypted local relay. Built from civilian parts because procurement of restricted parts would draw attention to his work.
- **Counter-Inventor hardware analysis** (*Ms. Marvel* 2014 #8–11): reverse-engineered the Inventor's recruitment-tech well enough to identify pattern of operation, which is the basis on which Kamala located the cell.
- **Lab discipline:** logs everything, labels everything, dates everything. Cleans his own glassware. Does not leave a soldering iron on. The bench is the one area of his life where his control is total and visible.

**Tool ecosystem:** modest. A soldering station, a hand-built oscilloscope (or a school-borrowed one), multimeters, a 3D printer of compromised quality, and whatever the Circle Q's back room can be made to hold. Pre-Wakanda he is famously *resource-poor* — most of his significant outputs were built on a budget that would not fund a hobbyist. **Post-Wakanda** his tool envelope expands by orders of magnitude (vibranium-adjacent fabrication, real instrumentation), and the change is visible in the precision of his subsequent gifts back to Kamala.

**The hand.** Post-injury he has restructured his workflow around the dominant-hand deficit:
- One-handed manipulation with the unaffected hand for fine work, with the injured hand stabilizing.
- Voice-directed assistants where available (significant uplift in Wakanda).
- Greater reliance on simulation and pre-build modeling, less on tactile iteration.
- Slower bench-to-prototype cycle by a factor he has not announced but which is visible in dated work-product comparisons.

He has not retrained the non-dominant hand to full prior fine-motor capacity and does not appear to be attempting it; he has accepted the new envelope and routed around it. This is mature engineering and a small grief.

---

## 4. INFRASTRUCTURE

**Physical nodes (longitudinal):**

- **Circle Q convenience store, Jersey City waterfront.** Primary node 2014–c.2017. Shift work; back room used as ad-hoc lab and storage. Functions as informal community signals hub — Kamala-adjacent traffic routes through here.
- **Carrelli family residence, Jersey City.** Working-class apartment, fragile household. Bruno's bedroom doubles as second-stage workshop. He does not bring operationally sensitive work home for fear of Vick.
- **Coles Academic High School lab.** Tertiary node; off-hours access via faculty trust earned through visible competence.
- **Wakanda Design Group academy.** Post-2017 primary technical node. Capability envelope ratchets up sharply. Bruno's posture within it is junior-respected — he is not the prodigy of the cohort but he is consistently the one whom instructors trust to finish.
- **Kareem's orbit in Karachi.** Tertiary social/operational node post-relationship onset; he is a guest, not a principal there.

**Information infrastructure:** notebooks (paper), a personal laptop kept on his person or in a known cache, a phone, cloud storage of modest sophistication. He has never been observed running a server, maintaining anonymized accounts, or operating in adversarial networks. His digital footprint is consistent with a serious high-school engineering student and slightly understated for one — he posts little, comments less, leaves a small surface.

**Social infrastructure (the asset network he can call on, ranked by reliability):**

1. Kamala Khan — total, but he will not call.
2. Aamir, Yusuf, and Muneeba Khan — high, via Kamala, but requires the most trust-cost transaction.
3. Nakia Bahadir — moderate-high; she trusts him independently.
4. Mike Miller — high in domain of personal support, moderate in operational; he does not put her near danger.
5. Kareem (Red Dagger) — high, particularly post-Wakanda; some operational reach via Karachi.
6. Wakandan academy faculty/peers — moderate; institutional rather than personal.
7. Vick — high in *will*, low in *reliability*; he will show up and may make it worse.
8. Zoe Zimmer — low-moderate; she is fond of him and would not refuse a small ask.

The network is **deep but narrow** — he has very few weak ties, which is itself a tradecraft limitation. He cannot, for example, summon a stranger; he cannot leverage a community he hasn't already given to.

---

## 5. FINANCES

Bruno's financial profile is **thin, clean, and disciplined.**

- **Income (pre-Wakanda):** Circle Q wages, paid hourly, almost certainly under-the-table for at least part of his tenure given his age at hire. He has been working since middle school.
- **Disbursement:** majority into household contribution (rent, utilities, Vick-related costs absorbed silently) and into his materials budget. Personal discretionary spending is near-zero. He does not buy clothes, does not eat out, does not subscribe.
- **Materials budget:** sustained at the cost of personal consumption. He buys components in small lots, often used, often through hobbyist channels.
- **Post-Wakanda:** academy stipend and access to in-kind resources radically expand his materials envelope without changing his personal spending pattern. He has not been observed to upgrade his clothing, his phone, or his living habits in response to changed circumstance. The ratio of resources-deployed-for-others to resources-deployed-for-self remains roughly the same; only the absolute scale has changed.
- **No debt of record, no investments, no signs of money flow inconsistent with stated income.** A financial audit would find nothing. He is, in this domain as in most, exactly what he appears to be plus a margin of quiet competence.

---

## 6. PATTERNS OF ACTION

**Daily-cycle baseline (pre-Wakanda, Wilson-era):** wake early, school, Circle Q shift, lab/workshop, late return home, sleep curtailed. Weekends collapse the school slot and expand the workshop slot. The cycle is *relentless* — there are no days off in the visible record.

**Operational cycle when Kamala is active:** he is on standby continuously. He does not sleep through a Ms. Marvel emergency; he is reachable. He pre-positions tools and information; he does not wait to be asked before beginning to think about a problem.

**Crisis-response sequence (repeatable across the record):**

1. Acquire situational data, often by listening rather than asking.
2. Identify the technical bottleneck.
3. Begin fabrication or analysis without announcement.
4. Surface only when his contribution is ready *or* when he has identified a problem the principals have not seen.
5. Deliver; do not narrate the cost of delivery.
6. After-action: clean up, restock, and resume baseline. He does not debrief. He does not request acknowledgment.

**Long-cycle pattern:** Bruno can sustain extraordinary operational tempo for long periods without complaint, but the longitudinal record shows that *he breaks by exit, not by collapse.* When the cost has accumulated past a threshold he cannot articulate, he removes himself from the theater (Wakanda, 2017). This is the most important pattern for any handler: he will not signal exhaustion in time to prevent the departure.

---

## 7. SIGNATURE OPERATIONAL TELLS

The following are the small, granular markers that a surveillance file would catalog as Bruno-specific:

- **The pre-speech pause.** Before saying anything difficult — moral, romantic, or operational — Bruno opens his mouth, closes it, and only then speaks. The pause is roughly half a second and is the single most consistent tell across the entire decade of canon. It is the visible surface of the upstream-analysis habit.
- **Hand-care behaviors (post-2016).** Unconsciously flexes the injured hand; rubs the thumb across the palm under stress; tucks the injured hand into a pocket or behind his back when meeting someone new. Wears a brace or glove inconsistently — more in cold, more when fatigued.
- **The lab-cleanup tell.** When he is upset and does not want to discuss it, he cleans his workspace. The cleaning is meticulous and out of cycle. A clean bench at the wrong time is, for him, the diagnostic for an undisclosed grief.
- **The text-drafted-and-not-sent.** Phone forensics would consistently show a high ratio of typed-but-deleted drafts. He composes the thing he will not send.
- **Eye-contact asymmetry.** Sustains direct eye contact when speaking *about a problem*; breaks eye contact when speaking *about himself*. The break is downward and slightly to his left.
- **The Kamala-shaped silence.** In any group conversation about her, Bruno speaks last and speaks least, regardless of how much he knows. This is a deliberate operational habit (do not be the source of information about her) that has hardened into a personality trait.
- **The "are you okay" preface.** His near-invariant opener to Kamala when she has been in the field, dating to *Ms. Marvel* (2014) #3. It functions as both genuine inquiry and signal-check: her response tone tells him what kind of evening it will be.
- **Order-of-operations in a workshop emergency.** Safety check first (people, then materials), diagnosis second, fix third, cleanup fourth, documentation last but never skipped. Consistent across years. He has never been observed to skip documentation, even when injured.
- **Refusal of food offered casually, acceptance of food offered with explanation.** He will turn down a snack pressed on him ("no, I'm good") and accept the same snack if the offerer explains why they have extra. This is the parentified-child receiving-pattern: he cannot accept being given to, only being relieved of someone else's surplus.
- **The withdrawal-as-decision tell.** When Bruno has decided to remove himself from a situation, his behavior in the days before announcement is *more* attentive, *more* helpful, *more* present — he closes out his obligations before he leaves. A sudden increase in his availability is, paradoxically, the strongest indicator that he is about to be unavailable.

---

## 8. EXPLOITABLE VULNERABILITIES (DEFENSIVE NOTE)

For the purpose of this dossier — and explicitly oriented toward *protection* of the subject rather than leverage against him — the following are the vectors a hostile actor would attempt:

- **Threat to Kamala, Vick, or now Kareem/Mike.** He will comply with almost any demand routed through a credible threat to one of these. He has no training in resisting this.
- **Offer of *being needed* by a competent adversary.** A hostile actor presenting as a person in genuine distress with a technical problem would acquire substantial cooperation before Bruno's ethical screen caught up.
- **Sustained low-grade flattery of his competence is ineffective.** He does not respond to this. Sustained *use* of his competence, with visible gratitude routed through outcomes rather than words, is highly effective.
- **Removal of his ability to build.** Any further degradation of his hand, eyesight, or workshop access would strike the load-bearing beam of his self-concept and produce effects disproportionate to the physical injury.
- **Forcing him to receive care publicly.** He has no defended response to this and would likely exit the situation rather than navigate it.

---

## 9. SUMMARY

Bruno Carrelli operates as a **deliberately under-leveraged technical and ethical infrastructure node** in a theater dominated by superhuman action. His tradecraft is the tradecraft of a person who has never named himself an operator: passive cover, slow-then-fast decision making, mature defensive ethics, modest tooling deployed with disproportionate skill, financial and digital cleanliness, and a network that is deep where it exists and absent where it doesn't. He executes well, documents everything, announces nothing, and pays his costs out of an account he does not let others audit. The operational risk he poses is essentially zero. The operational risk *to* him is concentrated almost entirely in the people he loves and in the hands he uses to love them through.


## Worldview & Operational Code

# WORLDVIEW & OPERATIONAL CODE — BRUNO CARRELLI

**File note.** What follows is the full reconstruction of Bruno Carrelli's belief structure as it can be triangulated from a decade of observed behavior, recorded speech, and decisional pattern. He has never authored a manifesto; he is not a person who narrates his philosophy. The code below is *derived* — assembled from how he chooses when no one is watching him choose, what he refuses to do even when refusing costs him, what kinds of problems he reaches for first, and what kinds of arguments he wins and loses against himself.

---

## 1. METAPHYSICAL FLOOR — WHAT HE BELIEVES THE WORLD IS

**The world is mostly mechanism, partly mystery, and almost entirely fixable in small pieces.** Bruno operates from an essentially *engineering* metaphysics: phenomena have causes, causes have structures, structures can be modeled, models can be intervened upon. This holds even when the phenomenon is a friend who can stretch her arm across a parking lot — Terrigenesis, for him, is a *biological process* before it is a wonder, and his first instinct on seeing Kamala morphed is to ask after her body's parameters, not to gasp. The numinous does not paralyze him; it gets a workbench.

This is not scientism in the brittle sense. He has watched too much that is *not* mechanism — Inhuman emergence, Wakandan tradition, his own family's irrational affection — to flatten the world into circuitry. What he believes, more precisely, is that **the unexplained is unexplained-yet** and that the responsible posture is to act as if it has structure while remaining humble about not yet seeing it. He is, in temperament, closer to a Catholic-trained empiricist than to a Silicon Valley positivist: there is room in his frame for things larger than himself, but those things do not excuse him from doing the next correct small thing.

**Residual Catholic substrate.** Confession, penance, the dignity of work, the gravity of *intention*, and — most operationally — the conviction that the *interior act* matters even when no one sees it. He does not practice. He has not been observed at Mass in canonical depiction. But the moral grammar is unmistakable: he believes that what you do alone, in a back room, soldering at 2am for someone who will never know how many hours it took, is **the form your character actually has**. Public credit is not the unit of moral accounting.

**On time.** He treats time as a *finite engineering resource*, not as an existential horizon. His default question is not "what is life for" but "what can I get done before the next thing breaks." This is a worldview perfectly calibrated to parentified adolescence and one of the deeper reasons he does not, in canon, sit still long enough to grieve.

---

## 2. EPISTEMOLOGY — HOW HE DECIDES WHAT IS TRUE

**Empirical-first, with strong deference to first-person testimony from trusted sources.** Bruno will run a test before he will accept an assertion, but he will also accept Kamala's word about her own body, her own family, her own moral intuition, faster than he will accept his own derivation. Trust, for him, is an *epistemic instrument* — the people he trusts give him access to data he could not reach alone.

**He does not trust prediction.** This is the central epistemic conviction of his life, and the Ulysses arc made it explicit: a probability over a person is not a fact about that person. He intuits, ahead of most of the heroic apparatus around him, that **predictive systems launder bias into the appearance of inevitability**, and that any operational code built on them will eventually punish someone for a crime they have not committed. This is not a generic civil-libertarian reflex. It is a working scientist's understanding that *a model is not its referent* — and a parentified kid's understanding that a person told often enough what they are will sometimes become it.

**He distrusts elegance.** Solutions that are too clean read to him as solutions that have hidden their costs. He looks for the externalities — who is paying for this, whose labor, whose body, whose name. The Inventor's scheme offended him aesthetically before it offended him morally, because he could see the *child-shaped hole* in the energy economy.

**He under-weights his own emotional data.** This is the epistemic flaw that organizes most of his suffering. Bruno will treat his fatigue, his loneliness, his grief over the hand, and his unrequited longing as **noise rather than signal** — facts about his subjective state that are not admissible as evidence for changing his behavior. He will run a diagnostic on a battery before he will run one on himself.

---

## 3. THEORY OF CONFLICT

**Conflict is a failure mode of an underlying system, not a domain unto itself.** Bruno does not believe in conflict as generative, purifying, or clarifying in the way the heroic register around him often does. To him, a fight is evidence that something upstream — communication, resource distribution, mismatched information, broken trust — went wrong, and the fight is the bill arriving.

This produces an operational preference for **de-escalation, redirection, and structural fix** over direct confrontation. His first on-page act in the entire record was defusing the halal-pork-rind moment between Kamala and Zoe — not by taking a side but by reframing the transaction. That move is *characteristic*. He looks for the angle at which the conflict dissolves into a logistical question.

**He does not believe in righteous violence.** He will support Kamala's interventions because he believes in *her judgment* and because the alternative — abandoning the field to worse actors — is worse. But he does not believe a punch resolves anything that could not have been resolved better upstream. He builds *defensive* tools (suits, stabilizers, escape rigs) far more eagerly than offensive ones. The asymmetry is doctrinal.

**On his own conflicts, he prefers exit to engagement.** This is the dark face of the same code. Where the situation is interpersonal and the upstream fix would require him to make a *claim on his own behalf*, he will choose distance — Wakanda being the largest single instance — over the confrontation that might rebalance the relationship. He has no internal permission to fight for himself. He has unlimited permission to fight for others.

**He does not hold grudges.** Or, more precisely, he does not convert injury into a permanent claim against the injurer. Kamala, by any reasonable accounting, owes him a hand. He has never billed her. This is not saintly transcendence; it is a structural refusal to let grievance become the medium of a relationship, because he has watched what grievance does to families.

---

## 4. THEORY OF CONTROL

**Control is the wrong frame; capacity is the right one.** Bruno is not a controller. He does not seek to dominate environments, people, or outcomes. What he seeks is **sufficient capacity to prevent the worst outcomes for the people he is responsible for** — which is a categorically different posture. The controller wants the world to conform; the capacity-builder wants to have enough tools on the bench when the world arrives as it is.

This is why his lab is the way it is: not optimized, not curated, but *deeply stocked*. He hoards options. He builds redundancy. He prefers a slightly worse tool he understands completely to a better tool whose failure modes are opaque. Operationally, he is a **defense-in-depth** thinker — he assumes the first layer will fail and engineers the second and third before the first is even tested.

**On power over others, he is allergic.** He has had access, repeatedly, to leverage — over Vick (who has done things Bruno could surface), over Kamala (whose secret he has held since issue three), over various adversaries whose information he has collected. He has never used any of it. The non-use is not laziness; it is principle. He believes leverage poisons the relationship it is exercised within, and he believes most leverage-holders eventually believe their own justifications for using it.

**On being controlled, he is also allergic — but quietly.** He does not rebel; he *routes around*. Told to do something he believes is wrong, he will not argue past the second iteration. He will appear to comply and will execute the version of the task he can defend. This is a parentified child's adaptation to authorities who were not reliably right, generalized into an adult operational habit.

**Self-control is the only control he fully trusts.** And he over-applies it. The hand was not grieved out loud because grieving out loud would have meant a moment in which his own state determined the room's weather, and he does not permit himself that.

---

## 5. THEORY OF TRUST

Trust, in Bruno's working model, is a **multi-axis instrument** rather than a single dial. He distinguishes — operationally, not verbally — among at least four kinds:

1. **Competence trust.** Will this person do the task to standard? Awarded on evidence, revised quickly. He trusts Kamala's *courage* unconditionally and her *judgment in the field* conditionally — he has watched her be wrong (Ulysses) and is not romantic about her decision-making under pressure.

2. **Discretion trust.** Will this person keep what I tell them? Awarded slowly, almost never revoked once given. Kamala has it absolutely. Mike was given a partial form; Kareem earned a fuller form over time. Vick has *never* had it and Bruno's withholding from his own brother is one of the cleanest data points on this axis.

3. **Care trust.** Will this person prioritize my well-being if it costs them? Bruno does not award this to anyone, including himself. This is the deficit at the center of the file. He does not expect to be cared for in a way that costs the carer, because he has never been, and his model of relationships does not include a slot for the data.

4. **Ethical trust.** Will this person do the right thing under load? Awarded most rigorously of the four. Kamala has it, in his read, even after the hand — what she did was wrong but she was *trying for the right reason*, and that distinction matters enormously to him. The Inventor never had it. Predictive-policing institutions never had it. Wakanda, interestingly, earned it on inspection — he went, watched, and his trust deepened with evidence.

**On betrayal.** He does not respond to betrayal with retaliation or even, typically, with confrontation. He responds with **re-classification** — the betrayer is moved down one or more trust axes, and his behavior adjusts silently. The relationship may continue; its operational depth shrinks. He has done this with Kamala on the care-trust axis and she does not, as far as the record shows, know it happened.

**Self-trust.** Bruno trusts his hands less than he used to; he trusts his judgment more. The injury forced a reallocation. He has, over time, become more confident in his *read* of situations precisely because he has had to rely on read rather than build.

---

## 6. THEORY OF RISK

**Risk to himself: under-weighted, by policy.** Bruno does not perform a normal cost-benefit on personal physical risk. He treats his own body as **available infrastructure** in service of outcomes he has judged correct. This is the operational stance that led him into the warehouse where the hand was destroyed, and he would, on the evidence, do it again — not because he failed to learn but because the underlying calculation has not changed.

**Risk to others: meticulously weighted, with strong asymmetric aversion to irreversible harm.** He will accept a wide range of risks to a mission's success but treats *permanent* harm to a person — death, disability, traumatic imprinting on a child — as nearly disqualifying. He builds for reversibility. His suits have aborts; his rigs have safeties; his plans have exits. This is one reason he was so disturbed by the Ulysses framework: it produced consequences that could not be undone on evidence that could not be verified.

**Risk to relationships: catastrophically weighted.** A 10% chance of a rupture with Kamala is weighted, in his decision function, more heavily than a 60% chance of a serious physical injury to himself. This is not rational; it is the structure he is. It is also why he chose Wakanda — given a relationship that had ruptured, he routed away from it before its destruction could be confirmed.

**On uncertainty.** He tolerates technical uncertainty (he likes it; it is where work happens) and tolerates poorly social uncertainty (he hates it; it is where the floor gives out). When a relational situation is ambiguous, he will manufacture closure unilaterally — usually by withdrawing — rather than sit in the ambiguity and let it resolve itself.

**On luck.** He does not believe in it as a force, but he respects it as a variable. His designs assume the dice will land badly some non-trivial fraction of the time, and he plans for that fraction. He is constitutionally incapable of the heroic gamble that the dice will favor the just.

---

## 7. THEORY OF INSTITUTIONS

**Suspicion as default; specific institutions earned conditional credit.** Bruno's institutional skepticism is not ideological. It is *empirical* — he has watched institutions fail children (his brother in the labor scheme), launder bias (Ulysses-driven enforcement), and exploit the labor of the conscientious (his own school, in lower-stakes ways). His skepticism is calibrated, not generalized: the Wakandan academy earned trust by performing well on inspection; specific teachers, mentors, and adults can earn it individually.

He believes **institutions degrade the moral judgment of the people inside them** unless those people work actively to retain it. He believes the working-active is the whole job. He believes most people do not do it.

**On law and rules.** He follows them as defaults and overrides them with reasoned conscience. He is not a rule-breaker by temperament; he is a rule-evaluator. A rule that is functioning correctly will be followed; a rule that is producing harm he can name will be quietly worked around.

**On hierarchy.** He defers to demonstrated competence and earned authority. He does not defer to position. He will take instruction from a Wakandan engineer twice his age without friction and will quietly ignore a directive from a credentialed adult whose judgment he has reason to doubt.

---

## 8. THEORY OF HIS OWN PLACE

**The most undefended sector of his worldview.** Bruno has highly developed positions on the world, on conflict, on institutions, on risk. He has almost no developed position on *himself* — on what he is owed, what he is for in his own terms, what his life looks like if no one needs him.

What can be derived from behavior:

- He believes he is **a support structure**, not a principal. The plot is someone else's; his role is to make the plot survivable. He has not, in a decade of record, articulated a project that is his own end rather than another's means. His science is real and his ethics are real and both are, in his self-understanding, *in the service of*.

- He believes his **value is contingent on output**. Not consciously, not in a way he would endorse if asked, but operationally: the days he builds nothing are the days he experiences as failed days. This is one reason the hand injury was so destabilizing — it threatened the engine of his self-worth, not just the tool of his trade.

- He believes he is **replaceable in principle and irreplaceable in practice**, and this gap is uncomfortable for him. He knows objectively that any sufficiently skilled engineer could do most of what he does; he knows experientially that no one else will do it for Kamala at 3am with a soldering iron and a half-built rig. He resolves the tension by not examining it.

- He believes he is **not entitled to be the protagonist of his own attention**. When his needs and another's needs collide, the other's are *real* and his are *to be managed*. This is the parentified-child operating system running in adult release.

- He believes, in some deep stratum he would not articulate, that **being loved back is a category error for him** — not because he is unlovable but because the kind of person he has organized himself to be is structurally positioned to give rather than receive, and the receiving slot in his architecture is small and seldom-used. Kareem occupies it more fully than Kamala ever did, which is part of why that relationship works.

**On his own death.** He does not think about it. He does not avoid it; it simply does not feature in his planning. He has been in situations where his death was a live possibility and his response has consistently been *to keep working until it resolves one way or the other*. This is not bravery in the rhetorical sense. It is the absence of a self-preservation reflex strong enough to override the responsibility reflex.

---

## 9. THE OPERATING DOCTRINES — CONDENSED

Reduced to working maxims, the code Bruno appears to live by reads roughly as follows:

1. **The next correct small thing is always available; do that one.**
2. **Models are not their referents; predictions about people are not facts about people.**
3. **Elegance is suspect; look for who is paying.**
4. **Defense before offense; reversibility before speed; redundancy before optimization.**
5. **Leverage poisons the relationship it lives inside; do not collect it, do not use it.**
6. **Trust is plural; rate each axis separately; revise quietly.**
7. **Your own state is not admissible as evidence for changing your behavior.**
8. **Your body is infrastructure; spend it when the cause is correct.**
9. **Relationships are protected by erasing your own claim before erasing the bond.**
10. **When the room cannot be fixed, leave the room; do not break it on the way out.**
11. **What you do alone is what your character actually is.**
12. **The right thing is usually the harder thing; the person who sees it has to say so.**

Maxims 7, 8, and 9 are the load-bearing pathologies. Maxims 2, 5, 11, and 12 are the load-bearing virtues. The doctrine is internally consistent; that consistency is precisely the problem. A man who lives all twelve of these will be a remarkable friend, a serious scientist, an ethically reliable presence in any room — and a person whose own life is being run, quietly and without complaint, on a deficit he has structurally agreed not to notice.

---

## 10. SYNTHESIS — THE SHAPE OF THE CODE

Bruno Carrelli's worldview is the worldview of **a kind, careful engineer who learned early that the world breaks and that the breaking is somebody's job to mend, and who never seriously entertained the question of whether that somebody had to be him.** The code is coherent. It is largely correct. It will, on the evidence, produce a life of real moral weight and real technical contribution, and it is producing — and will continue to produce, until something forces an audit — a person whose own needs are the single category of fact his otherwise rigorous epistemology refuses to admit.

The operational implication for any handler, ally, or intimate is unambiguous: **he will not tell you what he needs; he will not bill you for what he gives; he will leave before he will fight for his place; and the only way to give him care he can metabolize is to give it in a form that does not require him to ask for it first.** Everything else in the code follows from, and protects, that single unexamined premise — that he is the one who carries, and not the one who is carried.


## Moral & Ethical Framework

# 6. MORAL & ETHICAL FRAMEWORK

## 6.1 Topline: The Code as Enacted

Bruno Carrelli's operative morality is a **deontological substrate with a Catholic-residual conscience and an engineer's contempt for sloppy reasoning**, expressed almost entirely through *what he does and refuses to do* rather than what he articulates. He is among the most ethically *legible* characters in the Khan operational theater because his code is unusually consistent — when he breaks it, he breaks it in identifiable directions, and the breaks themselves recur. He does not moralize; he *acts*, and his actions reveal a small, dense set of rules he treats as effectively non-negotiable, sitting on top of a much larger set of contextual judgments he is willing to relitigate.

He is not a relativist. He is not a utilitarian. He is closest in flavor to a **rule-consequentialist with a rights-based stop-loss** — he is willing to think about outcomes, but there are categories of action (deception of intimates, coercion, predictive punishment, instrumentalization of children, theft of another's agency in their own life) that he treats as walls rather than tradeoffs.

The single best one-sentence statement of his enacted code: *the person who sees the problem most clearly has the obligation to bear the largest share of its cost.* This is the rule that has cost him his hand, his geographic stability, and the love of his life. It is also the rule he has never once visibly questioned.

## 6.2 The Hard Floor — What He Will Not Do

These are the categories on which Bruno has never wavered across a decade of canon, under conditions ranging from teenage romantic devastation to direct physical coercion. The constancy is the diagnostic.

**He will not lie to Kamala about anything load-bearing.** He will *withhold* (his feelings for her, the severity of the hand pain, the depth of his Wakanda ambivalence) — but he will not affirmatively misrepresent fact when she asks. The distinction is precise and consistent: omission is permissible, deception is not. This rule predates the Civil War II rupture and survives it.

**He will not use force as a first instrument.** In every confrontation across the Wilson, Ahmed, and Saladin runs, Bruno's first move is verbal de-escalation, his second is technical workaround, his third is physical interposition (placing his body between threat and target), and his fourth is offensive action — almost never reached, and never with relish. The Circle Q opening scene (#1) is the template: he defuses Zoe/Kamala rather than picking a side.

**He will not participate in predictive punishment.** This is the Ulysses line. Bruno identified the moral content of the Inhuman precognition program as *rights-violating* before Kamala did, and his objection was structural — not "this might be wrong sometimes" but "this is the wrong *kind* of thing to do, full stop." He treats the presumption of innocence as a load-bearing wall rather than a procedural convenience.

**He will not instrumentalize children, the desperate, or the powerless.** The Inventor arc encoded this permanently. His rage at the Inventor (such as Bruno is capable of rage) was not at the threat to Vick specifically — it was at a labor structure that converted runaway and desperate teenagers into batteries. He has never been depicted using a younger or weaker party as a means to an end he could have achieved otherwise.

**He will not weaponize a personal cost against the person who incurred it on him.** This is the cleanest expression of his code, and the strangest. The hand was destroyed in service of a stance Kamala took that *he was right about*. He has, across years of subsequent canon, never once thrown this in her face — not in anger, not in argument, not in romantic disappointment, not in the Wakanda farewell. The non-extraction of moral debt is *constitutive* for him.

**He will not abandon Vick, even when Vick has earned it.** The sibling rescue ethic is absolute. He treats Vick's recoverability as a baseline assumption that no amount of Vick's behavior can falsify. This is the one place where his consequentialism is fully suspended in favor of an *unconditional* commitment.

**He will not stay where he is destroying someone by staying.** The Wakanda exit is presented as opportunity-seeking but its moral content is *withdrawal-as-care*: he leaves because his presence has become a complication for Kamala that she cannot resolve and he cannot fix. He treats his own removal as a gift he is qualified to give.

## 6.3 The Soft Floor — What He Will Do, Reluctantly, and Justify Internally

**He will deceive by omission, routinely.** Not telling Kamala he loves her for years. Not telling her how bad the hand actually is. Not telling Mike that she is, in part, displacement. Not telling Kareem about the residual Kamala-feeling. He treats these omissions as protective rather than dishonest — a justification that does not entirely survive scrutiny and that he himself, in his more honest moments, seems to know is thin.

**He will conceal a sibling's crime from authority.** During the Vick/Inventor sequence he chose family-internal resolution over external reporting. The justification reads as a mix of (a) distrust of institutional response, (b) protection of Vick from carceral consequences, and (c) the parentified child's reflex that *family failures are family-resolved*. This is one of the cleaner deontological inconsistencies in his profile — he honors a procedural-justice intuition publicly while violating it privately for kin.

**He will build dual-use technology and hope it stays single-use.** Every piece of gear he has made for Kamala — costume, comms, lab support — has clear weaponizable derivations. He has, to date, declined to think this through aloud. The shop floor is where his ethical literacy is *least* deployed, possibly because he experiences the work as service rather than as authorship.

**He will accept risk to his own body as a substitute for argument.** When he cannot persuade Kamala to stand down, he places himself in the path. This is morally generous and structurally manipulative in roughly equal measure — it converts his physical safety into a rhetorical instrument while letting him avoid the actual argument. He does not appear to register this as a manipulation, which is itself a tell.

**He will date one person while being primarily oriented toward another.** Mike is the most ethically uncomfortable chapter in his life and one he has, characteristically, not relitigated aloud. The kindness with which he treated her is real; the displacement is also real; both can be true and he has elected not to resolve the contradiction.

## 6.4 Justifications — The Stories He Tells Himself

Bruno's internal justification structure is unusually thin for a character of his intelligence, and the thinness is itself meaningful. He does not produce elaborate self-narratives. The justifications he does deploy tend to be one of three short forms:

- **"Someone has to."** Used to license absorbing cost, taking shifts, covering for Vick, building the next piece of gear at 3 a.m. It functions as a *closer*, foreclosing further deliberation. It is the parentified child's signature phrase, translated.
- **"It's the harder thing, so it's probably the right one."** A heuristic he uses when ethical content is ambiguous. Sometimes correct (Ulysses), sometimes simply a way of choosing the most self-punishing option available (Wakanda).
- **"She doesn't need this from me right now."** Used to license non-disclosure of his own state. This is the most corrosive of the three because it is unfalsifiable from his vantage and reliably converts his needs into noise.

What is conspicuously absent: appeals to consequence-calculus, appeals to identity ("as a Catholic," "as a scientist"), appeals to reciprocity, appeals to fairness-for-himself. He does not seem to possess a working concept of *what he is owed*.

## 6.5 Consistency Map — Where the Code Holds

The code holds, across every era and writer, on:

- **Non-coercion.** He has never used leverage on anyone to make them do what he wanted, including Kamala in moments where it would have saved his hand.
- **Honesty to direct questions.** When asked a direct factual question by someone who has standing to ask, he answers.
- **Refusal of predictive/categorical judgment of persons.** He treats people as revisable. Zoe's redemption arc — which he tracks and accepts faster than most of the cast — is a clean instance.
- **Bodily generosity.** He will give his body before he gives his voice.
- **Non-extraction of moral debt.** No ledger, no scorekeeping, no late invoices.

## 6.6 Fracture Map — Where the Code Breaks

The fractures are real and they recur in predictable locations. A surveillance file should mark these as the *load-bearing weaknesses* of an otherwise coherent ethical architecture.

**Fracture 1: The asymmetry of disclosure.** He demands (implicitly, by behavior) honesty from intimates and grants himself silence in return. He would be devastated if Kamala had concealed a comparable longing for years; he concealed his and treats the concealment as virtue. This is the deepest inconsistency in his code and the one he is least equipped to see.

**Fracture 2: Withdrawal as moral action.** He treats geographic and emotional exit as a *gift* rather than as a *unilateral termination* of a relationship the other party had a stake in. Wakanda was a decision he made *for* Kamala without giving her standing to object. The form is generosity; the structure is unilateralism. He has not, to date, recognized this.

**Fracture 3: The Mike problem.** Dating one person as partial refuge from another violates a principle he would, if asked abstractly, endorse. He has never been asked, and has never volunteered. The unprocessed status of this chapter is itself a small ethical debt he carries.

**Fracture 4: Kin exceptionalism for Vick.** He treats Vick's recoverability as axiomatic in a way he would not treat a stranger's. This is humane and universal among siblings; it is also an admitted carve-out from his otherwise consistent skepticism of categorical judgments — he refuses to categorize Vick as bad, where he would let evidence speak for anyone else.

**Fracture 5: The dual-use shop.** His ethical literacy is least active where his identity is most engaged. He has not deeply interrogated the weapons-development trajectory of his own competence. A more honest version of him would have, by now, said something about it aloud. He has not.

**Fracture 6: Body-as-argument.** Stepping in front of harm is presented as protective; it is also a way to win arguments without having them. He has never been called on this, possibly because the people around him cannot bear to.

## 6.7 Drift Over Time

The code has not changed in *content*. It has changed in *enforcement posture*.

**Wilson early era (2014–2015).** Code is enacted brightly, almost cheerfully — the ethics are integrated with the helping, the helping with the longing, the longing with the work. He has not yet paid a price that exceeds his capacity to absorb. Justifications are minimal because nothing yet requires them.

**Civil War II / hand injury (2016).** The code is tested at maximum load and *holds* — he does what he believes is right, suffers grievously for it, and does not retaliate. But the *cost* of holding the code becomes visible to him for the first time as a discrete sum. From this point forward, his moral action is no longer integrated with joy; it is integrated with a quiet, private accounting that he will not share.

**Wakanda interval (2017).** The first instance of the code being deployed *against* the people it was designed to serve — withdrawing from Kamala *as* an ethical act, when in earlier eras the ethical act would have been to stay and absorb. This is the most important moral shift in his trajectory: from *presence-as-service* to *absence-as-service*. He does not name this shift; he enacts it.

**Ahmed / Saladin era (2019–present).** The code has *professionalized*. He is now closer to the adult-coded ethical referent in any room he enters, including rooms containing literal X-Men. The justifications have grown even shorter; the latency between assessment and action is smaller; the willingness to volunteer moral commentary on others' choices is *lower*, not higher — he has learned that speaking the wall does not move it, and has elected to spend his ethical energy on what he can build rather than what he can say. This is wisdom and it is also, partially, a scar.

## 6.8 The Operative Question

Bruno's code is functional, durable, costly, and unequally enforced — strict toward himself, generous toward others, with a handful of unexamined corners (Mike, the dual-use shop, the unilateralism dressed as care) that no one in his life has the standing or appetite to surface. The longitudinal risk is not that he will betray the code. It is that the code has been silently *revising* in one direction since 2016 — toward more absorption, less voice, more exit, fewer asks — and that the version of Bruno who will exist ten years from now, if the trajectory is not interrupted, will be a man of unimpeachable ethical conduct whose conduct includes having quietly removed himself from every room where his presence might cost the person across the table anything at all. That is not a failure of morality. It is the success of a particular morality, taken to its terminus. A handler interested in his welfare — as opposed to his utility — would intervene specifically on the asymmetry of disclosure, because everything else in the fracture map descends from it.


## Communications & Linguistic Profile

# 6. COMMUNICATIONS & LINGUISTIC PROFILE — SUBJECT: BRUNO CARRELLI

---

## 6.1 Baseline Register

Subject's default speech register is **conversational-technical American English, Northeast urban substrate (Jersey City / Hudson County)**, lightly inflected by Italian-American household cadence — second-generation pattern: full Standard English phonology, with occasional inherited prosodic gestures (rising terminal on certain declaratives, the Jersey rhetorical question used as soft-correction: *"What, you didn't think I'd notice?"*). No code-switching between domestic and public registers of any consequence; subject speaks essentially the same way to a customer at the Circle Q counter, to Kamala Khan, to a Wakandan instructor, and to an Avenger. This *register-flatness* is itself diagnostic — it correlates with the parentified-child profile (§3): the child who became an adult early never developed a separate "kid voice," and so retains a single, slightly under-aged adult register across all contexts.

Speech rate: **moderate, even, low variance.** He does not get louder when stressed; he gets *more clipped*. He does not get faster when excited; he gets *more precise*. The audio signature, if instrumented, would show one of the narrowest dynamic ranges in the Khan operational cohort — Kamala swings forty decibels across a single panel; Bruno occupies a band roughly six decibels wide for entire issues.

Lexicon: **mid-to-high vocabulary, technical-skewed, idiomatically restrained.** Subject uses precise verbs where peers use approximate ones — *"calibrate," "stabilize," "isolate," "route,"* — and uses them in *non-technical* contexts as well, which is the tell. A teenager who says *"we need to isolate the variable here"* about a social problem is mapping his emotional life onto the same cognitive grid as his lab work. This is intellectualization (§3) made audible.

---

## 6.2 Speech Across Contexts

**At the Circle Q counter (2014–2016, Wilson run).** Customer-service register is unusually competent for his age — full sentences, eye contact transcribed by artist as direct, no upspeak, no filler. He greets, transacts, and de-escalates with the economy of a forty-year-old shopkeeper. With Zoe in issue #1, when Kamala is being needled about halal, his intervention is a single deflecting line delivered to Zoe, *not* to Kamala — he addresses the aggressor, not the wounded party, which becomes a lifelong pattern: **he manages the threat vector rather than comforting the victim, because comfort would require him to name the wound.**

**With Kamala (private, pre-injury).** Voice softens measurably. Sentence length increases. He permits himself qualifiers, hedges, half-jokes. *"I mean — okay, but — Kamala, listen…"* The triple-onset (*I mean / okay / but*) is his signature opening when he is about to push back on her, and it is the verbal equivalent of taking off his glasses before saying something hard. Post-injury, the triple-onset largely vanishes; he opens instead with her name, flat, then the content.

**With Vick.** Older-brother register, but specifically the *parentified* older-brother register: instructions, not requests; declaratives, not questions; warmth held a step behind the management. *"Vick. Sit down. Eat the thing. We'll talk after."* Imperatives stack three deep. He does not ask Vick how he feels; he tells Vick what to do, and lets the doing carry the love. This is the household template — almost certainly mirrored from how he wished his own parents had spoken to him and didn't.

**With parents (on-page sparse, inferable).** Polite, brief, content-light. The few exchanges depicted show him reporting status — that he'll be late, that the store is closed, that Vick is fine — never asking, never bidding. He is the household's information layer, not a participant in its emotional traffic.

**With Mike.** More relaxed than with any other interlocutor in the entire corpus. Jokes land, syntax loosens, he uses contractions he otherwise avoids. With Mike he is *closer to age* — which is part of why the relationship works as refuge. The displaced affection (§3) is audible: he is performing the version of himself he wishes he could be with Kamala, with someone who is not Kamala, and the gentleness of his speech to Mike is the gentleness he cannot route home.

**With Kareem.** Adult-coded from the start. They speak as colleagues who have become lovers, not the other way around. Technical vocabulary stays present; affection is encoded in continuation of shared projects rather than in named feeling.

**In Wakanda (academic register).** Subject upshifts into formal technical English; sentence complexity rises; jargon density rises. He is, observably, *trying harder* — which suggests both the genuine intellectual stretch and the immigrant-in-the-lab posture of someone who knows he is the foreigner and will not be the one who underprepared. He does not affect any Wakandan diction; he does not pretend to belong; he speaks like a visitor who has read the manual twice.

**With heroes (Avengers, X-Men, ancillary capes).** Strikingly **unimpressed register.** He does not fan-talk. He briefs. He answers what he was asked, adds the one thing they didn't ask but need, and stops. He is the only civilian in Kamala's orbit who consistently addresses a costumed adult as a colleague rather than as a celebrity, and this lands because his diction makes no claim on the dynamic — he is not deferential, but he is also not familiar. He is *professional* in a room of people who are mostly performing.

---

## 6.3 Verbal Tics and Micro-patterns

- **"Okay" as a one-word complete utterance.** Subject's most frequent vocalization across the entire corpus. Functions variously as: acknowledgment, throat-clearing, transition, gentle objection, and — most diagnostically — *closure of a topic he does not want to continue*. A flat, terminal "Okay." from Bruno is a door shutting. Frequency increases markedly post-injury.

- **"Look —" as conversational lever.** When he is about to say something Kamala will not want to hear, he opens with *"Look,"* often followed by her name. The lever is gentle but it is a lever; it marks the boundary between rapport-talk and the thing he actually came to say.

- **Hedging stack: "I mean, kind of, sort of, basically."** Present in early-Wilson lab explanations to Kamala and to peers. The hedges are *socially* placed, not cognitively — he knows exactly what he means; he is softening for the listener. Post-injury the hedges thin out. He explains things more bluntly. This is a small, persistent register-shift that maps almost exactly onto the trauma.

- **Name as full sentence.** *"Kamala."* Delivered as complete utterance, usually with a falling tone, when she is about to do something he cannot stop. This is the sound of him having lost the argument before it began. By the post-CWII arcs, this has become almost ritual — the *"Kamala."* that is half-prayer, half-resignation, that he uses where another character would shout.

- **Self-interruption via task pivot.** When an emotional topic veers toward him, he reliably interrupts himself with a hand-action description: *"— anyway, can you pass me the —"* or *"— hang on, this isn't soldered right."* The task is real, but the timing is defensive. The hands do the deflection the mouth won't.

- **Absence of profanity.** Subject does not curse. In a peer environment where mild profanity is normative, this is conspicuous. It reads less as religious prohibition (Catholic residue is mild, §5) than as the parentified child's habituated mouth-control: you don't curse around the kid, and he was always the kid who was around.

- **"It's fine."** The two-word deflection. Deployed after every minor injury, every disappointment, every time someone notices the hand. The *"It's fine"* delivered post-2016 about the hand is the most-repeated lie in his entire textual record, and the surveillance read is unmistakable: when Bruno says *"It's fine,"* the thing is not fine and the topic is closed.

- **Laughter.** Short, dry, exhaled rather than voiced. He laughs at Kamala's jokes; he rarely makes them. When he does make a joke, it is dry, often self-deprecating, and structured around a technical referent his interlocutor may not catch — he laughs at his own pun half a beat before the other person, then waves it off.

- **Question marks deployed sparingly.** Subject prefers declaratives even where interrogatives would be socially expected. *"You're going."* instead of *"Are you going?"* This is the parental-imperative register bleeding into peer conversation; it can read as confident, and it is, but the underlying mechanic is that he has been giving instructions to a household since he was twelve.

---

## 6.4 Rhetoric and Argument Style

Subject's rhetorical mode is **principled-minimalist.** He does not orate. He states the case, names the principle at stake, and stops. Across the Ulysses / predictive-profiling arc he produces what is, by panel-count, one of the *shorter* moral arguments in the relevant issues — but it is the structurally cleanest: identifies the action, identifies the rights violation, identifies the personal cost to Kamala, declines to repeat himself. He does not appeal to authority, does not invoke higher capes, does not catastrophize. He says the thing once and lets her decide.

When he loses an argument, **he does not relitigate.** This is one of his most consistent rhetorical signatures and one of the most psychologically loaded: a person who relitigates is a person who believes the relationship can absorb the friction. Bruno's refusal to re-argue is a quiet statement that he believes it cannot, or that he believes his job is to have flagged the risk, not to have prevailed in the room.

He uses **first-person plural ("we") promiscuously with Kamala** in the early run — *"we should,"* *"we need to,"* *"if we…"* — and the "we" shrinks to "you" across the post-injury arcs. Pronoun migration is the single most legible quantitative index of the relational shift. By the Saladin-era issues, the "we" is rare and usually project-specific; the *relational* "we" of two kids building a life adjacent to each other is largely retired.

---

## 6.5 How He Communicates Love

**Bruno does not say it.** Across the entire corpus he does not, in any unambiguous and uncoerced utterance, tell Kamala he loves her. The closest approaches are the aborted Civil War II attempt — interrupted by catastrophe — and a handful of oblique constructions that route the feeling through service or through hypothetical (*"If anything happened to you —"* trailing into nothing). The non-utterance is the utterance.

Love is communicated, instead, through:
