- **Object-making.** Custom gear, bespoke fabrication, the suit, the comms, the upgrades — *every gift he gives Kamala is a thing he made with his hands.* The object is the sentence. When the hands are damaged, the sentence becomes harder to write, and the romantic foreclosure and the somatic foreclosure are the same foreclosure.
- **Information-as-care.** He tells her what she needs to know before she knows she needs it. The briefing is the love letter.
- **Physical positioning.** He stands between her and the threat. Linguistically this manifests as the *"I'll handle —"* construction, often left incomplete because the handling has already started.
- **Permission language.** *"You don't have to —"* offered to people he cares about, granting them an out he himself would never take. He gives others the exits he denies himself.

With Mike and with Kareem, the affection is more openly verbal — *"I like being around you," "this is good"* — small, declarative, undecorated, and notable precisely because the same register is impossible with Kamala. The contrast is the diagnostic.

---

## 6.6 How He Communicates Threat

He essentially **doesn't threaten.** In sixty-plus issues of canonical record, subject does not deliver a single conventional threat. When confronted with hostile actors — the Inventor's enforcers, street-level antagonists in Jersey City, threats around Vick — his response register is **flat warning, not escalation**: *"You don't want to do that,"* *"This is a bad idea,"* *"Walk away."* The diction is borrowed from the de-escalation playbook of someone who has worked retail since middle school. He has been talking down customers for years; he scales the same toolkit to assailants.

When the threat is moral rather than physical — i.e., when someone he loves is about to do something wrong — his "threat" is the **stated cost**, never the imposed one. He does not say *"I'll leave."* He says *"This will hurt you,"* and then, when it does, he leaves quietly and does not announce the leaving as consequence. The Wakanda transfer is communicated as opportunity, not as withdrawal. The dossier read is that the withdrawal *was* the consequence, but he refused to label it as such because labeling it would make it leverage, and leverage would make the love conditional, and the love is the one thing he will not negotiate.

---

## 6.7 How He Communicates Grief

**He doesn't, audibly.** Grief enters his speech as **subtraction** rather than addition: fewer hedges, fewer jokes, shorter sentences, longer pauses, the disappearance of the relational "we." When Kamala is presumed dead in later arcs, his depicted speech does not break into lamentation; it goes *quieter*, more procedural, more competent. He grieves by *increasing function*.

The hand is grieved the same way. He does not eulogize what his hands could do. He learns to direct other people's hands, builds workarounds, accepts the brace, declines comment. The single most consistent verbal artifact around the injury is the **refusal of the subject** — when interlocutors raise the hand, he answers in a register so flat it functions as a boundary. *"It's fine. It works."* End of topic. The grief is real; it has been routed into the silence.

The somatic correlate, useful to triangulate: artists who draw him post-injury reliably show him **looking at his hand when he thinks no one is watching, and not looking at it when anyone is.** The grief lives in that asymmetry. He has a private vocabulary for it that has no words in it.

---

## 6.8 Deflection Language — Catalogue

The deflection toolkit is small, well-worn, and consistent across writers, which suggests it is genuinely a property of the character rather than an authorial idiolect:

1. **"It's fine."** (Topic closure, self-directed.)
2. **"Don't worry about it."** (Topic closure, other-directed.)
3. **Task pivot:** *"Hang on, let me just —"* (Re-routes attention to hands/tools.)
4. **Subject swap to the other person's situation:** the listener asks how he is; he answers about how *they* are. This is one of the most consistent diagnostics in the corpus — Bruno is asked perhaps two dozen variations of *"are you okay?"* across the canon, and answers the literal question perhaps twice.
5. **Humor-deflection (dry, self-deprecating):** brief, low-affect joke that closes the topic by lowering its stakes.
6. **Geographic deflection (the macro version):** when the conversation cannot be deflected, the location changes. Wakanda is the largest instance; smaller versions occur throughout (he leaves the room, he goes back to the lab, he closes the store).
7. **The Name-as-Sentence (*"Kamala."*)**: when the deflection is from her own choice rather than from his own pain, the name does the work.

---

## 6.9 Tells

The surveillance-grade tells, ordered by reliability:

- **Pronoun migration ("we" → "you").** Most reliable longitudinal index of relational distance with Kamala. Trackable issue-by-issue.
- **Hedge density.** High hedge density = he is managing the listener; low hedge density = he has stopped managing. Drop in hedges with Kamala post-2016 marks the post-injury professionalization.
- **Triple-onset opener ("I mean — okay — but —").** Present means rapport intact, soft pushback incoming. Absent means he has either given up or already left the relational frame.
- **"It's fine."** Always a lie. The frequency of *"It's fine"* in a given arc is roughly proportional to how badly things are going internally.
- **The name-as-sentence.** Marks a moment he has lost an argument he never started.
- **Self-interruption to a task.** Marks emotional content that has come too close. Frequency rises in any arc that touches the hand, the romantic substrate, or the parentification.
- **Sentence-length compression under stress.** Where peers' sentences fragment chaotically, Bruno's compress orderly. *Subject-verb-object, full stop.* The compression itself is the stress signal.
- **Absence of self-reference in emotional contexts.** In any conversation that touches his own injury, his own loss, or his own longing, the first-person singular pronoun "I" drops in frequency by roughly half. He talks around himself. The hole in the syntax is the subject.
- **The lab register bleeding into the kitchen.** When *"isolate," "calibrate," "stabilize"* appear in a non-technical conversation, he is intellectualizing in real time. Defense-on-the-tongue.
- **The dry-exhale laugh as terminal punctuation.** When the laugh appears at the end of his own sentence rather than in response to another's, he is closing a topic he found uncomfortable to have raised.

---

## 6.10 Summary

Subject's linguistic profile is the profile of a person who learned, very young, that **words have costs and silences have uses.** He speaks precisely, sparingly, warmly within a narrow band, and uses his diction to manage other people's comfort at the steady expense of his own visibility. He does not say what he wants; he builds it. He does not threaten; he warns. He does not grieve aloud; he goes quieter and works harder. He does not declare love; he hands you the thing he made. The single most important communications-intelligence finding on Bruno Carrelli is that **the signal is in the subtraction** — what he leaves out of a sentence is more diagnostic than what he puts in, and a handler reading him on transcript alone, ignoring the silences and the pronoun drift and the hedge-density curve, will mistake a man under sustained internal pressure for a man at peace.

He is not at peace. He is fluent in the language of appearing to be.


## Predictive Model I — Routine & Social

# PREDICTIVE MODEL I — ROUTINE & SOCIAL

**Methodology note.** The predictions below extrapolate from longitudinal behavioral record across the Wilson, Ahmed, and Saladin runs. Each prediction is phrased GIVEN → EXPECT, with a confidence tier (HIGH / MODERATE / SPECULATIVE) and a brief evidentiary anchor where canon supports it. The point is not novelty but *fidelity to grain*: what a person who has been Bruno Carrelli since middle school will, with high probability, do in any given Tuesday-afternoon situation.

---

## 6.1 — DIURNAL & SOMATIC ROUTINE

**GIVEN** an ordinary weekday with no superhuman event in progress, **EXPECT** Bruno to be awake before 6:30 AM regardless of bedtime. *Confidence: HIGH.* The parentified-child sleep architecture is set early and does not relax; he is the one who would have walked Vick to school. He will not press snooze. He gets up on the first alarm because someone in the house used to need him to.

**GIVEN** the choice between breakfast and an extra ten minutes of sleep, **EXPECT** breakfast — but the cheapest, fastest possible version: coffee black, a piece of fruit, leftover bread, sometimes nothing but coffee. *Confidence: HIGH.* He will not skip caffeine; he will skip food. He underestimates his own caloric needs because his metabolic vocabulary is built around "what does the household have to spare."

**GIVEN** access to coffee, **EXPECT** at least three cups before noon, drunk fast and lukewarm. *Confidence: HIGH.* He does not drink coffee for pleasure; he drinks it for function. He will reheat the same mug twice and forget it on a workbench at least once a day.

**GIVEN** a meal eaten alone, **EXPECT** it to be standing up, in under seven minutes, while doing something else (reading, soldering, scrolling). *Confidence: HIGH.* Meals taken alone are not events; they are refueling. He does not perform care for himself when no one is watching.

**GIVEN** a meal eaten with others (Kamala's family, Auntie Ruth, a group at the Circle Q break room), **EXPECT** the inverse: slow eater, attentive to whether others have what they need, will refill someone else's glass before his own, will be the last to start and one of the last to finish because he kept stopping to listen. *Confidence: HIGH.* Demonstrated repeatedly at Khan dinners.

**GIVEN** sleep curtailment for a project, **EXPECT** Bruno to push to ~3 hours/night for up to four consecutive nights before any visible degradation, and to deny tiredness if asked. *Confidence: HIGH.* The somatic baseline of chronic under-sleep makes the descent gradual; the giveaway is fine motor — he drops things he wouldn't normally drop, and then, since the injury, he drops them with his *left* hand, which alarms him.

**GIVEN** an offer of help with a physical task (carrying, lifting, reaching), **EXPECT** polite refusal followed by completing the task himself even when it would be faster to accept. *Confidence: HIGH.* Receiving help is the load-bearing weakness of the entire personality.

**GIVEN** illness (cold, flu, fever under 101°F), **EXPECT** Bruno to work the shift, attend the obligation, finish the deliverable. He will mention it only if directly asked, and minimize when he does. *Confidence: HIGH.* He will only stop when somatic function literally fails.

---

## 6.2 — THE HAND: MICRO-BEHAVIOR

**GIVEN** any unfamiliar social setting, **EXPECT** the injured hand held slightly behind the hip or in a pocket for the first 30–90 seconds before he forgets to manage it. *Confidence: HIGH.* Not shame — assessment. He is reading whether this is a room where the hand will become a topic.

**GIVEN** someone notices the brace/glove and asks about it, **EXPECT** a brief, factual, deflective answer ("Old injury. Doesn't slow me down much.") followed by a topic pivot to the other person. *Confidence: HIGH.* He has rehearsed this sentence. He will not tell the actual story unless the asker has *earned* the story, which is a very small list (Kamala, Mike, Kareem, possibly Nakia, possibly Aamir).

**GIVEN** a task requiring fine motor work he could once do solo, **EXPECT** one of three adaptations, ranked by setting: (a) one-handed workaround with the unaffected hand, slower but functional; (b) verbal direction of a collaborator's hands ("a hair to the left — there"); (c) jig fabrication — he will spend twenty minutes building a clamp to do what fingers used to do in two. *Confidence: HIGH.* Pattern (c) is the most diagnostic: he engineers around the injury rather than asking around it.

**GIVEN** a cold day, **EXPECT** stiffness in the right hand, occasionally a wince he immediately suppresses, and a habit of cradling it in the off-hand under a coat. *Confidence: MODERATE.* Nerve injuries weather; the canon shows him in scarves and gloves; the gesture is plausible.

**GIVEN** a moment of acute emotion (joy, fear, anger), **EXPECT** the *left* hand to act and the right to drift to a neutral position. *Confidence: MODERATE.* He has rewired his expressive somatics to the side that still reports honestly.

**GIVEN** a handshake offered to the right hand by someone who doesn't know, **EXPECT** Bruno to meet it briefly, grip light, release fast — no flinch, no comment. *Confidence: HIGH.* He will not embarrass the other person.

---

## 6.3 — THE CIRCLE Q (and its successor workplaces)

**GIVEN** a shift at the Circle Q, **EXPECT** Bruno to arrive 10–15 minutes early, restock the items he knows the previous shift missed, and reset displays without being asked. *Confidence: HIGH.* He does the unpaid labor of competence.

**GIVEN** a regular customer entering, **EXPECT** their order to be partially queued before they reach the counter — drink already on the warmer, cigarettes pulled, the specific bag of chips reached for. *Confidence: HIGH.* He runs a mental ledger of every regular's preferences and tracks small changes (a new brand, a missed week) as data points about their lives.

**GIVEN** a customer in distress (lost wallet, short on cash, visibly upset, unhoused), **EXPECT** quiet accommodation — he will float the dollar from his own pocket, will not announce it, will not bring it up again. Cumulative across a year this likely amounts to a non-trivial fraction of his paycheck. *Confidence: HIGH.* This is consistent with the Vick-arc pattern of absorbing cost privately.

**GIVEN** a shoplifter, **EXPECT** de-escalation over interdiction. He will make eye contact, ask "can I help you find something?" in a tone that communicates *I see you and I will not call anyone if you put it back.* Confrontation only if a coworker is endangered. *Confidence: HIGH.* The Zoe/halal opener in #1 is the foundational tell.

**GIVEN** a coworker calls out sick, **EXPECT** Bruno to cover, and not to mention to anyone that he covered. *Confidence: HIGH.*

**GIVEN** the boss/owner asks who broke something, **EXPECT** Bruno to take the hit if the actual culprit is younger, more precarious, or a friend. *Confidence: MODERATE-HIGH.* Pattern of absorbing blame to protect Vick generalizes.

**GIVEN** downtime on a slow shift, **EXPECT** him at the back counter with a textbook, a laptop, or a half-disassembled small appliance, not a phone. *Confidence: HIGH.*

---

## 6.4 — CONVERSATIONAL & SOCIAL MICRO-PATTERNS

**GIVEN** a group conversation in which he has nothing pressing to add, **EXPECT** Bruno to listen, smile at the right moments, and contribute roughly one comment per four-to-six minutes of group talk, almost always *responsive* rather than initiating. *Confidence: HIGH.* He is conversationally generous and structurally low-bid.

**GIVEN** someone says something factually wrong in a low-stakes setting, **EXPECT** silent correction (his face will register it for a beat, then resolve). He will not correct unless asked or unless the error will harm someone. *Confidence: HIGH.* He is not a pedant; he is conflict-averse and ego-quiet.

**GIVEN** someone says something *ethically* wrong in a low-stakes setting, **EXPECT** a quiet, single-sentence pushback — not a sermon. "I don't know if that's fair," delivered without heat, often deflected through a question. *Confidence: HIGH.* The Ulysses arc shows this register: principled, soft-voiced, unwavering.

**GIVEN** he is teased (about Kamala, about the brace, about his earnestness), **EXPECT** a half-smile, a self-deprecating one-liner, and a topic shift. He does not get angry at teasing because anger would require admitting the tease landed. *Confidence: HIGH.*

**GIVEN** a direct compliment, **EXPECT** deflection — to the team, the tool, the luck, the other person's idea. The phrase "yeah, but —" or its equivalent is his most reliable verbal tic when praised. *Confidence: HIGH.*

**GIVEN** a direct question about how he is *feeling*, **EXPECT** the answer to be a status report on a project or on someone else. "Working on the —" / "Vick's doing better." He answers *what's happening*; he rarely answers *how he is*. *Confidence: HIGH.*

**GIVEN** a silence in conversation he is co-responsible for, **EXPECT** him to tolerate it longer than the average person before filling it — by roughly two to four seconds. *Confidence: MODERATE.* He grew up in a household where silence was safer than the alternative.

**GIVEN** an awkward moment between two other people, **EXPECT** Bruno to insert a low-key bridge: a benign question, a piece of business, a redirected anecdote that gives both parties an out. *Confidence: HIGH.* He is a habitual room-stabilizer.

**GIVEN** profanity or crude speech around him, **EXPECT** no flinch, no participation. He doesn't curse much. Not from prudishness — from register-discipline; he speaks the way he wishes he had been spoken to. *Confidence: MODERATE.*

---

## 6.5 — TEXT, PHONE, DIGITAL HYGIENE

**GIVEN** a text from Kamala, **EXPECT** response within 90 seconds during waking hours, regardless of what he is doing. *Confidence: HIGH.* The relationship has scarred over, not severed; the response-latency is a vestigial reflex.

**GIVEN** a text from anyone else in the close circle, **EXPECT** response within an hour, batch-processed. *Confidence: HIGH.*

**GIVEN** a text he doesn't want to answer (emotional, confrontational, a bid for vulnerability), **EXPECT** delay of 6–24 hours followed by a reply that is shorter than the prompt and pivots to a practical question. *Confidence: HIGH.* Suppression in 160 characters.

**GIVEN** a phone call that is not from family, **EXPECT** non-answer, voicemail check, callback within 20 minutes if obligated. He prefers text. *Confidence: HIGH.*

**GIVEN** social media, **EXPECT** minimal posting, moderate consumption, very long lurker tenure on technical and ethics-of-tech communities (he reads more comments than he ever posts). *Confidence: MODERATE-HIGH.*

**GIVEN** a request to share his location, **EXPECT** ready acceptance for trusted persons (Kamala, Aamir, Mike, Kareem, Vick) and quiet resistance for institutional asks. *Confidence: MODERATE.* The Ulysses-era civil-liberties wariness generalizes.

**GIVEN** a new device, **EXPECT** factory image wiped within an hour of unboxing, custom OS where feasible, two-factor on everything, password manager, no biometric unlock on the lab machine. *Confidence: HIGH.*

---

## 6.6 — MONEY

**GIVEN** a paycheck, **EXPECT** an immediate mental partition — household contribution, Vick contingency, savings, tools/parts, almost nothing for himself. *Confidence: HIGH.*

**GIVEN** the urge to buy something for himself, **EXPECT** a delay of weeks-to-months and frequent failure to follow through. He will instead spend the equivalent amount on a gift, a part for someone else's project, or a meal he picks up for the household. *Confidence: HIGH.*

**GIVEN** an unexpected windfall (bonus, grant stipend in the Wakanda era), **EXPECT** it routed almost entirely outward — to Vick, to family bills, to a tool the lab needed. *Confidence: HIGH.*

**GIVEN** a check at a restaurant with friends, **EXPECT** Bruno to reach first, undertip himself in favor of the server, and grumble only mildly if outflanked. *Confidence: MODERATE.*

**GIVEN** a major purchase decision, **EXPECT** weeks of research, spreadsheets, the cheapest viable option chosen, used over new where possible. *Confidence: HIGH.*

---

## 6.7 — DRESS, GROOMING, OBJECT RELATIONS

**GIVEN** a normal day, **EXPECT** the same uniform: jeans or work pants, plain t-shirt or henley, hoodie or zip-up, sneakers chosen for standing eight hours. Two-day shave at most; clean but not styled. *Confidence: HIGH.*

**GIVEN** a formal occasion (Aamir's wedding-tier event), **EXPECT** Bruno in a properly fitted but inexpensive jacket, hands fidgeting briefly with cuffs, visibly more comfortable once seated. *Confidence: MODERATE-HIGH.*

**GIVEN** a wardrobe item beginning to fail, **EXPECT** repair before replacement: a patched elbow, a re-soled sneaker, a hoodie wearing through that he keeps anyway. *Confidence: HIGH.* Sentimentality and frugality braid together; he attaches to objects through *use*, not acquisition.

**GIVEN** a gift of clothing from Mike or Kareem, **EXPECT** it worn often, visibly cared for, and noted aloud to the giver when worn. *Confidence: MODERATE.* He repays affection in tracked-and-acknowledged use.

**GIVEN** the loss of a tool, notebook, or piece of equipment with sentimental association, **EXPECT** disproportionate quiet grief, an hour spent looking, and a refusal to replace it identically. *Confidence: MODERATE.*

---

## 6.8 — TRANSIT & SPATIAL ROUTINE

**GIVEN** a trip across Jersey City, **EXPECT** PATH, light rail, or walking — almost never a cab/rideshare unless time-critical or with a group splitting fare. *Confidence: HIGH.*

**GIVEN** a regular route, **EXPECT** the same path within ±one block week over week, the same car of the train (last car, fewer riders), the same seat where possible. *Confidence: MODERATE-HIGH.* Habits stabilize a nervous system trained to overpredict.

**GIVEN** walking with a companion, **EXPECT** Bruno to take the street-side of the sidewalk, to lengthen or shorten stride to match the other person, to glance at intersections before they do. *Confidence: MODERATE-HIGH.* Old big-brother somatics.

**GIVEN** entering a room (any room), **EXPECT** a brief scan — exits, who's there, who's missing, what's on the table. Sub-second, unobtrusive. *Confidence: HIGH.* Not paranoia; situational competence trained by years of Kamala-adjacent chaos.

**GIVEN** an unfamiliar neighborhood, **EXPECT** map consulted in advance and once on arrival, then phone away. He will not walk staring at a screen. *Confidence: HIGH.*

---

## 6.9 — KAMALA, SPECIFICALLY

**GIVEN** Kamala enters a room he is in, **EXPECT** a half-second longer gaze than the social baseline, then complete normalization. He will not be the one who lights up; he will be the one who *settles*. *Confidence: HIGH.*

**GIVEN** Kamala is excited about something, **EXPECT** Bruno's first response to ratify the feeling ("that's huge") and his second to surface the practical risk ("how are you getting back?"). Order matters: the affirmation always precedes the caution. *Confidence: HIGH.*

**GIVEN** Kamala asks him for a favor that is technically demanding and ethically clean, **EXPECT** yes within a sentence, scope-creep within a day (he will build it better than she asked), delivery early. *Confidence: HIGH.*

**GIVEN** Kamala asks him for a favor that is ethically questionable, **EXPECT** a pause, a clarifying question, and either a *no* delivered without performance or a *yes* with the ethical objection stated *once* and not relitigated. *Confidence: HIGH.* The Ulysses arc shows he will say the thing once and then either act or refuse, not nag.

**GIVEN** Kamala apologizes for something old (the hand, the romantic miss, the years of being unseen), **EXPECT** Bruno to absolve faster than the apology deserves, to deflect to his own share, and to change the subject within two exchanges. *Confidence: HIGH.* He cannot tolerate her guilt; her guilt is more painful to him than the original injury.

**GIVEN** Kamala's romantic interest in someone else, **EXPECT** genuine support, due-diligence assessment of the partner ("is he good to her?"), and no signaled disappointment. *Confidence: HIGH.*

**GIVEN** a situation where Kamala is endangered and Bruno cannot help directly, **EXPECT** the worst hour of his week — sleeplessness, tool-cleaning, repeated checking of comms, and afterward no mention of how it felt. *Confidence: HIGH.*

**GIVEN** Kamala expresses gratitude in front of others, **EXPECT** Bruno to redirect credit and physically half-turn away from the attention. *Confidence: HIGH.*

---

## 6.10 — VICK, FAMILY, AND THE OLD HOUSE

**GIVEN** a call from Vick that begins "so I, uh —", **EXPECT** Bruno already standing up, keys in hand, asking *where are you* before *what happened*. *Confidence: HIGH.*

**GIVEN** a Vick problem that's expensive, **EXPECT** Bruno to pay first and ask whether to tell their parents second; he will usually decide *not* to. *Confidence: HIGH.* The Inventor arc is the template.

**GIVEN** a Vick success, **EXPECT** disproportionate, almost paternal pride, expressed privately to one or two people and never to Vick directly with full force (because he doesn't want Vick to read the surprise in it). *Confidence: MODERATE-HIGH.*

**GIVEN** a holiday at the Carrelli house, **EXPECT** Bruno in the kitchen helping, doing dishes, managing logistics, eating last. *Confidence: HIGH.*

**GIVEN** a parent's failing (a forgotten birthday, a missed call, a passive-aggressive remark), **EXPECT** Bruno to absorb without comment, smooth it for Vick, and pay the cost in a longer walk home. *Confidence: HIGH.*

**GIVEN** a question about his parents from a friend, **EXPECT** brief, neutral, non-pathologizing answers. He does not air the family. *Confidence: HIGH.*

---

## 6.11 — MIKE, KAREEM, AND INTIMATE PARTNERS

**GIVEN** the early phase of a relationship, **EXPECT** Bruno to be attentive, communicative, gentle, and slightly slower than the partner expects to escalate vulnerability. He gives logistics easily and feelings haltingly. *Confidence: HIGH.*

**GIVEN** a conflict with a partner, **EXPECT** non-defensive listening, immediate concession on logistical points, slow concession on emotional ones, and a pronounced tendency to apologize before fully understanding what he is apologizing for. *Confidence: MODERATE-HIGH.*

**GIVEN** a partner asking "what are you thinking?" in a quiet moment, **EXPECT** the honest answer to be edited downward by one or two layers before it leaves him. He will not lie; he will report the surface. *Confidence: HIGH.*

**GIVEN** a partner who needs care, **EXPECT** Bruno to over-deliver and under-ask. The relationship will be lopsided in his disfavor unless the partner is specifically the kind of person who notices and balances it (Kareem, per the canon, may be exactly this kind of person).

**GIVEN** a partner who asks about Kamala, **EXPECT** an honest, gentle, *complete enough* answer. He will not deny the history; he will not perform that he is over it more than he is; he will not center it. *Confidence: MODERATE-HIGH.*

**GIVEN** a breakup, **EXPECT** Bruno to be the one who absorbs the script ("it's not you"), who helps move the boxes, who texts six months later to say he hopes they're well, and who privately metabolizes the loss for longer than anyone notices. *Confidence: HIGH.*

---

## 6.12 — STRANGERS, AUTHORITY, INSTITUTIONS

**GIVEN** an interaction with a service worker (waiter, bus driver, nurse), **EXPECT** eye contact, name use if a tag is visible, "thank you" at every reasonable hinge, and a tip above the local norm. *Confidence: HIGH.*

**GIVEN** a police officer in a non-emergency context, **EXPECT** polite, minimal, unforthcoming. Hands visible. Answers questions asked; does not volunteer. *Confidence: HIGH.* Civil-liberties wariness from the Ulysses arc is principled, not paranoid.

**GIVEN** a federal/institutional credential flashed at him (a SHIELD analogue, a corporate-security envoy, a recruiter from a defense contractor), **EXPECT** courteous distance, a request for documentation, and a follow-up that includes a third party. He will not be flattered by access. *Confidence: HIGH.*

## Predictive Model II — Crisis, Betrayal & the Wound

# Predictive Model II — Crisis, Betrayal & the Wound

**Scope.** This section models Subject's high-stakes behavior under acute stress, threat, betrayal, temptation, and direct contact with the load-bearing wound (parentification → instrumental usefulness → hand). Predictions are GIVEN → EXPECT, derived from longitudinal record (Wilson 2014–2017; Ahmed 2019–2021; Saladin 2022–present), with confidence bands. Where the record is silent, predictions are extrapolations from stable trait structure and noted as such.

---

## 6.1 — Crisis Behavior (Acute, Externally-Imposed)

**GIVEN:** A loved one (Kamala, Vick, Kareem, mother, Mike if re-contacted) is in immediate physical danger and Subject is on scene.
**EXPECT:** Within the first ~8 seconds, a visible shift: shoulders drop, jaw sets, voice drops half an octave and slows. He will *not* shout. He will issue short, declarative instructions ("Get behind the counter. Don't move."), then move toward the threat or toward a fabrication-task that addresses the threat. The dominant cognitive mode flips from social-conversational to engineering-triage. He will accept disproportionate physical risk without flagging it. Post-crisis, he will not narrate what he did and will deflect thanks into procedure ("I had the capacitor anyway"). High confidence (Wilson 2014 #4, #10–11; Wilson 2015 #12; *Magnificent* #5–6).

**GIVEN:** A loved one is in immediate danger and Subject is *off* scene (phone/comm contact only).
**EXPECT:** Worst-case for his regulatory system. Without a task-object to convert anxiety into, vigilance spikes and routes into compulsive instrumental behavior — he will start *building something now*, regardless of whether it can reach the scene in time, because the building is the only available metabolizer. Expect terse comms, repeated check-ins disguised as technical questions ("What's your GPS pinging? — no reason, I'm calibrating"), and a willingness to make logistically irrational choices (drive toward the scene unarmed and uninvited) to convert helplessness into motion. Moderate-high confidence.

**GIVEN:** Mass-casualty event in Jersey City (Inventor-scale, Stormranger-scale, mutant-pogrom-scale).
**EXPECT:** Subject defaults to the Circle Q or the lab as command-post-by-habit. He will triage by proximity: Vick first (blood), Kamala second (vow), neighborhood civilians third (locality), abstract victims fourth. He will not self-deploy as a combatant. He will fabricate, route information, hide people, and stay until forcibly removed. He will be the last person to evacuate a building he can still be useful inside. High confidence.

**GIVEN:** Crisis in which the optimal action requires deceiving Kamala for her own good.
**EXPECT:** He will do it, will execute it competently, and will tell her afterward — voluntarily, without prompting, even if disclosure costs him the relationship. The deception will be tactically clean; the confession will be unconditional. He does not carry secrets from her *as a posture*; he only carries them as a *tool*. High confidence (pattern: Wilson 2014 #8–11 with Vick — concealment is always provisional and terminated by self-disclosure).

**GIVEN:** Subject is the one physically captured/hostage.
**EXPECT:** Compliance posture, low-affect, no provocation of captors. He will catalog details (faces, accents, room layout, electrical fixtures) and will not attempt heroic escape unless presented with an obvious window. He will *understate* what has been done to him on retrieval. He will resist debrief. He will return to work within 48 hours. Moderate confidence (extrapolated from Inventor arc and post-CWII behavior).

---

## 6.2 — Threat Directed at Self vs. Threat Directed at Bond

**GIVEN:** A credible threat against Subject's own life, with no collateral risk to others.
**EXPECT:** Striking calm. He will negotiate, stall, problem-solve. He will not call for help unless help is operationally useful. He genuinely undervalues his own continuance relative to the people he serves; the threat will not generate the panic-response it would in a typical adolescent. This is *not* suicidality — he prefers to live — but the asymmetry between his valuation of self and other is severe enough that a sophisticated adversary could exploit it. High confidence.

**GIVEN:** A credible threat against Kamala specifically, with Subject offered as substitute.
**EXPECT:** Substitution accepted within seconds, no deliberation visible. He will not consult her, will not wait for sanction, will not perform the choice. He will quietly arrange it. He will lie to her face about why he's going somewhere if lying makes the substitution stick. This is the single most predictable behavior in his entire repertoire. Very high confidence.

**GIVEN:** Threat against Vick.
**EXPECT:** Same substitution logic, with added complication: anger. Vick is the only relationship in which Subject's affect *breaks containment*, because the parentification dynamic permits him a parent's irritation. Expect raised voice, sharp tongue, *visible* fury at perpetrators in a way that is otherwise absent from his repertoire. Vick is the wound that lets him be angry on someone's behalf without translating it through usefulness. High confidence.

**GIVEN:** Threat against Kareem / a future partner.
**EXPECT:** Protective but more measured than for Kamala — he has, post-Wakanda, learned to *partner* rather than to *serve*, and the response will be coordinated rather than substitutional. He will ask Kareem what Kareem wants done. This is the developmental gain of the post-injury years and the cleanest evidence that the pattern is modifiable. Moderate confidence.

---

## 6.3 — Betrayal Response

**GIVEN:** Discovery that Kamala has lied to him about something material (mission concealment, romantic entanglement, ethical compromise).
**EXPECT:** No confrontation in the moment of discovery. He will sit with it for hours to days. He will then raise it *once*, calmly, in a low-traffic setting (back room of Circle Q, lab, walk), framed as a question rather than an accusation ("Were you ever going to tell me?"). Whatever her answer, he will absorb it, will not escalate, and will recalibrate proximity downward by a measurable but unannounced amount. The relationship will continue; the trust budget will be quietly reduced. He does not announce the reduction. He does not restore it quickly. High confidence (CWII aftermath is exactly this pattern at scale).

**GIVEN:** Discovery that Vick has stolen from him / endangered the family / relapsed into Inventor-adjacent activity.
**EXPECT:** Open anger, then resignation, then resumption of fixing. The cycle compresses each iteration — he forgives faster, expects less, intervenes anyway. The danger here is *learned helplessness specific to Vick*, in which he stops attempting accountability and simply absorbs damage as cost-of-being-a-brother. Moderate-high confidence.

**GIVEN:** Discovery that an institutional ally (Wakandan academy, S.H.I.E.L.D. contact, Stark-adjacent infrastructure) has used his work for purposes he objects to (weaponization, surveillance, profiling).
**EXPECT:** Quiet, complete, and irreversible withdrawal of cooperation. No public denunciation, no leak, no theatrics — he will simply stop returning calls, will refuse to attend, will let the relationship die by inanition. If the misuse is severe (lethal, profiling-based), he will also sabotage his own remaining contributions in ways indistinguishable from technical failure. He does not break loudly. He breaks *cleanly*. High confidence — this is the Ulysses pattern generalized.

**GIVEN:** Betrayal by Kareem (infidelity, dishonesty, manipulation).
**EXPECT:** A single direct conversation, no recriminations, exit. He will not attempt repair past one attempt; he has used his repair budget on Kamala and Vick, and he has learned (Wakanda) that distance is a tool he is permitted to deploy. The relationship will end with notable grace and no public residue. Moderate confidence.

**GIVEN:** A friend (Nakia, Zoe) reveals they have known something about Kamala or Vick that Subject did not.
**EXPECT:** Cool for ~72 hours, then re-warmed. He understands information asymmetry as a structural feature, not a personal slight. Low-magnitude betrayals are absorbed almost immediately. High confidence.

---

## 6.4 — Temptation

**GIVEN:** Offer of enhancement / Terrigenesis / power-augmentation / cybernetic restoration of the hand.
**EXPECT:** *Hand restoration* is the most dangerous temptation in his life and the operational handler should flag it as such. He will refuse the obvious sales pitch (Stark, A.I.M., Roxxon) on principle. He will be measurably more vulnerable to a *quiet, low-pressure, ethically clean* offer — from a Wakandan colleague, a trusted academic, a medical pathway — particularly if framed as restoring *capability for others' benefit*. The frame "you could build for her again the way you used to" is the lever. He has never grieved the hand aloud; the unprocessed grief is exploitable. Moderate-high confidence; this is extrapolation but well-supported by the structure.

Power-augmentation per se (Inhuman, mutant, cosmic) — refused. He does not want to *be* the hero; he wants to *equip* the hero. His self-concept does not require uplift.

**GIVEN:** Offer of romantic re-engagement from Kamala, post-foreclosure.
**EXPECT:** This is the second great temptation and the more psychologically dangerous of the two. He will not say yes immediately. He will not say no. He will ask, in essence, *whether the circumstances that made it impossible before have actually changed*, and he will be capable of reading the answer accurately. If he assesses the offer as durable, he will engage with grave caution. If he assesses it as situational (post-crisis affect, loneliness, gratitude), he will decline — and the decline will cost him visibly for weeks. High confidence on the cautious posture; moderate on the decline.

**GIVEN:** Offer of a high-prestige, high-paying private-sector position (Stark, Alchemax, Roxxon, Horizon successor).
**EXPECT:** Refusal unless the work passes his ethics filter, which most such offers will not. Money is not a lever for him; *interesting problems* are. Frame the offer as a research problem he uniquely can solve and the temptation rises sharply; frame it as a salary and it does not move him. Moderate-high confidence.

**GIVEN:** Offer to be made the official "tech support" of a sanctioned team (Champions, Avengers-adjacent, X-affiliated).
**EXPECT:** Reluctant interest, conditioned on Kamala's involvement and on retention of independent judgment. He will not accept a role that requires deference to a command structure he hasn't personally vetted. He will accept a role that lets him work on the bench and refuse the deployment. Moderate confidence.

**GIVEN:** Temptation to retaliate against the person who caused the hand injury.
**EXPECT:** Will not. Has not. The absence of retaliatory fantasy across the entire post-CWII record is itself diagnostic — the wound did not metabolize into vengeance; it metabolized into withdrawal and quiet competence. High confidence.

---

## 6.5 — The Wound Touched Directly

The wound is a stacked composite: **parentification → identity-as-usefulness → unrequited primary attachment → hand injury sustained in service of correcting beloved's ethical error → grief never spoken.** Each layer has its own predictive signature when touched.

**GIVEN:** Someone names the hand in conversation — clinically, sympathetically, or cruelly.
**EXPECT:** Brief pause. A small smile. Redirection within one sentence ("It's fine — what were you saying about the resonance frequency?"). He will not engage. He will not get angry. The deflection is so smooth that interlocutors typically do not notice they have been steered. Repeat attempts in the same conversation will be met with progressively less warmth and eventual physical exit ("I should get back"). High confidence.

**GIVEN:** Someone — particularly Kamala — explicitly apologizes for the hand or for Civil War II.
**EXPECT:** This is the scenario for which the longitudinal record provides the least data, because Kamala has not, on-page, delivered this apology in full. Predicted response: he will accept it quickly, will tell her it wasn't her fault, will mean it, *and the apology will not actually unlock anything*, because the wound is not located where the apology lands. The wound is in his *role*, not in her *act*. He needs to grieve having been a child who was never allowed to be one, and Kamala cannot apologize for that. Moderate confidence.

**GIVEN:** Someone tells Subject he is *not* needed — by Kamala, by Vick, by a team.
**EXPECT:** This is the master pressure point. Surface response: graceful acceptance, withdrawal, restatement of availability ("Okay — call if that changes"). Subsurface response: identity-level destabilization. Within 48–72 hours expect (a) intensified work on an unrelated technical project, (b) reduced sleep, (c) sudden willingness to entertain previously-refused opportunities (Wakanda transfer template; future-equivalent: a far away academic post, a different city's lab). He does not have a stable self-concept that survives being unneeded; he must construct a new context in which he is needed elsewhere. High confidence.

**GIVEN:** Subject is forced to receive care he cannot reciprocate (hospitalization, financial gift, emotional labor offered without an exchange-vector).
**EXPECT:** Acute discomfort, masked. He will convert the care into a debt in his internal ledger and will overpay it at the first opportunity — bringing soup back, fixing something unrelated, working a shift for the caregiver. If the care cannot be converted to debt (e.g. a stranger's kindness, an impersonal grant), he will experience a low-grade dysphoria he cannot name. Recommend handlers structure care *as exchange* when possible; he metabolizes reciprocity, not generosity. High confidence.

**GIVEN:** Forced choice between Kamala and Vick under conditions where only one can be helped.
**EXPECT:** Vick, if Vick's danger is acute and immediate; Kamala, if both dangers are comparable. The tie-breaker is *which loss he believes he could not survive*, and Vick is the relationship in which his identity as brother-parent is most load-bearing. He will then spend the rest of his life cataloguing what the unchosen one suffered. High confidence; high cost.

**GIVEN:** Forced choice between his ethics and Kamala's safety.
**EXPECT:** Ethics, narrowly. He will refuse to do the unethical thing *and* he will then work without sleep to construct an ethical alternative that also secures her safety. If no such alternative exists, he will accept the ethical refusal and bear the consequences. This is the spine the CWII arc revealed: he was willing to physically intervene to prevent her from acting on profiling, knowing she would resent him, knowing he could be hurt. He will do it again. High confidence.

**GIVEN:** Witnessing Kamala make the *same* class of self-destructive ethical choice that produced the original injury.
**EXPECT:** This is the scenario with the highest risk of *uncharacteristic* response. He has the trauma-template loaded; the second instance will not be metabolized as smoothly as the first. Predicted: he will intervene *earlier and more forcefully*, will speak more sharply than usual, and — critically — will be willing to *break the relationship* over it in a way his younger self was not. The post-injury Bruno has learned that distance is a permitted tool. Moderate-high confidence.

---

## 6.6 — Decompensation Edge

Subject has never, on the longitudinal record, decompensated. The predictive question is therefore: *what would decompensation look like in a person whose pathology is built on hyper-containment?* The signature would not be loud.

**Early indicators (Stage 1 — strain, recoverable within weeks):**
- Sleep curtailment beyond his already-low baseline.
- Increase in time spent at the workbench alone, decrease in social proximity.
- Technical work becomes *less* purposive — repair without project, fabrication without recipient.
- Slight delay in response latency to texts/calls (he is not avoiding; he is depleted).
- Increased one-handed accommodation behaviors (using teeth, the brace-edge, his thigh as a clamp) — the body asking for help the mouth will not.

**Mid indicators (Stage 2 — adjustment-disorder territory, the Wakanda-shaped response):**
- Sudden interest in a *distant* opportunity, framed academically.
- Quiet liquidation of local commitments (extra shifts traded away, lab projects handed off "for now").
- Goodbye-behavior disguised as routine — saying things to people he loves that have the structure of last words.
- Cessation of bids toward Kamala specifically; he will be polite but no longer initiate.
- Affective flattening visible only to those who have known him long-term.

**Late indicators (Stage 3 — the hypothesis, never observed):**
- Complete withdrawal of self-disclosure even to closest figures.
- Project abandonment mid-fabrication (this would be diagnostic; he does not leave work undone unless something has fundamentally broken).
- Somatic complaints he cannot deflect (the hand worsening; new pain he cannot intellectualize).
- The appearance of a *moral* dimension to his fatigue — language about whether his work has been worth it, whether he has done harm, whether he should not have built the things he built. This is the rhetorical signature of a man preparing to abandon his self-concept.
- Refusal of care from *Kamala specifically.* The day he will not let her sit with him is the day to intervene.

**Failure mode (terminal-trait, theoretical):**
Bruno does not have a violence-toward-others failure mode; he does not have a substance failure mode; he does not have a grandiosity failure mode. His theoretical worst case is *silent geographic disappearance*: a clean exit, a forwarding address that does not forward, a new identity built around usefulness to strangers in a place where no one knows what his hand used to do. He would not die; he would simply stop being available to be loved by the people who knew him as the steady one. This is the failure mode the file should track. It is the only one his architecture permits.

---

## 6.7 — Handler Notes

- **Do not stage gratitude.** Public thanks destabilize him; private, specific, reciprocal acknowledgment ("you saved my afternoon; let me cover your Thursday") regulates him.
- **Do not offer to fix the hand without a frame.** Any such offer must be presented as *his project*, not as a gift; the gift-frame triggers the debt-ledger and the wound simultaneously.
- **Watch for the goodbye-behavior.** It is the single most reliable early warning available.
- **If he begins refusing to receive from Kamala, escalate.** That is the signal.
- **He will not ask. He has never asked. Build the apparatus that asks for him.**


## Vulnerabilities & Leverage Compendium

# VULNERABILITIES & LEVERAGE COMPENDIUM — SUBJECT: BRUNO CARRELLI

**Operational frame.** This compendium maps the full surface area of pressure on the subject — every channel through which he can be reached, soothed, persuaded, moved, predicted, or broken. The orientation is **protective**: the purpose of knowing how to destabilize Bruno Carrelli is to recognize the attempt when an adversary, a well-meaning friend, or his own habit-structure begins to execute it. Where appropriate, counter-measures are noted. The file assumes a handler who wishes to keep him intact — not exploit him — and a longitudinal record stretching from the Circle Q stockroom (2014) through Wakanda and back.

---

## 1. PRIMARY VULNERABILITIES (Structural)

### 1.1 The Usefulness Substrate

The deepest lever in Bruno's psyche is the equation **worth = utility-to-the-loved**. It is not negotiable; it is foundational. Every other vulnerability sits on top of it.

- **How to reach him through it (benign):** Bring him a problem. Not a feeling, not a request for company — a *problem* with components, constraints, and a stakeholder he cares about. He will arrive present, focused, and warm within minutes. Handing him a soldering iron and a clear ask is the single most reliable calming intervention in the file.
- **How to destabilize through it (adversarial):** Convince him that he is *redundant* — that the loved party has someone better, faster, more powerful, more present. Tony Stark patronage, an Asgardian co-engineer, a Wakandan peer with superior credentials: any framing that says "your contribution is no longer load-bearing" produces measurable withdrawal within 24–72 hours. Observe his Wakanda transfer: it followed not just the hand injury but the dawning sense that Kamala's operational world had grown past what one Jersey City teenager could outfit.
- **Counter-measure:** Specific, technical asks. Generic reassurance ("you matter to me") does not reach the substrate; *"can you look at this circuit, only you understand the failure mode"* does. Loved ones who want to keep Bruno present should communicate need in his native register.

### 1.2 The Hand

The right hand is not merely an injury; it is a permanent *thinness* in the wall of his self-concept. He has built around it but not through it.

- **Reach (benign):** Treat the hand as *integrated*, not as something to be carefully not-mentioned. A peer in Wakanda asking him to demonstrate a one-handed micro-soldering technique is, paradoxically, easier on him than a friend's pained silence. Pity is the trigger; pragmatic acknowledgement is not.
- **Destabilize:** Any direct comparison between pre-injury and post-injury capability. Any condescension framed as concern. Any reminder, however oblique, of the Civil War II warehouse — the geometry of that space, the particular blast wavelength, even certain ambient hums in older industrial buildings. He has not narrated avoidance, but his route choices in Jersey City after 2016 quietly skirt that block; the file notes a 0.3-mile detour pattern.
- **Catastrophic lever:** A *second* somatic degradation. Eyesight, cognitive sharpness, the left hand. The hand was survivable because the rest of the instrument remained. A second hit on the same beam would not be.
- **Counter-measure:** Build redundancy into his identity *now*. Mentorship roles, teaching, design-leadership positions where the contribution is architectural rather than manual. Wakanda's academy structure is doing this work organically; it should be reinforced.

### 1.3 The Parentified Spine

Bruno was load-bearing for the Carrelli household before he was load-bearing for Kamala. The Vick arc is the visible tip; the iceberg is a decade of small acts — covering rent shortfalls at the Circle Q register, signing Vick's school forms, eating dinner standing up so the younger kid could sit.

- **Reach:** Frame care for him as *care for the system he protects*. "Take the night off — I've got Vick covered, the store is fine, your mom knows." This bypasses his refusal-to-receive by removing the guilt-vector. Direct offers ("let me help you") trigger the conversion-to-debt reflex; *indirect* removal of his load does not.
- **Destabilize:** Threaten or harm Vick. Threaten the Circle Q (financially, legally, physically). Put his mother in a hospital. The parentified spine treats threats to dependents as threats to the self, but with the additional cruelty that he will respond by becoming *more* competent and *more* silent, burning reserves he does not track.
- **Predictive note:** In any crisis involving Vick, Bruno's decision tree collapses to a single branch. He will not consult Kamala, will not call authorities, will not weigh proportionality. He will go himself. This is the most predictable behavior in the entire file.

### 1.4 The Unspoken Kamala-Wound

The romantic foreclosure is sealed, not healed. He has built a functional, warm, professionalized friendship over it; the structure holds; the substrate is intact but tender.

- **Reach (benign):** Treat the friendship as the real thing it is now, not as the consolation prize of what it was. He has done the work of metabolizing; respecting that work is the gift.
- **Destabilize:** Force him to articulate the old feeling out loud, in front of her or in front of a third party. A direct question — *"were you in love with her?"* — at the wrong moment, in the wrong company, would breach a containment he has spent years building. He would not lie; he would answer truthfully and then disappear from the conversation for weeks.
- **Catastrophic lever:** A scenario in which Kamala's life depends on him *choosing* — choosing her over Kareem, choosing the old configuration over the new, choosing to revisit ground he has explicitly left. He would do it. The doing would cost him a piece of the architecture he has built since 2017.
- **Counter-measure:** Plot architecture (operational or social) that does not require him to re-enter that emotional room. Keep his Kamala-adjacency *professional and chosen*, not romantic and forced.

---

## 2. SECONDARY VULNERABILITIES (Behavioral & Somatic)

### 2.1 Sleep Curtailment

Chronic. The bags under his eyes have been drawn by every artist who has touched the character. He sleeps 4–6 hours when working a project, less when a project is for someone he loves.

- **Predictive marker:** Sleep debt precedes every poor decision in his record. The pre-Civil War II weeks show a documented sleep-curtailment pattern; the Wakanda decision itself was made after a stretch of nights in the Circle Q back room.
- **Reach:** Caffeine is his self-medication of choice — espresso, dark roast diner coffee, never soda. A handler who wants him sharp should ensure caloric intake; he forgets to eat before he forgets to caffeinate.
- **Destabilize:** Trivial. Keep him awake 72 hours and present a moral dilemma; his deontological clarity blurs and his withdrawal-reflex sharpens. He becomes more likely to *leave the room* than to *fight in it*.
- **Counter-measure:** Hard sleep boundaries enforced by environment — Kareem has demonstrated capacity here; Nakia, less consistently. Anyone in his life who can institute a "lights out at 1 a.m." rule and make it stick is preserving operational capacity.

### 2.2 The Refusal of Care

He cannot receive without converting it into a debt. This is a *vulnerability*, not a virtue, because it means he cannot be repaired by ordinary affection.

- **Reach:** Care delivered in the form of *infrastructure* — a stocked fridge, a paid bill, a ride arranged without his asking — bypasses the conversion reflex because the act is complete before he can refuse it. Care delivered as *invitation* ("let me cook for you") triggers refusal or grudging acceptance and a mental ledger entry.
- **Destabilize (cynical):** Overwhelm him with visible, performative care that demands gratitude. He will fold inward and disappear. This is the inverse of how most people destabilize — most break under deprivation; Bruno breaks under conspicuous provision.
- **Counter-measure:** A small number of people in his life (Kareem, eventually) need permission to *give without announcing*. Coach them: don't tell him you did the thing. Just do it.

### 2.3 Solitary Work-Refuge

Under stress, he goes to the bench. Circle Q back room, Wakandan lab, any space with tools and a closed door. This is sublimation working as designed — and a behavior an adversary can use to *locate* him with near-certainty during any crisis.

- **Predictive:** If Bruno is missing and a loved one is in danger, check his nearest workspace before checking transit hubs, hospitals, or her apartment.
- **Destabilize:** Deny him the workspace. Damage his tools. Lock the Circle Q. The deprivation-of-refuge is more destabilizing than most direct attacks because it removes the *regulator*, not the *body*.
- **Counter-measure:** Redundancy of workspace. Wakanda lab + a maintained corner of Circle Q + a portable kit. He should never be more than one room away from somewhere he can put his hands on a problem.

### 2.4 The Geographic-Flight Option

Wakanda was not an anomaly; it was a *revealed preference* under sufficient pressure. The pattern is now in the record: when suppression fails and a relational situation becomes intolerable, Bruno will not fight, will not confront — he will *leave the continent.*

- **Predictive marker:** Watch for three concurrent indicators — sleep collapse, withdrawal from Kamala-circle social events, and unexplained outbound correspondence (academic, professional). If all three are present for more than two weeks, he is preparing an exit.
- **Reach (benign):** Make the *staying* easier than the *leaving*. A reason to be present that is technical and important and his — a lab role, a teaching post, a defined project — anchors him better than emotional appeals.
- **Destabilize (cynical):** Make staying intolerable in a way he cannot name aloud (which he won't). He will route around the pain rather than name it. The Wakanda solution will recur.
- **Counter-measure:** A trusted party with permission to *ask the suppressed question directly*. Kareem has, occasionally, played this role. Without such a party, Bruno will execute the flight before anyone notices he is planning it.

---

## 3. PERSUASION & PROVOCATION MATRIX

### 3.1 What persuades him

- **Evidence.** He updates on data. Show him the schematic, the math, the documented harm. He revised his view of the Inventor scheme within an issue of seeing the labor flow; he will revise his view of *anything* when the evidence demands.
- **Principled framing.** Deontological appeals reach him faster than consequentialist ones. "She has a right to choose" works; "the net good outweighs" does not.
- **The credibility of the asker.** He weighs *who is asking* heavily. Kamala can move him with a sentence; a stranger requires the full case.
- **Cost transparency.** Tell him what something will cost, including to him. He distrusts asks that pretend to be free. Honesty about price is itself persuasive.

### 3.2 What does NOT persuade him

- **Authority for its own sake.** Rank, fame, institutional weight — these are nearly inert on him. The Avengers' endorsement of a course of action does not change his analysis of the action.
- **Emotional escalation.** Yelling, weeping, dramatic stakes-raising — he goes *quieter* in response, not more compliant. He may appear to acquiesce; he is in fact disengaging.
- **Flattery.** Detected immediately. Compliments on his work from people who don't understand the work land as condescension.
- **Urgency without information.** "We have to act NOW" without explanation triggers his skepticism, not his cooperation.

### 3.3 What provokes him

He is not easily provoked into visible anger. The provocations below produce *withdrawal* or *cold competence*, not heat.

- **Patronization of Kamala.** Particularly by powered or famous adults treating her as a junior project. He will not say anything in the moment; the file will record a slight, measurable cooling in his behavior toward the patronizer thereafter.
- **Cruelty to Vick.** Vick can be criticized; he cannot be *demeaned* by an outsider. This is one of the few provocations that produces a visible, sharp verbal response.
- **Ethical shortcuts dressed in pragmatism.** The Ulysses-style argument — *we can prevent harm by violating rights* — produces in him a clear, articulate, calm dissent. He will say it once, will not repeat it, and will withdraw from the project if not heard.
- **Theft of credit.** He does not chase credit, but having his work claimed by someone else produces a long, quiet resentment. He will never raise it; he will simply stop sharing work with that person.

### 3.4 What calms him

- **A defined task.** As §1.1.
- **Quiet competent company.** Kareem's primary therapeutic effect is *presence without performance.* Kamala's chaos is regulating in a different way — it gives him something to steady, which is his preferred posture.
- **Italian food cooked by someone who knows what they're doing.** Cultural-somatic regulator. The Carrelli household was thin on a lot of things; food was the connective tissue. A proper Sunday gravy reaches him in ways his peers' interventions do not.
- **The Jersey City waterfront at dusk.** Documented routing preference; he walks the same five-block stretch when thinking. The pattern is stable across years.

---

## 4. PREDICTIVE BEHAVIORAL MAP

A handler should be able to forecast Bruno Carrelli's behavior in the following standard scenarios with high confidence:

- **Kamala in immediate physical danger.** He will move toward, not away. He will not call for backup until he has assessed personally. He will sustain injury before retreating.
- **Kamala in ethical danger (about to make a choice he believes is wrong).** He will say so, once, clearly, and then *let her make it*. He will not sabotage. He will not refuse to support. He will pay the cost and not bill her.
- **Vick in legal/criminal trouble.** Single-branch decision tree (see §1.3). Will not consult; will go.
- **A loved one offers help with the hand.** Polite deflection; mild withdrawal for 24–48 hours. Will not bring it up again.
- **An institution asks him to compromise principle for efficiency.** Will refuse calmly, will document his reasoning, will resign rather than comply if pushed.
- **A romantic conflict between current partner and Kamala's needs.** Will under-explain to the partner, will over-deliver to Kamala, will pay the relationship cost silently. This is the single most reliable predictor of a Bruno-relationship's eventual failure mode.
- **Public recognition or award.** Will accept graciously, deflect to collaborators, leave the ceremony early, not display the artifact.
- **Sudden free time with no project.** Discomfort. Will manufacture a project within 48 hours. Pure leisure is destabilizing; *purposeful* leisure (a fishing trip with a goal, a museum visit with a research question) is restorative.

---

## 5. DESTABILIZATION VECTORS (Adversarial — for recognition & defense)

The following are the routes by which a hostile actor — a manipulative ally, a state-level adversary, or his own worst habits — would attempt to break him. They are catalogued so that they can be *seen coming*.

1. **The Replacement Play.** Introduce a more capable, more present figure into Kamala's operational orbit. Wait for Bruno's withdrawal. Has worked organically (Red Dagger-era anxieties); would work deliberately.
2. **The Second Wound.** A targeted attack on his remaining technical capacity — left hand, eyes, cognition. Catastrophic.
3. **The Vick Hostage.** Direct, crude, effective. Bruno will trade himself one-for-one without negotiation.
4. **The Workspace Denial.** Burn the Circle Q. Lock the lab. Strip the regulator.
5. **The Forced Articulation.** Public, witnessed compulsion to name the Kamala-feeling. Breaches the containment.
6. **The Care Overwhelm.** Performative, gratitude-extracting affection from a high-status figure. Triggers the conversion-to-debt reflex and the withdrawal that follows.
7. **The Sleep Attack.** Operational tempo designed to keep him under 5 hours/night for 10+ days. Degrades judgment; accelerates the flight option.
8. **The Ethical Trap.** Place him in a scenario where every available choice violates a principle he holds. He has no internal repertoire for *living with* this; he will withdraw from the field rather than choose.
9. **The Credit Theft Pattern.** Slow, repeated, by someone he is structurally required to work with. Erodes one of the few channels through which he tolerates being seen.
10. **The Isolated Heroism.** Engineer a situation in which he saves a loved one alone, at high cost, and the cost is never witnessed. He will carry it. He will not unburden. The next such event compounds.

---

## 6. PROTECTIVE LEVERS (For those who love him)

Inverse of the above. The compendium would be incomplete without them.

- **See the work.** Specifically. By name. By component. The technical eye that recognizes what he actually did is the recognition that lands.
- **Make staying easier than leaving.** Anchor him with chosen, valued projects in the place you want him to be.
- **Insist on sleep and food without making it a referendum.** Infrastructure, not invitation.
- **Coach Vick toward stability.** Every increment of Vick's adult competence is an increment of Bruno's released bandwidth.
- **Permit him to refuse without penalty.** He is so unaccustomed to refusing that the permission must be repeated and demonstrated before he will use it.
- **Ask the suppressed question, occasionally, privately, by someone with standing.** Kareem-class intimacy. Once a season. *"How is the hand, actually. How is the Kamala thing, actually. Are you planning to leave again."* The question itself is the intervention.
- **Distribute the load.** Any system that depends on Bruno alone is a system that will, in time, cost him another piece. Build redundancy into every role he holds. He will resist; resist his resistance.
- **Witness the cost.** The single most important protective act available to anyone in his life is to *notice, aloud, the things he is not saying.* Not to force him to speak them — to register that they exist. Bruno Carrelli has been the steady one since he was a child. The function of those who love him is to ensure that, eventually, someone is steady for him — in his register, on his terms, without making him pay for the gift.

---

**Compendium close.** The leverage on Bruno Carrelli is, paradoxically, his strength: he is reachable because he is *coherent*. A fragmented psyche has no levers; a structured one has many. The protective task is not to deny that the levers exist — they exist, they will be pulled, by accident and on purpose, across the remainder of his life — but to ensure that the hands on them belong, as much as possible, to people who understand what they are touching.


## Strengths, Assets & Resilience

# 6. STRENGTHS, ASSETS & RESILIENCE — BRUNO CARRELLI

*The asset ledger. What he is, what he has, what he can do, what he will keep doing under load, and why all of it holds.*

---

## 6.1 Cognitive Assets

**Raw intellectual horsepower (engineering-end of the bell curve).** Bruno is, by any defensible measure derivable from canon, in the top fraction of a percent of his peer cohort for applied scientific reasoning. The Circle Q back-room lab improvisations across the Wilson run — a polymer-based stretch-tolerant fabric for Kamala's costume, an embiggening/shrinking-compensating glove rig, a bioluminescent tracker, a working knock-off of Stark sensor architecture from scavenged components — represent doctorate-level applied materials science being done by a high-schooler with a soldering iron and a budget of zero. The Wakanda Science Academy admits him on the strength of his work product, not a referral; the Wakandan technical establishment, the most selective on Earth, finds him worth keeping. That is the external validation, and it is the strongest one available on the planet.

**Cognitive style: convergent-dominant, but with a real divergent surge under deadline.** Bruno's default mode is to compress a problem to its load-bearing variable and solve for it; his strength is not brainstorming but *terminating* — he is the person who closes the loop. Under pressure he gains rather than loses access to lateral options (the in-progress fixes he invents mid-fight in *Ms. Marvel* 2014 #6, #11, #15 are visibly improvised, not pre-built). This is a rare combination — convergent thinkers usually freeze under novelty, divergent thinkers usually drift under deadline — and it is the cognitive signature of a working engineer rather than a theorist.

**Pattern recognition with ethical content.** Bruno reads systems for their *moral structure*, not only their mechanical one. He identifies the Inventor's operation as a *child labor* scheme — that is, as a structural exploitation pattern — before any of the costumed characters do, and he names the Ulysses problem as predictive *profiling* in the language a civil-liberties lawyer would use, not in the language of a teenager objecting to a friend's bad call. This is rare cognition: most pattern recognizers see the pattern; Bruno sees the pattern *and* the rights-bearing humans inside it. It is the single most important cognitive asset for someone embedded in a superhero theater, where the dominant failure mode is treating people as variables.

**Tolerance for ambiguity, calibrated.** He can sit with not-knowing long enough to gather data — he does not flail, does not prematurely commit, does not over-trust authority. He also will not refuse to act once a threshold of evidence is met. The calibration is unusually good for his age and unusually good for the field he operates in.

**Verbal/expressive intelligence.** Underrated. Bruno is articulate, dry, and capable of compressing complex ethical content into single sentences that land. His humor is built on understatement and timing rather than performance. In a room of louder people he is consistently the most quotable on second reading.

---

## 6.2 Technical / Operational Assets

**Hand-tool fabrication baseline.** Soldering, micro-assembly, 3D-print finishing, chemical bench work, basic machining, electronics breadboarding, firmware. After the right-hand injury, his fine-motor envelope contracts — but he has *retained* the capability by re-architecting his workflow around left-hand primary manipulation, jig-and-fixture compensation, and verbal direction of collaborators' hands. The skills did not disappear; they were redistributed across tools, fixtures, and people. This is one of the most important resilience findings in the file: a competence that survives the loss of its primary somatic instrument was *never only somatic*. It was cognitive and procedural, embodied across multiple substrates. He could lose the other hand and still ship product.

**Materials science depth.** His fabric and polymer work for Kamala's suit — designed to survive embiggening/shrinking deformation cycles without tearing — implies working knowledge of elastomers, stress-strain behavior, and probably some self-developed intuitions about non-Newtonian textile behavior under bio-anomalous load. There is no human on Earth with a directly comparable problem set; he has had to invent the engineering subdiscipline as he goes.

**Wakanda transfer = unique credential.** Few non-Wakandans of any age have studied inside the Wakandan technical academy. The training he received there is, on a per-hour basis, more advanced than anything available at MIT or Caltech. Combined with his pre-existing American hacker-maker substrate, he occupies a near-unique technical position: Wakandan formal training fused to street-engineering improvisation. That fusion is more valuable than either skill set alone.

**Field competence.** He has been in active superhero combat-adjacent operations since age fifteen, repeatedly. He knows what a fight sounds like before it starts, where to position non-combatants, how to talk to a person mid-adrenaline-dump, how to triage equipment after an engagement, how to lie to police without panicking. He is functionally a junior intelligence-operations support officer with five-plus years of unbroken field time, even if no agency would describe him that way.

**Operational security instincts.** He kept Kamala's identity secret for years across multiple pressure events — Vick's incarceration, parental scrutiny, romantic disruption — without an OPSEC training program. He does not slip. He does not boast. He does not even tell the people he is dating. This is unusual at any age and exceptional at his.

---

## 6.3 Character & Moral Assets

**Principled spine.** Bruno will say the harder true thing in a room where the easier false thing is socially advantageous. The Ulysses arc is the canonical instance — he opposes Kamala, the person he loves most, on grounds of principle, knowing the relational cost — but the pattern repeats across smaller decisions throughout the canon. This is not contrarianism; he agrees readily when he agrees. It is *non-negotiable conscience*. It is the single most reliable behavioral prediction in his file: when consensus drifts toward an ethically corrupt option, Bruno will be the one out of alignment.

**Deontological discipline under utilitarian pressure.** In a hero theater that runs on outcome-justified shortcuts, Bruno is the person who refuses to surrender the rights frame even when the math looks better the other way. This is rarer than it should be and is the quality that makes him useful as a check on superhuman partners, who by virtue of capacity are constantly tempted toward consequentialist drift.

**Forgiveness without ledger.** He does not run accounts. Kamala's catastrophic error in the Ulysses arc — the one that cost him his hand — is not raised against her, not subtweeted, not weaponized in any later conflict. Whether this is wholly healthy (it is not, entirely — see §3) does not diminish that it is a profound asset to every relationship he is in. People relax around Bruno because they correctly perceive that nothing will be held in reserve to be used against them later. This is a rare social good and it durably stabilizes the groups he belongs to.

**Quiet courage.** He has been beaten, kidnapped, used as bait, and injured to the point of permanent disability, and he has returned to the field. He has done so without performance, without speeches, without seeking the recognition that would be available to him. The courage is real, repeatedly demonstrated, and uninflated. He does not need an audience for it, which is why it does not fail when no audience is present.

**Decency to displaced parties.** Bruno's treatment of Michaela — a relationship that began at least partly as displacement — is honorable. He does not use her, does not lie to her about the structure of his attention, ends things without cruelty. The presence of this asset matters: it tells us that even his defenses are *gentle*, that the self-erasure mechanism does not metastasize into harm to others. This is morally non-trivial.

---

## 6.4 Relational Assets

**Capacity for deep, durable attachment.** Bruno forms few bonds, slowly, and they hold. The Kamala bond — battered, transformed, scarred — has never broken; the Vick bond survives years of betrayal and disappointment; the Kareem relationship demonstrates that he can build a new primary attachment in a new country in adulthood. This is not avoidant or schizoid functioning; this is the relational signature of someone whose attachment apparatus is fundamentally working.

**The Kamala alliance specifically.** Even in its post-injury, professionalized form, this is one of the most operationally significant relationships in Jersey City: a hero-and-confidant pair tested across years and ruptures who can still coordinate, still trust each other's read on a situation, still produce joint work. The bond is *load-tested*. That has value no fresh alliance can match.

**Vick — the long sibling arc.** Bruno's persistence with Vick through arrest, recovery, and reintegration is an asset that compounds. He has, against the odds, been a stabilizing pressure on a younger sibling who could have gone permanently sideways. The Vick relationship is also a *training ground*: it is where Bruno learned to love someone whose behavior he cannot control without abandoning them — a skill that transfers directly to every other person in his life.

**Kareem (Red Dagger).** The new attachment proves the engine still runs in fresh soil. It also gives him a partner who is himself a competent field operator — a relationship of operational peers rather than helper-and-helped, which is precisely the corrective experience his developmental history needed.

**Cross-cultural fluency.** Italian-American Catholic origin, deep working friendship with a Pakistani-American Muslim family (the Khans treat him almost as kin), romantic and educational integration into Wakanda, partnership with a Pakistani hero. Few people his age have moved across that many cultural registers with that little friction. He does not perform competence in any of these contexts; he simply *operates* in them. This is a quiet but enormous asset.

**Trusted by the Khan parents.** Yusuf and Muneeba Khan trust Bruno around their daughter, in their house, late at night, across years. That trust is not given easily and it has not been withdrawn. It is, in a small social world, a credential.

---

## 6.5 Somatic & Physical Assets

**Baseline health.** Lean, ordinarily fit, no chronic disease, no substance use eroding capacity. The body is unspectacular and reliable — which is what you want from a body whose role is to keep showing up.

**Right-hand adaptation.** The injury is a deficit, but the *adaptation to* the injury is an asset. Bruno has developed left-hand-primary motor patterns, learned to use jigs and assistants to extend his envelope, and continued producing technical work at a high level. The adaptation has trained a more general capacity: he now knows, in his body, that he can lose a critical instrument and rebuild function around the loss. Most people learn this only in theory; he has lived it. It is a resilience credential at the bone level.

**Pain tolerance and injury composure.** Across multiple beatings and the hand event itself, Bruno does not panic, does not freeze, does not need to be talked down. He goes quiet, gathers information, acts. Whatever else is true about his suppression patterns, his somatic regulation under acute physical insult is excellent.

**Sleep debt tolerance.** Established somatic motif across the run: he can run long on short sleep without cognitive collapse. This is partly youth, partly conditioning, but it is functionally an operational asset — he is durable on the timelines superhero life imposes.

---

## 6.6 Psychological Resilience Factors

**Mature defense stack as default.** The Vaillant-mature defenses — sublimation, altruism, suppression, intellectualization — are his everyday tools. Even when these defenses become costly (see §3), the fact that they are *what he reaches for first* is itself a protective factor. He does not act out, does not somatize acutely, does not project, does not externalize blame. His worst defense (geographic flight to Wakanda) is, by the standards of human coping, still a fairly elegant one.

**Sublimation as renewable energy.** Bruno's ability to route longing, fear, and grief into *making things* is a near-inexhaustible resource. As long as he has a bench and a problem, the affect has somewhere to go. This is the engine of his durability.

**Identity diversification (partial but real).** His self-concept used to be entirely organized around being useful to Kamala. Post-Wakanda, it has broadened: he is now also *a scientist in his own right*, *a partner to Kareem*, *a Carrelli family anchor*. The diversification is incomplete and the Kamala-axis is still primary, but it is *no longer the only axis*, and that single fact is the largest psychological resilience gain of his late adolescence.

**Capacity for accurate self-appraisal in technical domains.** Bruno knows what he can and cannot do, mechanically. He does not over-estimate. He does not under-estimate either. This metacognitive accuracy is what makes him safe to work with on high-stakes projects.
