**Capacity to exit.** The Wakanda transfer, whatever else it was, demonstrated that he *can* leave a situation that is destroying him. He does not have the trapped-helper's worst trait, which is the inability to walk away. He walked. This proves the door exists.

**Absence of substance escape route.** He has not built any chemical bypass into his coping repertoire. The resilience apparatus he has built is the one he will still have at forty.

**Humor as regulator.** Dry, understated, consistent across the canon. He uses it to take pressure off rooms, including his own. Humor that does not require an audience is humor that will still work when he is alone, which is most of when he needs it.

---

## 6.7 Material, Social & Institutional Assets

**Wakandan academic credential and network.** Possibly his most valuable single asset. Access to faculty, alumni, and institutions almost no one on Earth has access to. A door he can use for the rest of his life.

**Jersey City civilian network.** The Circle Q, the Khans' home, the neighborhood. He is *known* in his patch of the city — by shop owners, neighbors, classmates' parents. This is small-scale but real social capital, the kind that makes a person hard to disappear and easy to vouch for.

**A safe house in plain sight.** The Circle Q back room has functioned as lab, infirmary, planning room, and refuge across years without exposure. The location is operational infrastructure that costs him nothing and that no adversary has compromised.

**Bilingual cultural capital.** Italian-American Catholic literacy plus deep working familiarity with Pakistani-American Muslim domestic life plus Wakandan acculturation. He can read the room across three cultural matrices most people cannot read across one.

**A relationship with a sovereign-state-adjacent operator (Red Dagger).** Inadvertently, by virtue of his partnerships, Bruno has soft channels into Pakistani superhero infrastructure and Wakandan technical infrastructure. He does not exploit these. They exist.

**Reputation as the trustworthy one.** Across every cohort he has been in, the consensus reads of Bruno is *reliable, principled, will not betray you*. This reputation is the slowest-built and most valuable social asset a person can have. He has it at nineteen-ish. It will compound.

---

## 6.8 Failure-Mode Resistances (what does NOT break him)

- **Public humiliation:** he metabolizes it without retaliation; ego is not the load-bearing structure.
- **Asymmetric loyalty:** he is calibrated for it; it does not destabilize him.
- **Loss of a relationship's original form:** the Kamala bond changed shape and he absorbed the change without rupturing the bond itself.
- **Loss of a body part's full function:** survived; reorganized around.
- **Geographic dislocation:** Wakanda proved he transplants.
- **Long-term low recognition for high contribution:** he has lived in this condition continuously and shows no resentment buildup that has translated into action.
- **Being wrong:** rare, but when it happens he updates. He does not defend a position past its evidence.
- **Being right while alone:** the Ulysses arc proved he can hold a correct minority position under social pressure without collapsing.

---

## 6.9 Synthesis — Why the Assets Hold

Bruno Carrelli's strength profile is unusual in that nearly every asset is *durable* rather than peak. He is not the strongest, fastest, or most brilliant person in any room he walks into; he is, with high reliability, the person still functioning in that room in hour six. The asset stack is built on substrates that compound over time — character, principle, technical procedure encoded into both hands and habits, relationships maintained across years of strain, defenses that are mature even when over-used. There is no single capability here that an adversary could remove to disable him; the hand injury was the universe's best attempt at that and he routed around it inside a year.

The cost of this resilience is the matter of §3 and §7 — self-erasure, displaced longing, an under-tended interior life. But the *positive ledger* is enormous, and it is the ledger that explains how a non-powered nineteen-year-old has remained operationally indispensable in a theater dominated by gods, mutants, and Inhumans for half a decade without dying, breaking, or selling anyone out.

He is, in the most precise sense available to this dossier, **load-bearing infrastructure with a conscience**. Few assets in any file are more valuable than that.


## Failure Modes & Decompensation

# 6. FAILURE MODES & DECOMPENSATION — BRUNO CARRELLI

**Operational summary up front:** Bruno does not fail loudly. He has, across a decade of canon, never produced a single panel of screamed rage, smashed object, drunken collapse, suicidal ideation, or breakdown weeping. This is not because he cannot break. It is because his break, when it comes, has the morphology of a *fade*, not a *fracture*. He decompensates by **subtraction** — of presence, of speech, of geography, of self — and the surveillance task is to recognize subtraction as a clinical event rather than as the absence of one. The single most diagnostically important sentence in this file is this: *the Wakanda transfer was a decompensation episode that was successfully camouflaged as a résumé line.*

What follows is the longitudinal failure-mode map.

---

## 6.1 The Baseline Against Which Failure Is Measured

To recognize Bruno breaking, one must first recognize Bruno **functioning**, because the difference is subtle and easily misread as mood.

Functioning Bruno: sleeps four to six hours, works the Circle Q closing shift, runs a parallel workbench (basement / back-room / Wakandan lab), maintains low-affect humor with Kamala (deadpan, the straight-man register), takes Vick's phone calls without complaint, eats irregularly but reliably, makes minor self-deprecating jokes about his own competence, *initiates technical conversation* with the people he loves as his primary love-language.

These last two are the canaries. Self-deprecating humor and *initiation of technical conversation* are the two behaviors that go dark first when Bruno is decompensating. When he stops making the small jokes — when his contributions become purely answers to questions asked of him — he is already three steps into the decline. When he stops bringing a half-finished project to Kamala unbidden ("look at this — I think I can make the morphogen field stabilize if—"), the structural withdrawal has begun.

---

## 6.2 The Escalation Path — Stages of Subtraction

Bruno's decompensation follows a near-stereotyped five-stage descent. The progression is observable across the Civil War II → Wakanda arc (the only fully-documented full-cycle decompensation in the longitudinal record) and replicates in micro-form during smaller stressors (Vick's relapses, Kamala's apparent deaths, the Stormranger arc, the mutant-cohort displacement of his role).

### Stage 1 — Hyperfunction (Compensated Distress)

The first sign that something is wrong is that Bruno gets *better at his job*. Sleep contracts further. Output increases. The workbench acquires a second project, then a third. He is producing redundancy — backups, contingencies, gadgets Kamala has not asked for and may not need. The hand-drawn evidence: artists draw the lab cluttered, multiple in-progress armatures, soldering iron warm. Eye bags deepen. He does not ask anyone for anything.

This stage is **invisible to civilians and most peers** because it presents as virtue. It is recognizable only against the baseline: the *ratio* of giving-to-receiving, already lopsided, becomes grotesque. He answers every text within minutes. He covers shifts for Kareem or for Aamir's friends without being asked. He fixes the Circle Q register before Mr. Blevin notices it is broken. Hyperfunction in Bruno is a tell because *equilibrium-Bruno is already overfunctioning*; the escalation is from a baseline most people would call burnout.

**Duration:** weeks to months. This is the longest stage and the most missable.

### Stage 2 — Linguistic Retreat into Technical Register

The intellectualization defense, which is normally one tool among several, becomes the only tool. Conversations that used to braid affect and engineering ("I'm worried about her — also her gauntlet's pulling left") become pure engineering ("the gauntlet's pulling left"). When pressed on the affective content, he routes the answer through metaphor or hardware: *the suit needs a stabilizer*, not *I'm scared*. *We should run a diagnostic*, not *something's wrong with us*.

He becomes *slightly more articulate* on technical matters and *measurably less articulate* on emotional ones — beats of silence before he answers personal questions, more "I dunno" and "it's fine" and "don't worry about it," more deflection through small humor that lands flatter than usual. He starts to **agree more**. Bruno-functioning argues with Kamala; Bruno-decompensating just builds what she asks for.

This stage was visible across the run-up to the Civil War II break: Wilson's scripting tightens his dialogue around the Ulysses ethics question into pure principle-speak, with the personal stake — *I cannot watch you do this to yourself* — never said aloud. He **tried** to say it; he could not; the warehouse went sideways instead.

### Stage 3 — Physical Disposition Toward Cost-Absorption

The pivot point. Stage 3 is when Bruno's body begins to be put between his loved ones and the consequences of their choices, *without* the prior negotiation that healthy Bruno would attempt.

In normative function he argues, then helps, then if necessary takes risk. In Stage 3 he skips the argument. He simply *positions*. He arrives early at a confrontation he wasn't invited to, he stands between, he reaches for the device, he steps in front. The Wakanda decision was preceded by exactly this: he ran toward Becky St. Jude's containment rig without a plan, because the plan had been replaced by the conviction that *being broken was a more honest outcome than being unable to prevent the break*.

Surveillance markers at this stage: increased solo movement at night, presence at locations not on his usual route (warehouses, perimeter sites of Kamala's known operations), suppressed comms (he stops responding to non-essential text threads), and — this is the somatic tell — **he starts eating standing up**. Sitting down to a meal requires a future tense he is no longer fully extending.

### Stage 4 — The Silent Decision

At some point — and this is the most clinically dangerous stage because it is the least externally visible — Bruno makes a decision. The decision is unilateral, fully formed before he speaks it, and articulated only as a fait accompli. Wakanda was announced, not discussed. The Mike relationship's reframings were declared, not negotiated. His withdrawals from Kamala's confidant-primary role were never proposed; they simply occurred and were narrated only retrospectively.

The hallmarks of Stage 4:

- **Sudden return of warmth.** This is the cruel feature. Once the decision is made, the pressure releases internally and he becomes briefly *more present* — softer with Kamala, gentler with Vick, more willing to make a joke. Naive observers read this as recovery. It is the opposite: it is the calm of a man who has already chosen exit and is now spending the remaining time in the room as a gift to the people he is about to leave.
- **Quiet accountancy.** He pays small debts. He returns borrowed books. He finishes the open project on the bench rather than leaving it for the next iteration. He hands off Circle Q logistics to whoever can take them.
- **One conversation per loved one.** Not a goodbye — Bruno does not do goodbyes — but a *settled* conversation, often technical in surface but valedictory in structure. The thing he wants you to remember he tells you flatly and then changes the subject.

This stage typically lasts days to two weeks. After Stage 4, intervention windows close fast.

### Stage 5 — Geographic / Relational Exit

The execution. Bruno removes himself. The removal can be literal (Wakanda) or structural (the demotion of his own role in Kamala's life from confidant-primary to one-of-the-team, accomplished by simply ceasing to show up to the meetings he isn't formally required at). In either case the architecture is the same: he relocates the center of gravity of his life **away** from the source of injury, and he does it without ever framing it as injury.

The exit is **gentle, polite, fully justified by external circumstance**, and *non-negotiable*. He will not be talked out of it. Attempts to talk him out of it trigger a regression to Stage 2 — he goes technical, he goes flat, he agrees with everything and changes nothing.

This is what his collapse looks like. Not a crash. A move.

---

## 6.3 The Conditions That Produce Decompensation

Decompensation in Bruno is not stochastic. It requires a specific stressor profile, and absent that profile he is essentially indestructible at the psychiatric level. The triggers are:

**Primary trigger — *witnessing a self-destructive ethical choice in a loved one that he is structurally unable to prevent.*** This is the master variable. It is what produced the Civil War II break (Kamala on the Ulysses team), what produced the smaller fractures during Vick's Inventor-cell period, and what would produce a future break if Kamala were to make a comparable choice. The unbearable element is not the loved one's danger — Bruno tolerates danger — but the loved one's **agency in choosing wrongly**. He cannot move against their will, he cannot stand by, and the resulting paralysis is the seam in his armor.

**Secondary trigger — *degradation of technical competence.*** The hand injury did not break him alone; it accelerated a break already underway. Any future loss of capacity — cognitive, sensory, motoric — that struck the load-bearing beam of his usefulness would produce the same descent at higher velocity. He is unusually vulnerable to neurological insult precisely because he has no backup self-concept to fall back on.

**Tertiary trigger — *being made the explicit object of asymmetric care he cannot reciprocate or refuse.*** If someone — Kamala, his mother, an institutional handler — were to insist on caring for him in a sustained way, without an exit ramp, he would experience it as a destabilizing pressure rather than a comfort. He would either convert the care into a debt and over-repay it (Stage 1 hyperfunction triggered by gratitude) or, if conversion failed, withdraw to escape it. The most counterintuitive operational fact in this file is that **kindness, badly calibrated, is more dangerous to him than hostility**.

**Quaternary trigger — *forced public visibility of his interior state.*** A confession scene, a media exposure, a friend group intervention, a therapist's room he hasn't chosen — anything that forces the inner content out of suppression and into a witnessed register before he is ready. He will not melt down; he will go *flat*, completely affectless, and the post-event decompensation will be silent and rapid. The Bruno who walks out of an emotional ambush is already in Stage 4.

**Compound triggers — multi-stressor windows.** The Civil War II break was multi-stressor: ethical injury (Ulysses), bodily injury (hand), romantic foreclosure (Kamala-Kamran, Mike collapse), and structural displacement (his role in Kamala's life destabilized by the Inhuman-political context). Bruno can absorb any one of these; two simultaneously degrade function; three or more in a narrow window are full-cycle.

---

## 6.4 What His Collapse Looks Like From the Outside

A summary for handlers and field assets:

- He will not call you. He has never called you in crisis; he is not going to start.
- His texts will get shorter, then one-word, then punctual-only ("k"), then absent. The absence is not silence — it is *output diverted into containment*. He is using all available bandwidth to manage the interior.
- He will look fine. He will look, in fact, slightly better than usual — cleaner, calmer, more present in conversation. Take this as warning, not reassurance.
- He will finish his projects. The half-built thing on the bench is the canary; if he completes and stows the works-in-progress with uncharacteristic tidiness, an exit is imminent.
- He will have one conversation with you that feels slightly weighted and not be able to tell you why.
- And then he will be gone — sometimes literally (a transfer, a flight, a job offer accepted in 48 hours), sometimes structurally (the same body in the same room, but the role vacated and reassigned by a process you did not witness).

The collapse is **non-spectacular and complete**. There will be no rubble to clean up. There will only be an absence where a person used to stand, and the residual feeling among those who loved him that something was wrong for a long time and they did not see it because he did not want them to.

---

## 6.5 The Failure Mode That Has Not Yet Occurred

The longitudinal record shows one full-cycle decompensation (Civil War II → Wakanda) and several aborted micro-cycles. In every documented case, the exit ramp existed: Wakanda was available, the workbench was rebuildable, the new attachment (Kareem) was forming, the relationship with Kamala — though scarred — survived in altered form. **Bruno has never decompensated without somewhere to go.**

The unaddressed risk in this file is what happens when the exit ramps close. The conditions for that scenario:

1. A precipitating ethical-injury event involving a loved one whose choice he cannot prevent.
2. Concurrent degradation of technical competence (a second physical injury, a neurological event, a forced separation from his lab).
3. Foreclosure of geographic/relational alternatives (loss of the Wakandan affiliation, dissolution of the Kareem attachment, Vick in a state that requires his presence and forbids his exit, Kamala in a state that requires his presence and forbids his exit).
4. Forced public visibility of his interior at a moment when suppression has been his only working defense.

Under that compound stressor with no exit available, the failure mode would not be the gentle subtraction documented above. It would be a **sudden, total functional collapse** — sleep loss escalating to insomnia, eating cessation, work cessation, social withdrawal complete, affect flattening into something near-catatonic — and, because Bruno has no prior history of help-seeking and no working vocabulary for asking, the collapse would be **discovered rather than reported**. Someone would find him.

He has never been here. Nothing in canon suggests he is approaching it. But the structural vulnerability is real, and any handler whose long-term planning extends past the immediate operational horizon should regard the maintenance of *exit ramps* — alternative attachments, alternative locations, alternative lab spaces, alternative ways to be useful — as a non-discretionary feature of his welfare profile.

---

## 6.6 Protective Factors Currently in Place

Against the above, the longitudinal record also documents the substrate that has so far kept full collapse out of reach:

- **Genuine vocation.** The science is real, not instrumental. Even stripped of Kamala, the workbench retains meaning. This is the single largest protective factor.
- **Capacity for new attachment.** Kareem is the proof of concept. Bruno can form bonds outside the Kamala-centric architecture; he is not romantically monogamously fixated in a way that would make Kamala's absence catastrophic.
- **Sibling load that is also a tether.** Vick is a stressor and a reason to stay alive. The parentified role that costs him so much is also what holds him in the world.
- **Ethical literacy.** He has a coherent moral grammar he did not borrow from anyone. He can reason himself through situations that would topple a less articulate interior.
- **No substance vulnerability.** The standard self-medicating exit ramps are closed by temperament; he will not drink or use his way into a worse failure mode.
- **Forgiveness as practice.** He does not maintain grievance ledgers. Resentment, the slow poison most parentified children eventually drink, does not appear to be metabolizing in him.

**Net assessment:** A young man whose failure mode is exit rather than explosion, whose collapse looks like a relocation, whose decompensation has — across the longitudinal record — successfully been camouflaged as personal growth. The risk is not that he will break visibly. The risk is that one day he will be gone, and the people who loved him will not have noticed when the leaving began.


## Trajectory & Forward Assessment

# 6. TRAJECTORY & FORWARD ASSESSMENT

**Subject:** CARRELLI, Bruno
**Section purpose:** Project the longitudinal vector forward. Identify open questions, decision-pressure points ("forks"), growth conditions, and catastrophe conditions. The subject is presently in his early twenties, late-adolescent canon having concluded; the load-bearing developmental window for the next decade is *now*.

---

## 6.1 The Vector at Present

The subject enters his early twenties in a stabilized but **structurally unfinished** configuration. Stabilized: scientifically productive (Wakandan-trained, demonstrably capable of working at frontier; reintegrated into Jersey City social field; not symptomatic; not isolated). Unfinished: the central architectural questions of his adolescence — *what is he when he is not the steady one for Kamala? what does he do with a body that has been broken once and a hand that will not fully recover? what does intimacy look like for him when it is not in the service of another's mission?* — have been **deferred rather than answered.**

Deferral is his characteristic move. The trajectory question is whether the deferral can hold another decade, and what breaks it when it cannot.

**Baseline projection (no intervention, no rupture):** Bruno continues as competent professional infrastructure inside the broader hero-adjacent economy. He becomes, by his late twenties, the kind of figure others go to: a quiet engineer with cross-disciplinary fluency, a moral conscience consulted by people who outrank him in raw power. He sustains a relationship — possibly with Kareem, possibly with someone new — that is loving, low-conflict, and faintly under-met on his side because he does not know how to ask for more. He is *fine*. He is also, in a way that no one around him will name, slightly hollowed.

This is the **default trajectory.** It is not catastrophic. It is also not the trajectory of a person who has metabolized his own life. The fork points below are the places where the default either breaks toward growth or breaks toward something worse.

---

## 6.2 Open Questions (the file's unresolved variables)

These are the questions the longitudinal record cannot yet answer and which a competent handler should be tracking actively.

1. **Has the hand been grieved?** No evidence yet that it has. The injury was integrated functionally and never processed affectively. The open question is whether the grief surfaces on its own timetable (somatic intrusion, late-onset depressive episode in his late twenties, an unexpected breakdown over a small mechanical failure) or whether it remains permanently encapsulated. Either outcome carries cost; the first is more dangerous acutely, the second more dangerous chronically.

2. **Is the Kamala-attachment metabolized or merely shelved?** Bruno's romantic foreclosure of Kamala was handled by *geography and time*, not by working it through. The question is what happens when geography ends — when he is back in Jersey City for an extended period and she is single, or married, or grieving, or in crisis. The pattern predicts he will not act on residual feeling. The pattern also predicts he will absorb whatever is asked of him. Both predictions could be wrong in the same moment, in either direction.

3. **What does his ethical fixity do under sustained institutional pressure?** Bruno's deontological streak has been tested in episodes (Ulysses, Inventor) but not in sustained employment by an institution whose interests do not always align with his principles. Wakanda is a benign frame. A defense contractor, a Stark-adjacent firm, a SHIELD-successor, a Krakoa-era mutant-state laboratory, or even a Damage Control engineering arm would test him differently. The open question is whether he is the kind of principled person who *quits* or the kind who *stays and gets quieter*. The pattern history weakly favors the latter, which is the more dangerous reading.

4. **Will he ever ask for something?** Across the canon, Bruno has functionally never made an unmediated bid for his own want. Not for Kamala, not after the injury, not in the Wakanda transfer (framed as offered to him). The forward question is whether a moment arrives in which the only path through is for him to *state a need*, and whether he has the equipment to do it.

5. **What is the second injury?** The hand was the first time his body was treated as expendable infrastructure. The pattern of his life — proximate to powered combatants, willing to place himself between threat and the people he loves — predicts a second injury. The open question is what part of him it takes, and whether he is closer to forty or closer to twenty-five when it happens. The closer to twenty-five, the more reorganizing it can do. The closer to forty, the more it ossifies what is already there.

6. **Does fatherhood enter the picture?** If yes, with whom and under what frame? Bruno was a father to Vick before he was a brother; the question of whether literal parenthood would *heal* the parentification (by giving the role a legitimate object) or *replicate* it (by re-recruiting him into adult-coded labor for which he was never allowed childhood) is genuinely undetermined. Children would expose him to the only category of demand he has historically been unable to suppress: a dependent who cannot wait.

7. **Vick.** The younger brother arc was never closed. Vick is a permanent variable. He will either stabilize (in which case Bruno can release a portion of his vigilance) or he will not (in which case Bruno's life will continue to be load-bearing on a sibling who cannot carry his own weight). The Vick trajectory is the single largest exogenous determinant of Bruno's available bandwidth for self-development.

---

## 6.3 Fork Points (decision pressures the trajectory will encounter)

### Fork A — The Career Fork (24–28)

Two paths visible.

**A1: Independent research / academic-adjacent.** A Wakandan postdoc converts into a junior PI position, or a Jersey City–based independent lab funded by an Avengers-adjacent grant. Lower compensation, higher autonomy, principled work selection. Growth-positive. Bruno's deontological constitution metabolizes this frame without conflict. Risk: isolation, overwork, sublimation pattern intensifies.

**A2: Institutional capture.** Recruitment — by Stark Unlimited, by a SHIELD-successor R&D arm, by Alchemax, by a state-actor lab, by Damage Control. Higher compensation, real engineering challenges, the seductive frame of *useful at scale*. Growth-negative under most scenarios. The institution will, eventually, ask him for something he should refuse. The pattern predicts he refuses *internally* and stays anyway, which is the configuration that produces the Robert Oppenheimer profile in miniature: a brilliant man who built something he did not endorse and could not unbuild.

**Tell to watch for:** which way he leans when the offers arrive. If he asks Kamala's opinion, A1. If he doesn't ask anyone, A2 is more likely than the file would suggest, because A2 will arrive with a salary that solves a Carrelli-family problem (medical bill, Vick's legal fees, a parent's lost income) and he will frame the decision as *responsibility*, not ambition.

### Fork B — The Romantic Fork (ongoing, peak pressure 23–30)

**B1: Sustained partnership with Kareem or a Kareem-analog.** Likeliest stable outcome. Real affection, geographic complication, mutual respect, lopsidedness slowly negotiated. Growth-positive if the partner names the lopsidedness; stagnant if the partner is also conflict-avoidant.

**B2: A late, unguarded Kamala moment.** Low base-rate, non-zero. Would arrive in a context of crisis (her injury, his injury, a shared loss). Growth outcome depends entirely on whether either of them has done the work that lets them encounter each other as adults rather than as the people they were at sixteen. If yes, possibly the most generative relationship of his life. If no, the second hand-injury equivalent — a wound that doesn't bleed but doesn't close.

**B3: A new partner who specifically requires him to ask.** The growth-positive wild card. A partner — could be anyone, no canonical prediction — whose love language is *being asked of*, and who refuses to accept the standard Bruno offering of pre-empted competence. This is the partner who would, over five to seven years, *actually change him*. Base-rate low; transformative if it happens.

**B4: Solitude by drift.** He never quite ends one relationship, never quite begins another, becomes by thirty-five the man whose friends say "we should set him up with someone" and never do because they can't think of anyone. Sub-clinical, common, and the most likely failure mode if Kareem-arc concludes without replacement.

### Fork C — The Hand Fork (timing uncertain, probably 25–35)

The hand is a count-down clock. Either it gets *worked through* — likely via a triggering event (a moment of public failure in a lab, a younger student watching him struggle, a conversation initiated by a partner who refuses to let him pretend) — or it gets *added to*. Adaptive technology (Stark prosthetics, Wakandan neural-interface gauntlet, a Reed Richards favor) is plausible in this universe and would itself constitute a fork: does he accept augmentation, and if so, what does it cost him to be the person whose competence is again unimpeded? There is a real risk that *restoration* of the hand would destabilize him more than the original injury did, by removing the somatic alibi that has allowed him to organize his post-2016 life around constrained ambition.

### Fork D — The Vick Fork (continuous)

Vick is either rescued one final time and stabilizes, or Vick is not, and at some point Bruno is forced to **decline a rescue**. This is the single hardest act Bruno has ever been asked to perform — saying *no* to family, to a sibling, to the role that constituted him. If he manages it, it is the deepest growth episode available in his life. If he doesn't, Vick becomes a permanent tax on his bandwidth, his finances, and his capacity for partnership.

### Fork E — The Second Injury Fork

A bodily event — another field-adjacent injury, an illness, a near-death — forces a question the hand never did, because the hand happened to an adolescent who had no other identity to fall back on and so absorbed it through the only frame available (silence). A second injury at twenty-eight or thirty-two arrives in a life with more resources: an established partner, a vocation he chose, friends who are now adults. The same event that destroyed the adolescent could rebuild the adult. Conversely, a second injury that mirrors the first (acquired in service of someone else's mission, again silently absorbed) ossifies the pattern permanently and produces the *Bruno at forty-five* who is genuinely concerning: the man whose body is a ledger of other people's wars and who has still never said it hurt.

### Fork F — The Faith Fork (low-probability, high-impact)

Residual Catholic substrate is, per §5, grammar without metaphysics. Late-twenties return-to-faith is a non-trivial base-rate in his demographic and personality type (high conscientiousness + ethical seriousness + the *what is this all for* question that arrives on schedule around twenty-eight). If it happens, it would supply the one thing his system currently lacks: a frame in which *being seen and known by something that does not require him to produce* is the foundational experience. Growth-positive if engaged seriously, hollow if engaged ritually.

---

## 6.4 Growth Conditions

The conditions under which Bruno's trajectory bends *toward* integration rather than refinement-of-default:

1. **A relationship — romantic, therapeutic, or deeply platonic — with a person who can name the pattern aloud and refuse to let him perform around it.** Therapy is the cleanest version; a partner who has done their own work is the most powerful version; a mentor (a senior Wakandan scientist, an older engineer in a Stark-orbit lab) is the most likely version. The non-negotiable feature is *someone who is not fooled by the competent surface.*

2. **A failure he cannot fix.** The hand was a failure he absorbed; what he needs is a failure he must *sit with*, publicly, without converting it into renewed service. A lab disaster, a student's death he could not prevent, a project that fails because his judgment was wrong (not because he was overruled). His system has never had to metabolize *being the cause* of a bad outcome. The first time it does, with adequate support, is potentially the most generative event in his adulthood.

3. **Saying no to a Carrelli family bid.** Per Fork D. This is the single discrete behavior whose presence in the record would shift the entire prognosis.

4. **Receiving care without converting it.** A discrete episode — illness, injury, grief — in which someone takes care of him and he allows it without immediately scheduling reciprocation. Base-rate currently near zero. Frequency in the next decade is the leading indicator of structural change.

5. **A sustained period — six months, a year — of work that is selected for his own interest rather than someone else's need.** A sabbatical, an independent research project, an art he picks up for no reason. The system has never been allowed to discover what it wants in the absence of a demand. This is the experiment that has not been run.

---

## 6.5 Catastrophe Conditions

The conditions under which the trajectory bends toward genuine harm. None are likely in isolation; clustering is the risk profile.

1. **Institutional capture (A2) + a Kamala-rupture (B failure) + a Vick relapse (D failure).** The three-vector collapse. He stays in a job he should leave because the salary is solving a Vick problem, while the romantic configuration he relied on for ballast dissolves. The pattern history predicts: he does not break, he does not act out, he does not seek help. He becomes the man who works late, drinks moderately for the first time in his life, loses weight, ages visibly, and presents to a primary-care physician at thirty-four with stress cardiomyopathy and no idea how he got there. **This is the most plausible catastrophe and it is invisible from the outside until the somatic event.**

2. **A second injury absorbed in the same posture as the first.** Permanently encodes "my body is for them" as the operating assumption. Closes the window on integration.

3. **A morally compromising act committed in service of someone he loves.** Bruno's ethical clarity has never been tested by a situation in which the right thing to do would hurt a person he is responsible for. The Vick arcs flirted with this and resolved benignly. A future scenario in which he must either turn in, abandon, expose, or refuse a loved one — and *can't* — would crack the deontological frame, and Bruno without his ethical spine is not a stable system. He would not become a villain. He would become a *quiet accomplice*, and the self-concept damage would be unrecoverable without therapeutic intervention he would not seek.

4. **The recruitment by a hostile actor who *sees the pattern.*** The single largest counterintelligence concern in this file. Bruno is uniquely vulnerable to a recruiter who arrives in the frame of *needing him*. Not flattery — *need*. A bad actor (a corporate intelligence arm, a foreign technical service, an AIM-successor cell wearing legitimate cover, a mutant separatist faction with a humanitarian veneer) who positions a project as *only you can do this, and someone vulnerable will be hurt if you don't* would bypass every defense he has. He has never been trained to recognize that his sense of obligation is itself an attack surface. This is the threat vector that should be actively monitored.

5. **Kamala's death or permanent disappearance.** Low base-rate in this universe; high impact if it happens. Bruno's adolescent self-concept was organized around a person he can no longer protect or be useful to. Without the integration work in 6.4, this event lands on top of an ungrieved hand and a deferred romantic foreclosure, and the resulting depressive episode would be his first true psychiatric event. Recoverable, but only with intervention.

---

## 6.6 The Twenty-Year Read

If the file is reopened in 2045, three Brunos are visible at the end of the projection cone.

**The likely Bruno (50–60% probability).** Mid-thirties, senior engineer or junior PI at a respectable institution, partnered, possibly a parent of one child, still in Kamala's life as a trusted friend with the old intensity professionalized into something durable. Quiet, competent, slightly under-met. A good man whose interior life remains substantially private even to those closest to him. The hand still hurts in cold weather and he has never said so.

**The grown Bruno (20–25% probability).** The same external life, with an interior reorganization. Has done the work — therapy, a sustained partnership that demanded it, a failure he couldn't fix and didn't flee. Speaks of the hand without irony. Has said no to at least one Carrelli family bid and survived it. Has, at some point, asked for something and accepted it. Capable of being a mentor to younger people in a way that does not replicate parentification, because he can model receiving as well as giving. This is the high-functioning, fully-integrated adult version, and it is genuinely achievable. The growth conditions are not exotic.

**The hollowed Bruno (15–20% probability).** Some combination of catastrophe conditions has fired. Either institutionally captured and morally diminished, or somatically failed (the stress-cardiomyopathy scenario, an autoimmune flare, an addiction that arrived late and quietly), or relationally drifted into a solitude he cannot articulate. Not a villain, not a tragedy in the operatic sense — a man whose life ran on the default trajectory for too long without the perturbation that would have rerouted it. The file's most important warning is that *this Bruno is produced not by any single bad event but by the absence of any sufficient good one.*

---

## 6.7 Handler Notes

For any benevolent party with sustained access:

- The single most useful intervention is **a friend who asks him what he wants and refuses the first three answers.** The first three will be other people's needs ranked in order of urgency. The fourth answer is the data.
- Do not offer help in the frame of *rescue*. He will refuse it and the refusal will calcify the pattern. Offer it in the frame of *collaboration on something he is curious about.* He cannot decline curiosity-shaped invitations as easily as he declines care-shaped ones.
- Track the somatic register. He will not narrate distress; his body will. Sleep, weight, the hand's reported pain frequency, the introduction of any substance use however moderate — these are the leading indicators, in that order.
- The Kamala variable will remain the dominant exogenous factor in his emotional weather for at least the next decade. This is not pathology; it is the structure of having been formed alongside someone whose life is bigger than the room they share. Monitor without intervening unless a clear catastrophe condition aligns.
- If the recruitment-by-need vector (6.5.4) materializes, intervene directly and early. He will not detect it. No one in his life is currently equipped to flag it for him.

The summary read of this section is the summary read of the file. **Bruno Carrelli's future is not determined by what happens to him. It is determined by whether anyone — possibly himself — ever insists that what happens to him is allowed to matter.**

## Relationship Graph
### [[Kamala Khan (Ms. Marvel)]]
- Primary attachment, oldest friend, unspoken love, principal he serves
- Trust: bedrock. Restored after Civil War II rupture but structurally repaired, not fully restored
- Failure mode: if Kamala were to take him for granted publicly and at length, or to repeatedly override his accurate warnings, the dysthymic flatness could become permanent withdrawal — not betrayal, but a quiet, irreversible decentering. He would still help her. He would no longer organize his life around her.
- Leverage: anyone wanting to predict, pressure, or reach Bruno does it through her — she is the load-bearing relationship, and a credible threat to her bypasses every other defense he has

### Vick Carrelli
- Older brother, family loyalty as non-negotiable obligation
- Trust: low operationally, absolute familially
- Failure mode: Vick is a recurring vector by which Bruno is dragged into crises he has correctly diagnosed as Vick's fault and cannot refuse
- Leverage: an adversary who threatens Vick gets Bruno's compliance faster than one who threatens Bruno

### Mike Miller
- Former girlfriend; the relationship was genuine, not a rebound
- Trust: high; she saw him clearly — which is precisely what ended it
- Failure mode: already realized — she named the triangulation with Kamala and exited
- Leverage: she is the witness to his unspoken want; anyone who got her to articulate what she saw would have a map of Bruno's interior

### Kaylee
- Post-Wakanda girlfriend, eventually exited
- Trust: moderate; the relationship was part of the convalescent narrowed self
- Failure mode: same structural problem as Mike, less time on-camera

### Yusuf Khan Muneeba Khan Aamir Khan
- The Khan family — trusted adult/sibling figures in his life by long proximity
- Trust: mutual and culturally fluent; he has earned standing in their household
- Failure mode: if he were ever positioned (by Vick, by circumstance, by an enemy) as a threat to Kamala in their eyes, the loss would be catastrophic to him and largely silent
- Leverage: their approval is a real anchor; framing him as having harmed or failed Kamala would devastate

### The Inventor
- First supervillain encounter; the crisis that nearly killed Vick and pulled Bruno into the powered world
- Trust: zero
- Failure mode (historical): the template for every later catastrophe — family entanglement plus impulsive escalation plus Bruno absorbing the cost

### Becky St Jude Discord
- Adjacent to the Civil War II hinge event; the lab/explosion environment in which his hand was destroyed
- Trust: none; trauma-associated
- Failure mode: a stimulus class — anyone who replicates the predictive-justice / lab-explosion configuration will trigger his deepest avoidance
